在此插件中，推荐的实现方式是什么？ 官方内置一些订阅源，用户勾选，还是用户主动添加url？（但失效风险很大）

## URL-based Background Sources: Complete Code Map

### 1. Dialog Component: `UrlDialog.svelte`
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/ui/dialogs/UrlDialog.svelte` (141 lines)

**How it works:**

| Step | Lines | Description |
|------|-------|-------------|
| **Input+debounce** | 68-78 | `handleInput()` uses 500ms debounce before calling `doCheck()` |
| **Extension validation** | 25-29 | `checkExt()` strips query string, extracts extension, validates against `IMAGE_EXTS.union(VIDEO_EXTS)` from `constants.ts` |
| **Content-type verification** | 43-64 | `doCheck()` does a real `fetch(url)` → checks `content-type` header: if `image/` → creates a `Blob` + `createObjectURL` for preview; if `video/` → marks valid but shows "no preview" placeholder |
| **Download+store** | 80-92 | `handleUpload()` calls `downloadUrl(trimmed, destPath)` from `api.ts`, which fetches the URL, gets a Blob, and uploads it via `putFile()` to `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/<filename>` |
| **Rendering URL construction** | 88-89 | After upload, calls `getFileUrl(destPath, 'upload')` from `utils/fs.ts` to build the canvas rendering URL (e.g., `public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/img.jpg`) |
| **Callback** | 89 | Calls `onSuccess(renderingUrl)` passing the upload-type rendering URL |
| **Alt: Enter key** | 109 | `Enter` key triggers `handleUpload()` directly when `validExt` is true |

**Key dependencies:**
- `downloadUrl()` from `../../utils/api.ts` (line 3)
- `getFileUrl()` from `../../utils/fs.ts` (line 4)
- `IMAGE_EXTS`, `VIDEO_EXTS` from `../../constants` (line 5)

---

### 2. Dialog Factory: `dialogs/index.ts`
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/ui/dialogs/index.ts`

| Lines | Function | Description |
|-------|----------|-------------|
| 43-57 | `showUrlDialog(onSuccess)` | Wraps `UrlDialog.svelte` in `svelteDialog()`. Passes `onSuccess` prop; when dialog's `handleUpload()` succeeds, it calls `onSuccess(uploadUrl)` then closes the dialog. |

Imported by:
- `topbarMenu.ts` (line 8)
- `SourcesTab.svelte` (line 15)

---

### 3. Config Store: URL Storage
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/stores/config.ts`

**Config schema** (from `src/types.ts`, lines 11-25):

```typescript
export interface AppConfig {
    // ... other fields ...
    currentFile: string | null    // ← stores the rendering URL of the currently active background
    // ...
}
```

**How URLs are stored:**
- There is **NO dedicated "urls" config key**. All URL-sourced backgrounds become `upload`-type files.
- When a URL is downloaded, it's saved to `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/<filename>`
- The `currentFile` config key stores the **canvas rendering URL** (e.g., `public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/img.jpg`)
- The file exists alongside other upload-type files in the `pluginAssetsDir` (`/data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/`)

**No separate "urlSources" list exists** -- URL sources are merged into the `upload` source type group.

---

### 4. URL Download: `api.ts`
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/utils/api.ts`

| Lines | Function | Description |
|-------|----------|-------------|
| 58-68 | `downloadUrl(url, destPath)` | 1. `fetch(url)` the remote resource; 2. `response.blob()` to get binary; 3. `putFile(destPath, blob)` uploads to siyuan's file system. Returns `boolean`. |

**The full download pipeline:**
```
UrlDialog.svelte:handleUpload()
  → api.downloadUrl(url, "data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/<filename>")
    → fetch(url) → response.blob()
    → api.putFile(destPath, blob)
      → FormData { path, isDir, modTime, file }
      → fetchSyncPost("/api/file/putFile", formData)
  → fs.getFileUrl(destPath, 'upload')  # builds rendering URL
  → onSuccess(renderingUrl)            # callback to topbarMenu or SourcesTab
```

---

### 5. URL-to-Rendering-URL Conversion: `fs.ts`
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/utils/fs.ts`

| Lines | Function | Description |
|-------|----------|-------------|
| 30-40 | `getFileUrl(apiPath, sourceType)` | For `'upload'` type (and `'assets'`): strips `/data/` prefix, resulting in relative webview paths like `public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/img.jpg`. For `'local'` type: prepends `file://`. |

**Path transformation for upload:**
```
Input:  /data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/img.jpg
Output: public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/img.jpg
```
This relative path is what gets stored in `currentFile` and used in `canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url('public/...')`.

---

### 6. Source Scanning: `sourceManager.ts`
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/services/sourceManager.ts`

| Lines | Function | URL-related behavior |
|-------|----------|---------------------|
| 10-43 | `scanAll(assetDirs, localFolders)` | Always scans `upload` group (line 15: `scanSource('upload', pluginAssetsDir)`). URL-downloaded files are discovered here alongside other upload-type files. |
| 45-83 | `scanSource(type, path)` | For `upload`/`assets`: calls `readSiyuanDir(path)` (siyuan API); For `local`: calls `readLocalDir(path)`. Each file gets its `url` via `getFileUrl(apiPath, type)` at line 66. |
| 85-97 | `pickRandom(items, excludeUrl?)` | Used for random selection; can exclude current URL. |

---

### 7. Background Rendering: `bgRender.ts`
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/services/bgRender.ts`

| Lines | Function | URL-related behavior |
|-------|----------|---------------------|
| 13-19 | `detectType(url)` | Determines image vs video from file extension in the URL |
| 66-70 | `render(url)` | Dispatches to `renderImage` or `renderVideo` |
| 72-84 | `renderImage(url)` | Sets `canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url('${url}')` -- the URL is used directly in CSS |
| 86-102 | `renderVideo(url)` | Sets `videoEl.src = url` |

---

- **Lines 97-106**: Topbar menu → "添加网络资源" → calls `showUrlDialog()` → on success: saves `uploadUrl` to `currentFile`, calls `renderImage`/`renderVideo`.

**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/ui/settings/SourcesTab.svelte`
- **Lines 277-292**: Settings panel → upload group's link button → calls `showUrlDialog()` → on success: saves to `currentFile`, renders, then `refreshAll()`.
- **Lines 354-359**: The "link" icon button in the upload group header.

### 9. Type Definitions
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/types.ts`

| Lines | Type | Fields relevant to URLs |
|-------|------|------------------------|
| 11-25 | `AppConfig` | `currentFile: string \| null` -- stores the rendering URL |
| 27-34 | `ImageItem` | `url: string` (rendering URL), `apiPath: string` (filesystem path), `sourceType: 'local' \| 'upload' \| 'assets'` |

**URL sources always have `sourceType: 'upload'`**, because they are downloaded into the plugin's public directory.

---

### Summary: Current URL Source Lifecycle

```
User enters URL in UrlDialog.svelte
  │
  ├─ Debounced validation (500ms): check file extension + HTTP content-type
  │
  ├─ User clicks "确认"
  │
  ├─ api.downloadUrl(url, destPath)
  │   ├─ fetch(url) → blob
  │   └─ api.putFile(destPath, blob) → saves to data/public/<plugin>/<filename>
  │
  ├─ fs.getFileUrl(destPath, 'upload')
  │   └─ Strips /data/ prefix → "public/<plugin>/<filename>"
  │
  ├─ onSuccess(renderingUrl) callback
  │   ├─ configStore.set("currentFile", renderingUrl)
  │   ├─ configStore.save()
  │   └─ bgRender.render(renderingUrl)
  │       └─ canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url('public/<plugin>/<filename>')
  │
  └─ File appears in upload group alongside other upload-type files
```

**Key design decision:** URL sources are **not a separate source type**. They are downloaded once and become permanent `upload`-type files, indistinguishable from files uploaded via the "上传多个文件" or "上传整个目录" options. There is no config key that tracks "URL origin" -- only the rendering URL in `currentFile` and the file in the plugin's public directory.

Nyanyaa~♡
</task_result>
```

## 1. `src/stores/config.ts` (159 行)

**配置存储单例类**，负责读取/写入 SiYuan 本地存储中的插件配置。

**默认配置 (`APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS`)：**

| 字段 | 类型 | 默认值 | 说明 |
|------|------|--------|------|
| `activate` | `boolean` | `true` | 是否激活背景 |
| `opacity` | `number` | `0.5` | 透明度 (用户设置域 `[0.1, 1]`，加权后域 `[0.74, 0.99]`) |
| `blur` | `number` | `5` | 模糊度 |
| `positionX` | `number` | `50` | 背景水平位置 (%) |
| `positionY` | `number` | `50` | 背景垂直位置 (%) |
| `localFolders` | `string[]` | `[]` | 本地文件夹绝对路径列表 (desktop only) |
| `assetDirs` | `string[]` | `[]` | 资源目录路径列表 (assets 类型) |
| `changeBgOnStart` | `boolean` | `true` | 启动时自动切换背景 |
| `autoRefreshTime` | `number` | `30` | 自动刷新间隔 (分钟) |
| `disabledThemes` | `DisabledThemes` | `{ dark: [], light: [] }` | 屏蔽的主题 |
| `imageOverrides` | `Record<string, ImageOverride>` | `{}` | 图片级别的覆盖配置 (位置等) |
| `currentFile` | `string \| null` | `null` | 当前背景文件路径 |
| `inDev` | `boolean` | `false` | 开发模式开关 |

**核心方法：**
- `load()` — 从 `window.siyuan.storage` 或 `/api/storage/getLocalStorage` 加载
- `save()` — 脏标记防抖写入 `/api/storage/setLocalStorageVal`
- `get/set/setAndSave` — 类型安全的属性访问
- `snapshot()` — 返回只读快照
- `isLocalPath(path)` — 判断路径是否属于 `localFolders` 列表
- `reset()` — 重置为默认值，清理 petal 旧数据和 public 上传文件
- `cleanOldConfigIfNeeded()` — 自动检测旧版配置并迁移

## 2. `src/types.ts` (42 行)

**所有类型定义：**

```typescript
// 主题屏蔽（按暗色/亮色分组）
export interface DisabledThemes {
    dark: string[]
    light: string[]
}

// 单张图片级别的覆盖配置
export interface ImageOverride {
    positionX?: number
    positionY?: number
}

// 根配置对象（与 config.ts 默认值一一对应）
export interface AppConfig {
    activate: boolean
    opacity: number
    blur: number
    positionX: number
    positionY: number
    localFolders: string[]
    assetDirs: string[]
    changeBgOnStart: boolean
    autoRefreshTime: number
    disabledThemes: DisabledThemes
    imageOverrides: Record<string, ImageOverride>
    currentFile: string | null
    inDev: boolean
}

// 背景图片/视频项（渲染引擎使用）
export interface ImageItem {
    name: string          // 文件名 (显示用)
    url: string           // 用于 CSS background-image / video src 的 URL
    apiPath: string       // 思源 API 路径 (用于上传/删除操作)
    type: 'image' | 'video'
    sourceType: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets'
    sourceLabel: string   // 来源标签 (如目录名或 URL 描述)
}

// 源配置（表示一组文件来源）
export interface SourceConfig {
    type: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets'
    path: string
    label: string
}
```

底部从 `constants` 重导出：`IMAGE_EXTS`、`VIDEO_EXTS`、`classifyFileType`。

## 数据结构关系总结

```
AppConfig (持久化到思源 localStorage)
  ├── 全局设置: activate, opacity, blur, positionX, positionY
  ├── 自动行为: changeBgOnStart, autoRefreshTime
  ├── 源列表:   localFolders (string[]), assetDirs (string[])
  ├── 运行时:   currentFile (string|null)
  ├── 高级:     disabledThemes, imageOverrides, inDev
  │
  └── [扫描时生成] ──→ ImageItem[] (不在 AppConfig 中，由 sourceManager 运行时构建)
                        ├── name, url, apiPath
                        ├── type: 'image' | 'video'
                        ├── sourceType: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets'
                        └── sourceLabel

三种源类型 (SourceConfig):
  local   → desktop only, fsp.readdir, url("file:///absolute/path/img.jpg")
  upload  → 全平台, readSiyuanDir, url("public/{packageName}/img.jpg")
  assets  → 全平台, readSiyuanDir, url("assets/.../img.jpg")
```

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

Now I have a good understanding of the current architecture. Let me analyze the user's question about implementing "random image API" support:

**Current behavior:**
- URL sources are downloaded ONCE and become permanent `upload`-type files
- No distinction between URL-downloaded files and manually uploaded files
- The Dark+ theme uses a different approach: it has a `web` config with `light[]` and `dark[]` URL lists, and a `random` flag. When random is on, it can dynamically pick from those URLs each time.

**The user's requirement:**
- Support URLs like `https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images` that return different images each time they're called
- These are essentially "random image API endpoints"

**Key design question:**
- Option A: Built-in subscription feeds (preset URLs, user checks boxes to enable)
- Option B: User adds their own URLs (high failure risk)

Let me think about the pros and cons:

**Option A (Built-in presets):**
- Pro: We can curate working URLs, reducing failure rate
- Pro: Easier UX, just check/uncheck
- Con: Feeds may go down, we need to maintain the list
- Con: Less flexible for users who want custom APIs

**Option B (User-added URLs):**
- Pro: Maximum flexibility
- Con: High failure risk as user noted
- Con: Need more complex UI for URL management

**My recommendation: A hybrid approach**
- Built-in presets (curated) + user can add custom URLs
- The random API URLs should NOT be downloaded permanently like the current "添加网络资源" does
- Instead, they should be treated as "dynamic sources" similar to Dark+ theme's approach

**Technical implementation:**

Current flow for "添加网络资源":
1. User enters URL → download → save as upload file → use that file
2. The file persists, so the same image is used every time

For random image APIs, the flow should be different:
1. Configure URL endpoints (preset or custom)
2. When picking a random background, fetch from the endpoint
3. Download the result, save temporarily, render it
4. The next time, fetch again (getting potentially different image)

But wait - there's a caching issue. The Dark+ theme mentions: "网络图片切换时可能需要禁用缓存". Random image APIs often return different images at the same URL, but browsers may cache the response and show the same image.

So the implementation needs to:
1. Add cache-busting (e.g., append `?t=timestamp` or set `Cache-Control: no-cache` headers)
2. Or download via `fetch()` in the plugin code and use `createObjectURL` (but the rules say NOT to use createObjectURL for thumbnails - but this is for the actual background, not thumbnails)

Wait, the rules say:
> 和最终背景插件渲染的URL保持一致，禁止使用 `createObjectURL` 生成临时 URL，避免内存泄漏。

So we should download the image, save it to the plugin's public dir (as upload type), and render from there. But this conflicts with the "random each time" requirement... unless we overwrite the same file each time.

Actually, looking at this more carefully:
- For a random image API endpoint, we could:
  1. Have a special config key for "dynamic URL endpoints" 
  2. When selecting random background, if one of these endpoints is selected, fetch from it with cache-busting
  3. Download the result to a fixed path like `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/_random_api_bg.jpg`
  4. Render from that path
  5. The file gets overwritten each time a new random image is fetched

This way:
- No `createObjectURL` memory leak
- Always uses the standard rendering pipeline
- `currentFile` stores the fixed path `public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/_random_api_bg.jpg`
- Cache-busting done via `fetch(url + '?t=' + Date.now())` or similar

Actually, let me reconsider. There's another approach used by some similar plugins:

**Approach 2: Direct URL rendering with cache bust**
Instead of downloading, we could modify bgRender to support dynamic URLs with cache-busting. The canvas would directly reference the URL with a timestamp parameter. But this has issues:
- Mixed content warnings if the API is HTTP
- CORS issues
- The image API might require specific headers
- Browser caching at the canvas level

The download approach is more reliable.

**Config schema addition:**

```typescript
// In AppConfig:
dynamicBgUrls: string[]  // list of random image API endpoints
enableDynamicBg: boolean  // whether to use dynamic URLs in random selection
```

Wait, but the user asked specifically about two options: built-in presets vs user-added URLs. Let me think about which is better...

Actually, looking at the Dark+ theme approach more carefully:
- It has hardcoded lists of URLs for light and dark themes
- `random: true` means it randomly picks from those URLs
- It's essentially Option A (built-in presets) but hardcoded in the theme

For this plugin, since it already has a settings panel, I think the best approach is:

**Hybrid: Built-in presets with user customization**

1. Define a curated list of known-good random image API endpoints as presets
2. Users can check/uncheck which presets to use
3. Users can also add their own custom URLs
4. When selecting a random background, if dynamic URLs are involved, fetch+download to a temp path

Actually, let me simplify this. The user asked for my recommendation. Let me provide a clear analysis.

The key insight from the implementation perspective:
- The current "添加网络资源" downloads a single image once → becomes upload type
- A "random image API" needs to repeatedly fetch from a URL that returns different images
- This is fundamentally a different concept

My recommendation:
1. **Built-in presets + user can add custom URLs** - hybrid approach
2. The presets provide curated, tested URLs with low failure risk
3. Users can still add their own if they want
4. Implementation: Add a new config section for "dynamic background URLs" with:
   - A preset list (with enable/disable checkboxes)
   - A text input for custom URLs
   - When a dynamic URL is used, fetch with cache-busting, download to a fixed temp path, render from there

Let me present this analysis to the user clearly.

Let me also quickly check the i18n files to understand the current text structure.

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

Now I have a complete picture. Let me summarize what I found and formulate my recommendation.

Key finding from the Dark+ theme reference:
- It uses a `web.light[]` and `web.dark[]` URL list approach
- These URLs are configured by the user in a JS config file
- The URLs are "random image API endpoints" - each call returns a different image
- The `random` flag controls whether to pick randomly from the list

Key finding from the current plugin:
- URL sources are downloaded ONCE and become permanent upload-type files
- There's no concept of a "dynamic URL" that returns different content each time
- `currentFile` stores a single rendering URL

The user's question: Should it be built-in presets or user-added URLs?

My analysis:

**The Dark+ theme approach** is essentially user-configured URLs (Option B), but it's a developer-oriented config file approach. For a plugin with a UI, we need something more user-friendly.

**My recommendation: Hybrid approach with built-in presets as primary, user-custom as secondary**

Reasons:
1. Most "random image API" URLs tend to go dead over time - having curated presets means we can update them in plugin releases
2. Users who know what they're doing can add custom URLs
3. This matches the plugin's existing philosophy of being easy to use

**Implementation plan:**

1. **Add a new callback data source type: `dynamicUrl`** (or extend existing)
2. **Config addition:**
   ```typescript
   // In AppConfig:
   dynamicBgUrls: string[]  // user-enabled random image API endpoints
   ```
3. **Logic:**
   - When selecting random background, dynamic URLs are also considered alongside local/upload/assets
   - When a dynamic URL is picked, `fetch(url + cacheBust)` → download to a fixed temp file → render from that file
   - The temp file uses a fixed path like `_dynamic_bg.jpg` in the plugin's public dir, overwritten each time
4. **UI:**
   - Add a new section in SourcesTab or a new source group
   - Show built-in presets with checkboxes
   - Allow adding custom URLs
   - The preset list is maintained in code with display names

But actually, thinking about this more carefully - the user specifically asked about "官方内置一些订阅源，用户勾选" vs "用户主动添加url". Let me provide a clear answer with pros/cons.

Let me also think about whether random image APIs should be a separate source type or integrated into the existing upload type.

The key difference:
- Current "添加网络资源": One-time download, permanent file
- Random image API: Repeated fetching, temporary file

These are fundamentally different concepts, so a separate treatment is warranted.

现在我对整个架构有了完整了解。以下是我的分析和推荐：

---

## 分析：当前插件 vs Dark+ 主题 vs 你的需求

### 当前"添加网络资源"的工作方式

```
用户输入 URL → fetch下载 → 保存为 upload 类型文件 → 永久存储
```

URL 来源的图片下载**一次**后成为普通 upload 文件，和手动上传的图片没有区别。不支持「每次调用返回不同图片」的 API。

### Dark+ 主题的工作方式

在主题的 JS 配置文件中硬编码 URL 列表（如 `source.unsplash.com/random`），`random: true` 时随机选取一个 URL，每次都去请求新图片。

### 你的需求

`https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images` 这种 API 每次返回不同图片，需要**每次都重新请求**（还需处理浏览器缓存问题）。

---

## 推荐方案：内置预设 + 用户自定义（混合）

| 方案 | 优点 | 缺点 |
|------|------|------|
| **纯预设（勾选）** | 维护精心筛选的可用源，用户零配置 | 缺乏灵活性，预设失效需等插件更新 |
| **纯自定义URL** | 完全灵活 | 普通用户不知道去哪找API；失效率高，体验差 |
| **混合（推荐）** | 兼顾易用性和灵活性 | 开发量略多 |

**推荐混合方案**的原因：
1. 这类随机图片 API 经常失效——预设列表可以在插件更新时维护
2. 懂行的用户可以添加自己的 API
3. 与插件现有的 "简单易用" 理念一致

---

## 技术实现概要

### 1. 新增配置项

```typescript
// AppConfig 新增
dynamicBgUrls: string[]   // 用户启用的动态背景URL列表（含预设和自定义）
```

### 2. 渲染策略

与普通 URL（下载一次存为 upload）不同，动态 URL 需要：

```
选中动态URL → fetch(url + 缓存破坏参数) → 下载到固定临时路径 
→ 渲染 → 下次选中时重新下载覆盖
```

- 固定路径如 `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/_dynamic_bg.jpg`
- 每次都覆盖同一文件，避免文件堆积
- 需要添加缓存破坏（`?t=timestamp` 或 `Cache-Control: no-cache`），否则浏览器可能返回缓存

### 3. UI 设计

在 `SourcesTab` 中新增一个 **"动态订阅源"** 组，包含：
- 内置预设列表（带勾选框 + 显示名称）
- "添加自定义URL" 按钮 → 弹出输入框
- 预设示例：
  - `https://api.dujin.org/bing/1920.php` — 必应每日壁纸
  - `https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images` — 随机风景
  - `https://source.unsplash.com/random/1920x1080` — Unsplash 随机

### 4. 随机选择逻辑

修改 `sourceManager.pickRandom()` 或 `bgRender` 的随机逻辑，当需要随机切换时：
- 先决定是从普通源（local/upload/assets）还是动态URL中选取
- 若选中动态URL，执行 fetch → 下载 → 渲染流程

---

## 实施计划：动态订阅源功能

### 整体架构

```
用户勾选/添加动态URL → 存入 config.dynamicBgUrls
                         ↓
sourceManager.scanAll() → 把启用URL生成 ImageItem（sourceType: 'dynamic'）
                         ↓
pickRandom() 随机选中 → bgRender.render()
                         ↓
如果是 dynamic 类型 → fetch(url+缓存破坏) → putFile(临时路径) → css url()
```

### 修改清单

| 文件 | 改动 |
|------|------|
| `src/constants.ts` | 新增 `DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS` 预设列表 |
| `src/types.ts` | `sourceType` 新增 `'dynamic'`；新增相关类型 |
| `src/stores/config.ts` | `AppConfig` 新增 `dynamicBgUrls: string[]` |
| `src/utils/api.ts` | 新增 `fetchAndSaveDynamicBg(url, destPath)` 下载+缓存破坏 |
| `src/utils/fs.ts` | `getFileUrl()` 支持 dynamic 类型的路径转换 |
| `src/services/sourceManager.ts` | `scanSource('dynamic')` 生成 ImageItem；`pickRandom` 统一池 |
| `src/services/bgRender.ts` | `render()` 对 dynamic 类型调用 fetch→download→渲染 |
| `src/ui/dialogs/index.ts` | 新增 `showDynamicUrlDialog()` |
| `src/ui/dialogs/UrlDialog.svelte` | 添加"作为动态源"模式（或新建组件） |
| `src/ui/settings/SourcesTab.svelte` | 新增"动态订阅源"区域 |
| `public/i18n/zh_CN.json` | 新增相关文本键 |
| `public/i18n/en_US.json` | 新增相关文本键 |

### 详细设计

#### 1. 预设列表 (`constants.ts`)

```typescript
export const DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS: { id: string; name: string; url: string }[] = [
    { id: 'bing_1920',    name: '必应每日壁纸',    url: 'https://api.dujin.org/bing/1920.php' },
    { id: 'imgapi_风景',   name: '随机风景',       url: 'https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images' },
    { id: 'unsplash_rand', name: 'Unsplash 随机',   url: 'https://source.unsplash.com/random/1920x1080' },
]
```

#### 2. 配置存储

```typescript
// config.ts defaults
dynamicBgUrls: [] as string[]
```

存储的是 URL 字符串（预设 + 自定义的合集），用户勾选即写入。

#### 3. 渲染流程（关键差异）

普通 source（local/upload/assets）：文件已存在，直接渲染
```typescript
canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url('public/plugin/img.jpg')
```

动态 source：每次需要先下载
```typescript
// 1. 缓存破坏
const fetchUrl = url + (url.includes('?') ? '&' : '?') + '_t=' + Date.now()
// 2. 下载到固定临时路径
const tempPath = '/data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/_dynamic_bg.jpg'
await fetchAndSaveDynamicBg(fetchUrl, tempPath)
// 3. 渲染
canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url('public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/_dynamic_bg.jpg')
```

#### 4. 随机选择池统一

`sourceManager.pickRandom(items, excludeUrl)` 的 items 中混合了四种 sourceType：`local`、`upload`、`assets`、`dynamic`，统一从池中随机选取。

这个计划是否满足你的预期？有什么需要调整的地方吗？

### 🤖 Assistant

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

The user is asking about how to implement reachability checking for dynamic URLs efficiently. Let me think about this carefully.

The context is:
- When users add URLs (both presets and custom), we need to verify they're reachable
- If unreachable, prevent adding (for custom) or disable the checkbox with "(不可访问)" label (for presets)
- They want to discuss performance - how to do this efficiently

Key challenges:
1. Network requests are slow - we need a strategy that doesn't block UI
2. Multiple URLs to check (presets + any custom ones)
3. The check needs to happen at appropriate times (plugin load, user adds URL, user opens settings)

Let me think about approaches:

**Approach 1: Simple HEAD/GET request with timeout**
- For each URL, do `fetch(url, { method: 'HEAD', signal: AbortSignal.timeout(5000) })`
- Fast but might not work for all APIs (some don't support HEAD)
- Timeout prevents hanging

**Approach 2: Lightweight range request**
- `fetch(url, { headers: { Range: 'bytes=0-1024' }, signal: AbortSignal.timeout(5000) })`
- Checks content-type header to confirm it's an image
- Gets a small amount of data, more reliable than HEAD
- Still lightweight

**Approach 3: Debounced/batched checking**
- Don't check all URLs at once - stagger them
- Check when settings panel opens
- Show results as they come in

**Approach 4: Cached results**
- Store last check timestamp and result
- Only re-check after certain interval (e.g., 30 minutes)
- Immediate feedback for recently-checked URLs

**My recommendation: Hybrid strategy**

1. **On plugin load / settings open**: Check all enabled URLs with timeout + concurrency limit (e.g., 3 at a time)
2. **Caching**: Store check results with timestamp in config/memory. Valid for 30 minutes.
3. **Method**: Use GET with `Range: bytes=0-1024` and short timeout (5s). Check content-type header.
4. **UI**: Show loading state, then update each URL's status as results come in
5. **Blocking**: For user adding a new custom URL - do a single immediate check (can afford a few seconds wait)
6. **Presets**: Check in background, cache results, only re-check periodically

Let me think about the specific timing:

For presets (built-in):
- Check on plugin startup (non-blocking, in background)
- Check when settings panel opens with SourcesTab active
- Cache results for 30 minutes
- Show status: ✅ reachable, ❌ unreachable, ⏳ checking...

For user adding custom URL:
- Immediate synchronous check (show spinner while checking)
- If unreachable, show error and don't add
- This is acceptable because user explicitly triggered an action

For existing user URLs in config:
- Same as presets - check on startup/panel open with caching

Let me think about concurrency and timeout:
- 3 concurrent checks max (to avoid overwhelming network)
- 5 second timeout per URL
- If any check is pending, show "checking..." state
- Cache valid for 30 minutes

For the content-type check:
- We expect `image/*` or sometimes `video/*` from these APIs
- Some APIs might return `application/octet-stream` or just `text/html` (error pages)
- The key is: content-type starts with `image/` or `video/`, OR the response is an actual image

Actually, for reachability we just need to confirm:
1. The URL is reachable (HTTP 200)
2. The response is an image/video (content-type check)

Let me also think about URL-specific issues:
- Some random image APIs don't support HEAD requests
- Some may redirect (301/302) - need to follow redirects
- Some may have CORS issues when fetched from the webview

Wait - CORS is important. Since the plugin runs in the SiYuan webview, `fetch()` from the webview might hit CORS restrictions for some third-party APIs. However, SiYuan's webview may have relaxed CORS policies since it loads local content.

Actually, in an Electron app, the webview can typically make cross-origin requests without CORS restrictions, especially if `webSecurity: false` is set. But it depends on the SiYuan configuration.

Let me present my analysis to the user with clear options.

Actually, I realize I should also think about whether we should do reachability checks at all, or use a simpler approach. The user asked specifically about performance.

Let me structure my response:

1. When to check
2. How to check (method, timeout, caching)
3. Concurrency strategy
4. Error handling

Let me be thorough but concise.

</details>

17:     return res.code === 0 ? res.data : null
18: }

20: export async function readSiyuanDir(path: string): Promise<string[]> {

22:     if (!Array.isArray(data)) return []
23:     return (data as IDirItem[])
24:         .filter(item => !item.isDir)

29:     if (!path) return false
30:     const parentPath = path.substring(0, path.lastIndexOf('/'))
31:     const targetName = path.substring(path.lastIndexOf('/') + 1)
32:     const files = await readSiyuanDir(parentPath)
33:     return files.includes(targetName)

38:     if (!Array.isArray(data)) return []

44:     formData.append("path", path)

46:     formData.append("modTime", Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000).toString())
47:     formData.append("file", file)

54:     const res: IResponse = await fetchSyncPost("/api/file/removeFile", { path })
55:     return res.code === 0
56: }
57: 
58: export async function downloadUrl(url: string, destPath: string): Promise<boolean> {
59:     try {
60:         const response = await fetch(url)
61:         if (!response.ok) return false
62:         const blob = await response.blob()
63:         return await putFile(destPath, blob)
64:     } catch (err: any) {
65:         devDebug('[bgCover] api.ts downloadUrl 失败:', url, err.message)
66:         return false
67:     }

56:                 validExt = true
57:             } else if (contentType.startsWith('video/')) {
58:                 validExt = true
59:             } else {
60:                 errorMsg = i18n.notImageOrVideo
61:             }
62:         } catch {
63:             errorMsg = i18n.networkFailed
64:         }
65:         checking = false
66:     }
67: 
68:     function handleInput() {
69:         const trimmed = url.trim()
70:         if (!trimmed) {
71:             validExt = false
72:             errorMsg = ""
73:             previewSrc = null
74:             return
75:         }
76:         if (debounceTimer) clearTimeout(debounceTimer)
77:         debounceTimer = setTimeout(() => doCheck(trimmed), 500)
78:     }
79: 
80:     async function handleUpload() {
81:         const trimmed = url.trim()
82:         if (!trimmed || !validExt) return
83: 
84:         const fileName = trimmed.split('/').pop()?.split('?')[0] ?? 'download'
85:         const destPath = `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${fileName}`
86: 
87:         const ok = await downloadUrl(trimmed, destPath)
88:         if (ok) {
89:             const renderingUrl = getFileUrl(`/data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${fileName}`, 'upload')
90:             onSuccess?.(renderingUrl)
91:         }
92:     }
93: 
94:     function getFileName(): string {
95:         return url.trim().split('/').pop()?.split('?')[0] ?? ''
96:     }
97: 
98:     onDestroy(() => {
99:         if (blobUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(blobUrl)
100:     })
101: </script>
102: 
103: <div style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 12px; padding: 8px; width: 100%;">
104:     <div>
105:         <input class="b3-text-field fn__block" type="text" style="width: 100%;"
106:             placeholder="https://example.com/background.jpg"
107:             bind:value={url}
108:             oninput={handleInput}
109:             onkeydown={(e: KeyboardEvent) => e.key === 'Enter' && validExt && handleUpload()}
110:         />
111:     </div>
112: 
113:     <div style="min-height: 160px; display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center;
114:         border: 1px dashed var(--b3-border-color); border-radius: 6px;
115:         background: var(--b3-theme-surface);">
116:         {#if checking}
117:             <span style="color: var(--b3-theme-on-surface);">{i18n.detecting}</span>
118:         {:else if previewSrc}
119:             <img src={previewSrc} alt="preview"
120:                 style="max-width: 100%; max-height: 300px; object-fit: contain; border-radius: 4px;" />
121:         {:else if validExt}
122:             <div style="text-align: center; color: var(--b3-theme-on-surface);">
123:                 <div style="font-size: 2em;">🎬</div>
124:                 <div>{getFileName()}</div>
125:                 <div style="font-size: 0.85em; margin-top: 4px;">{i18n.videoNoPreview}</div>
126:             </div>
127:         {:else if errorMsg}
128:             <span style="color: var(--b3-theme-error); text-align: center; padding: 12px;">{errorMsg}</span>
129:         {:else}
130:             <span style="color: var(--b3-theme-on-surface);">{i18n.enterUrlHint}</span>
131:         {/if}
132:     </div>
133: 
134:     <div class="fn__flex" style="justify-content: flex-end;">
135:         <button class="b3-button b3-button--text"
136:             disabled={!validExt}
137:             onclick={handleUpload}>
138:             {i18n.upload}
139:         </button>

(End of file - total 141 lines)

Now I have a clear picture. Let me think about the reachability checking strategy.

Current UrlDialog already does:
1. Extracts extension from URL, validates against known image/video extensions
2. Fetches the URL to check content-type header
3. If image/*, downloads blob and shows preview
4. Uses 500ms debounce for input

For dynamic URL reachability, the considerations are:

**Key differences from current URL dialog:**
- Dynamic URLs are "endpoints" that return different images each time - they don't have predictable file extensions
- Need to check multiple URLs (presets + user's), not just one at a time
- Check should happen in background, not block the whole UI
- Results need to be cached so we don't hammer APIs on every settings panel open

**Performance strategy:**

1. **Check method**: Use `fetch(url, { signal: AbortSignal.timeout(8000) })` with a small download (just check content-type). For these random image APIs, HEAD requests might not work (many don't support HEAD).

Actually wait - we should use a lightweight approach. Let me think...

Option A: Full content-type check (like current UrlDialog)
- Pro: Accurate, confirms it's an image/video
- Con: Downloads the full image in some cases, slow for bulk checking

Option B: Redirect-following HEAD request  
- Pro: Minimal data transfer
- Con: Many random image APIs don't support HEAD, or return 405

Option C: Stream-based check
- Use `fetch()` with a readable stream, read just enough to detect content-type and first few bytes
- Abort after receiving headers + first chunk
- Most efficient but requires AbortController

Option D: Graduated approach
1. First, quick HEAD/GET with range and timeout
2. If fails, fall back to full GET
3. Cache results aggressively

I think the best approach is a combination:

**For preset URL checking (bulk, background):**
- Use `AbortController` with 8s timeout
- `fetch(url)` - just check response.ok and content-type
- Don't download the full body - call `response.body?.cancel()` or just abort after checking headers
- Actually, with `fetch()`, we can just check `response.ok` and `response.headers.get('content-type')` without calling `.blob()` or `.json()`. The response body will be streamed but we can ignore it.
- Cache results for 30 minutes

**For user adding a custom URL:**
- Same approach but immediate, blocking the add button until check completes
- Show spinner during check

**Concurrency:**
- Check at most 3 URLs concurrently
- Use a simple queue system

**Cache strategy:**
```typescript
interface ReachabilityCache {
    [url: string]: {
        reachable: boolean
        checkedAt: number  // timestamp
    }
}
```
- Store in module-level variable (not in config, since it's ephemeral)
- TTL: 30 minutes
- On settings panel open: check all URLs that need re-checking

Let me also think about when to trigger checks:

1. **Plugin startup**: Optional - could check presets in background after a short delay
2. **Settings panel with SourcesTab active**: Check all enabled URLs (presets + custom)
3. **User adds custom URL**: Immediate check before adding
4. **Manual refresh button**: User-triggered re-check

For the UI feedback:
- Each URL shows: 🔄 checking → ✅ reachable / ❌ unreachable
- Unreachable presets: checkbox disabled, name shows "(不可访问)"
- Unreachable custom URLs: can be removed

Let me also think about edge cases:
- What if the API sometimes returns errors (503, 429 rate limits)?
- What if the API changes its content-type?
- What about APIs that require specific headers or cookies?

For rate limiting: We should not be too aggressive with concurrent checks. 3 at a time with 500ms delay between batches is reasonable.

For reliability: A single failed check shouldn't permanently mark a URL as unreachable. Maybe check twice with a short delay before marking as unreachable.

目前 `UrlDialog.svelte` 已有单 URL 的实时可达性检测（`fetch` → 检查 `content-type`），但动态订阅源的场景不同：需要**批量检测**多个 URL、**后台运行**、**缓存结果**。

---

## 可达性检测策略讨论

### 核心挑战

| 问题 | 说明 |
|------|------|
| **批量并发** | 预设 4-5 个 + 用户自定义 N 个，不能串行 |
| **阻塞UI** | 不能让设置面板卡住等检测结果 |
| **重复请求** | 每次打开设置页不应该重新检测全部 |
| **HEAD 兼容性** | 很多随机图片 API 不支持 HEAD 请求 |
| **下载开销** | 不能像 UrlDialog 那样下载完整 blob（太慢） |

### 推荐方案：AbortController + 仅读 Header + 本地缓存

```typescript
// 仅检查响应状态和 content-type，不下载 body
async function checkReachable(url: string, timeoutMs = 8000): Promise<boolean> {
    const ctrl = new AbortController()
    const timer = setTimeout(() => ctrl.abort(), timeoutMs)
    try {
        const resp = await fetch(url, { signal: ctrl.signal })
        if (!resp.ok) return false
        const ct = resp.headers.get('content-type') ?? ''
        return ct.startsWith('image/') || ct.startsWith('video/')
    } catch {
        return false
    } finally {
        clearTimeout(timer)
    }
}
```

**为什么不需要 `.blob()`？** `response.ok` 返回时 HTTP 状态行和 Headers 已接收，`content-type` 立即可用。不调用 `.blob()` / `.json()` 则 body 流不会被消费，GC 自动回收。

### 并发控制

```
待检队列: [url1, url2, url3, url4, url5]
              │       │       │
              ▼       ▼       ▼
         并发数=3，每批间隔 200ms，失败不阻塞其他
```

```typescript
async function batchCheck(urls: string[], concurrency = 3): Promise<Map<string, boolean>> {
    const results = new Map<string, boolean>()
    for (let i = 0; i < urls.length; i += concurrency) {
        const batch = urls.slice(i, i + concurrency)
        const batchResults = await Promise.allSettled(
            batch.map(u => checkReachable(u).then(r => results.set(u, r)))
        )
        if (i + concurrency < urls.length) {
            await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 200)) // 批次间喘息
        }
    }
    return results
}
```

### 缓存策略

```typescript
// 模块级缓存，不写入 config（无需持久化）
const reachabilityCache = new Map<string, { reachable: boolean; ts: number }>()
const CACHE_TTL = 30 * 60 * 1000  // 30 分钟

function getFromCache(url: string): boolean | null {
    const entry = reachabilityCache.get(url)
    if (!entry) return null
    if (Date.now() - entry.ts > CACHE_TTL) {
        reachabilityCache.delete(url)
        return null
    }
    return entry.reachable
}
```

### 触发时机

| 时机 | 行为 |
|------|------|
| 打开设置面板 (SourcesTab) | 检查所有**缓存过期**的 URL，后台异步，逐个更新 UI |
| 用户添加自定义 URL | **同步等待**单次检测结果，block 添加按钮 |
| 插件启动 | 延迟 3s 后后台静默检测预设 URL |
| 手动刷新按钮 | 强制重新检测全部（忽略缓存） |

### 单 URL 添加 vs 批量检测的 UI 差异

```
自定义URL输入框:
  [https://...]  [添加]  ← 点击后: [https://...]  [🔄 检测中...] → [✅ 已添加] / [❌ 不可达]

预设列表:
  ✅ 必应每日壁纸         [✓]
  ❌ 随机二次元 (不可访问)  [ ]  ← checkbox disabled
  🔄 Unsplash 随机       [✓]  ← 检测中可操作但标记待确认
```

---

### 潜在风险和降级

1. **API 限流 (429)**：`batchCheck` 的并发=3 + 批次间 delay=200ms 已经比较保守
2. **网络波动假阴性**：缓存 30 分钟过期后自动重试；提供手动刷新按钮
3. **CORS 问题**：思源 Electron webview 通常不限制 CORS，但部分 API 可能有额外限制。这些 URL 即使 `checkReachable` 失败，`render()` 时通过 fetch+putFile 可能仍然可用（因为渲染 pipeline 用的是相同的 fetch）。可考虑加一个"强制添加"选项

---

你觉得这个策略有什么需要调整的地方？特别是：
- 缓存 TTL 30 分钟是否合理？
- 并发数 3 是否合适？
- 是否需要"不可达但仍强制添加"的降级选项？

*[step-finish part]*

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

The user is asking whether we should skip reachability checking entirely and just directly insert the dynamic URL into the canvas when randomly selected, regardless of whether the URL works.

Let me think about this carefully from both a technical and UX perspective.

**Technical perspective:**

For the "direct canvas insertion" approach to work, we'd need to set the canvas CSS background-image directly to the dynamic URL:

```css
background-image: url('https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images');
```

Issues with this:
1. **Browser caching**: The browser will cache the image at the URL. If the same URL returns different images each time, the browser might serve the cached version instead. This defeats the purpose of random image APIs. We'd need cache-busting in the URL itself (append `?t=timestamp`).

2. **Mixed content**: If the API is HTTP (not HTTPS) and SiYuan's webview loads from HTTPS, the browser will block mixed content.

3. **CORS**: Canvas/background-image loading is not subject to CORS, so this is actually not an issue for CSS background-image.

4. **The current plugin's rendering pipeline** (`bgRender.ts`) sets `canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url('${url}')`. This would work with an absolute HTTPS URL directly.

5. **However**, the current plugin distinguishes image vs video by file extension. For dynamic URLs, the extension check wouldn't work because URLs like `https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images` don't have image extensions.

Wait, let me re-read the bgRender code to understand this better.

Actually, the user said "直接插入canvas中" - put the URL directly into the canvas CSS. This is different from the current approach of downloading to a local temp file. Let me evaluate both:

**Approach A: Direct canvas URL (user's suggestion)**
- Simply set `canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url('https://api.example.com/random')`  
- Need cache-busting: `url('https://api.example.com/random?t=Date.now()')`
- No download, no storage, no reachability check
- Minimal code complexity
- But: can't detect image vs video without fetching headers
- But: browser caching might still kick in even with cache-busting params
- But: some APIs might return redirects that don't work well with CSS url()

**Approach B: Download to temp file (my earlier suggestion)**
- `fetch() → putFile() → url('public/plugin/_dynamic_bg.jpg')`
- Need reachability checking for good UX
- More code, but more control
- Can detect type and handle both image and video
- Can handle errors gracefully

Actually, the simplest possible approach is user's suggestion. Let me think about whether it would actually work...

The biggest issue is **browser caching**. Even with `?t=timestamp`, some browsers/servers might still cache. The `Cache-Control` header from the server matters.

Another issue: **changing the background-image CSS property might not trigger a re-fetch**. Browsers are smart about caching and might serve from disk cache even if the URL has a different query parameter (though in practice, changing query params usually works as cache-busting).

Actually, in practice, `?t=${Date.now()}` is widely used for cache-busting and works reliably. Browsers treat different query params as different resources.

The real question is: is the simplicity worth the risk of silent failures?

**My analysis:**

PROS of skipping reachability checks:
- Minimal code (no checkReachable, no batchCheck, no cache, no UI states)
- No network overhead from the plugin side
- Fastest possible implementation
- Least complexity

CONS:
- If a URL is dead, user gets a broken background (silent failure)
- Can't distinguish image vs video before rendering
- Cache-busting still needed
- No feedback to user about which URLs work

I think the user's instinct is right - the simplest approach is often best. However, there's a middle ground:

**Middle ground: Minimal approach**
1. Store dynamic URLs in config (presets + custom)
2. When randomly selected, append `?t=timestamp` for cache-busting
3. Set `canvasEl.style.backgroundImage` directly to the URL
4. For video detection: maybe try a quick HEAD/fetch when the URL is selected (not when added)
5. No pre-checking, no caching, no reachability management UI

Actually, even simpler - since all these random image APIs return images (not videos), we can just:
1. Append cache-bust param
2. Set as background-image
3. If it fails, the background is just blank/transparent - the user's normal content is still visible

The user asked for plugin-side simplicity and performance. The direct approach meets that perfectly.

But wait - the current plugin's bgRender.ts distinguishes image vs video based on file extension in the URL. For URLs like `https://imgapi.cn/api.php?...`, there's no image extension. We'd need to update `detectType()` to handle this case. Or we could just assume image for dynamic URLs.

Let me think about what changes would actually be needed for the simplest approach:

1. `detectType()` in bgRender.ts: Needs to handle URLs without recognizable extensions. For dynamic URLs, assume image (or do a quick fetch to check content-type at render time).
2. Cache-busting in bgRender.ts: When rendering a dynamic URL, append timestamp param.
3. Config: Add `dynamicBgUrls: string[]`

153:     const posX = x ?? defaultX ?? 50
154:     const posY = y ?? defaultY ?? 50
155:     changePosition(posX, posY)
156: }
157: 
158: export function startAutoRefresh(callback: () => void, intervalMs: number): void {
159:     stopAutoRefresh()
160:     if (intervalMs <= 0) return
161:     devLog("[bgCover] startAutoRefresh: interval =", intervalMs, "ms")
162:     autoRefreshTimer = setInterval(callback, intervalMs)
163: }
164: 
165: export function stopAutoRefresh(): void {
166:     if (autoRefreshTimer !== null) {
167:         devLog("[bgCover] stopAutoRefresh")
168:         clearInterval(autoRefreshTimer)
169:         autoRefreshTimer = null
170:     }
171: }

(End of file - total 171 lines)

### 🤖 Assistant
*2026-05-19 14:16:11*

*[step-start part]*

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

Now I see the key issue: `detectType()` on line 13-19 splits by `?` and checks file extension. For a URL like `https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images`, the path after `?` removal is `https://imgapi.cn/api.php`, and `.php` is not in IMAGE_EXTS or VIDEO_EXTS. So `detectType()` returns `null`, and `render()` does nothing (neither renderImage nor renderVideo is called).

This is the main blocker for the "direct canvas URL" approach. But it's easy to solve: we can add one more parameter or path.

Let me think about the options to handle this:

Option 1: Modify `detectType()` to also check MIME types via fetch (adds complexity back)
Option 2: Add a `type` parameter to `render()` for cases where extension detection fails
Option 3: For dynamic URLs, always assume 'image' (since these APIs return images)
Option 4: Store the type alongside the URL in config

Actually, looking at the Dark+ theme approach, it simply adds these URLs to a list and uses them. Theme CSS sets `body { background-image: url(...) }` and the browser handles it. The theme doesn't do any download or type detection.

For our plugin's architecture, the simplest fix for `detectType()` would be:

```typescript
function detectType(url: string): 'image' | 'video' | null {
    // Dynamic URLs (random image APIs) are assumed to be images
    if (isDynamicUrl(url)) return 'image'
    
    const clean = url.split('?')[0]
    const ext = '.' + (clean.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
    if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) return 'video'
    if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext)) return 'image'
    return null
}
```

But how to know if a URL is dynamic? We could pass a flag, or check against the config's dynamicBgUrls list.

Or even simpler: change the `render()` function signature to accept an optional type:

```typescript
export function render(url: string, forceType?: 'image' | 'video'): void {
    const type = forceType ?? detectType(url)
    if (type === 'image') renderImage(url)
    else if (type === 'video') renderVideo(url)
}
```

This is the most backward-compatible approach. Source manager would call `render(url, 'image')` for dynamic URLs.

Now about cache-busting: we need to append `?t=timestamp` before setting the background-image. Where to do this?

Option A: In `renderImage()` - add cache-busting for all URLs (simple but changes behavior for all sources)
Option B: Only for dynamic URLs - the caller appends the cache-bust param before calling render
Option C: Add a param to `renderImage()` like `noCache: boolean`

I think Option B is cleanest - the caller (sourceManager or whoever picks the dynamic URL) handles cache-busting before passing to render.

So the flow for dynamic URLs would be:
```
pickRandom selects dynamic URL
  → append ?_t=Date.now() for cache busting
  → bgRender.render(cacheBustUrl, 'image')
    → detectType skips, uses forceType='image'
    → canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url('https://imgapi.cn/...?_t=1234567890')
```

This is extremely simple. No download, no temp file, no reachability check, no cache management. Just:
1. Config stores `dynamicBgUrls: string[]`
2. SourceManager includes dynamic URLs in random pool
3. When selected, append cache-bust + force render as image
4. Canvas CSS directly references the URL

The total code needed:
- Config: 1 new field
- bgRender: modify `render()` to accept optional type
- sourceManager: include dynamic URLs in pool, handle cache-bust on selection
- UI: presets list + custom URL input

This is indeed the simplest approach. Let me present this analysis to the user.

</details>

好问题。让我对比一下关键差异。

## 两种方案对比

### 方案 A：跳过可达性检查，直接插入 canvas

```
选中动态URL → 追加 ?_t=timestamp → canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url(...)
                                  → videoEl.src = url(...)
```

### 方案 B：下载到本地后再渲染（之前讨论的）

```
选中动态URL → fetch() → putFile(tempPath) → canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url('public/...')
```

| 维度 | 方案 A (直接 canvas) | 方案 B (下载到本地) |
|------|---------------------|---------------------|
| 代码量 | ~50 行 | ~150 行 |
| 可达性检测 | 不需要 | 建议有 |
| 本地缓存 | 不需要 | 需要 |
| 存储占用 | 0 | 每次覆盖一个临时文件 |
| 失败表现 | 背景空白（静默） | 有明确错误反馈 |
| 缓存破坏 | `?t=Date.now()` | 下载本身不缓存 |
| 需要修改 `detectType()` | 是（动态URL无后缀） | 是（同样问题） |

## 方案 A 完全可行，唯一需要处理的点

当前 `bgRender.ts:13-19` 的 `detectType()` 靠 URL 文件后缀判断 image/video：

```typescript
function detectType(url: string): 'image' | 'video' | null {
    const clean = url.split('?')[0]
    const ext = '.' + (clean.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
    // https://imgapi.cn/api.php → ext='.php' → null，不渲染！
}
```

只需让 `render()` 接受可选类型参数：

```typescript
export function render(url: string, forceType?: 'image' | 'video'): void {
    const type = forceType ?? detectType(url)
    if (type === 'image') renderImage(url)
    else if (type === 'video') renderVideo(url)
}
```

调用侧对动态 URL 传入 `'image'`（这类 API 不存在返回视频的）。

## 结论

**推荐方案 A**。理由：

1. 代码量最小，整个功能只涉及 5-6 个文件的少量改动
2. 失败静默降级：canvas 背景不显示，用户笔记内容完全不受影响
3. 无网络开销：不预先检测，只在真正需要渲染时才发一次 HTTP 请求
4. 缓存破坏用 `?t=Date.now()` 是成熟做法，Chrome/Electron 对 CSS `url()` 可正确处理
5. 用户如果发现某个源不行，从列表中去掉即可——不值得为此维护一个检测+缓存基础设施

要确认一下：方案 A 作为实施方向，可以吗？

The user is confirming plan A and providing additional requirements:

1. **Dynamic URLs default to image type** - these APIs return images, not videos
2. **Video background info in About tab** - list sites where users can download videos manually, then add via local/upload
3. **ConfigTab current background display** - needs to update when dynamic URL is selected, showing the URL itself (since there's no filename)
4. **404 fallback image** - if dynamic URL fails, show a built-in fallback image instead of blank canvas

Let me think about each point:

### Point 3: ConfigTab current background display

Looking at ConfigTab, it probably shows `currentFile` which is typically a filename or path. For dynamic URLs, `currentFile` would be something like `https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images` - which is quite long and unreadable.

The user wants it to update to show what the current background is. For dynamic URLs, we could:
- Show the URL (truncated)
- Show a label like "动态: 随机风景"
- Store both the URL and a display name

Actually, looking at how currentFile works: it stores the rendering URL. For dynamic URLs, the URL IS the source. So `currentFile` would just be the URL. The ConfigTab can display it differently based on whether it's a dynamic URL (maybe show a label from the preset list, or truncated URL).

### Point 4: 404 fallback image

This is smart. If a dynamic URL fails to load (network error, API down), the canvas shows nothing (blank). Having a fallback image provides graceful degradation.

How to implement:
- Include a small built-in fallback image (or use one of the existing `DEFAULT_BACKGROUNDS`)
- When `currentFile` is set but it's a dynamic URL, set up both:
  a. The dynamic URL as the primary background
  b. The fallback image as a secondary background (using CSS `background-image` with multiple layers?)
  
Wait, CSS doesn't have a "fallback if first fails" mechanism for `background-image`. We could use:
- Multiple background layers: `background-image: url(dynamic), url(fallback)` - but this shows BOTH if both load
- JavaScript `onerror` handler: listen for image load failure, then switch to fallback
- Set fallback first, then try dynamic - if dynamic loads, it overrides

Actually, for `<img>` elements there's `onerror`, but for CSS `background-image` on a canvas, there's no direct error event.

Options:
1. Use a hidden `<img>` element to test-load the dynamic URL, listen for onerror
2. Set fallback as background first, then dynamically set the URL - if URL loads, it covers fallback
3. Use `fetch()` to test the URL, then decide which to use

Option 1 is cleanest:
- Create a hidden `<img>` with the dynamic URL
- On `onload`: set canvas background to the dynamic URL
- On `onerror`: set canvas background to the fallback image

This adds a small amount of complexity but is robust.

Let me also think about the fallback image itself:
- Could use one of the existing default backgrounds: `DEFAULT_BACKGROUNDS[0]` or `DEFAULT_BACKGROUNDS[1]`
- Or create a simple "no background" image
- Or just use a plain color

Actually, the simplest and most useful fallback would be one of the existing default backgrounds. The user won't be left with a broken blank state.

65:             const files = await scanSource('assets', path + '/')
66:             return { type: 'assets' as const, label, path, files, normalized }
67:         })
68: 
69:         const localTasks = localFolders.map(async (dir) => {
70:             const files = await scanSource('local', dir + (dir.endsWith('/') ? '' : '/'))
71:             return { type: 'local' as const, label: dir, path: dir, files }
72:         })
73: 
74:         const allScanResults = await Promise.all([...assetTasks, ...localTasks])
75: 
76:         for (const r of allScanResults) {
77:             if (r.type === 'assets') {
78:                 newGroups.push({
79:                     type: 'assets', label: r.label, path: r.path,
80:                     removable: true, files: r.files,
81:                     inaccessible: r.files.length === 0 && r.path.length > 0,
82:                     collapsed: false, configKey: r.normalized,
83:                 })
84:             } else {
85:                 newGroups.push({
86:                     type: 'local', label: r.label, path: r.path,
87:                     removable: true, files: r.files,
88:                     inaccessible: r.files.length === 0,
89:                     collapsed: false, configKey: r.label,
90:                 })
91:             }
92:         }
93: 
94:         groups = newGroups
95:     }
96: 
97:     function toggleGroup(i: number) {
98:         groups[i].collapsed = !groups[i].collapsed
99:         groups = groups
100:     }
101: 
102:     function openAssetDirDialog() {
103:         showAssetsDirDialog((paths: string[]) => {
104:             for (const dir of paths) addAssetFolder(dir)
105:         })
106:     }
107: 
108:     function openLocalDirDialog() {
109:         showLocalDirDialog((path: string) => {

111:         })

113: 
114:     function addAssetFolder(dir: string) {
115:         if (!dir) return
116:         devLog("[bgCover] addAssetFolder:", dir)
117:         const dirs = [...configStore.get("assetDirs"), dir]
118:         configStore.set("assetDirs", dirs)

122: 
123:     function addLocalFolder(path: string) {
124:         if (!path) return

127:         configStore.set("localFolders", folders)
128:         configStore.save()
129:         refreshAll()
130:     }
131: 
132:     function removeGroup(i: number) {
133:         const g = groups[i]
134:         devLog("[bgCover] removeGroup:", g.type, g.configKey)
135:         const currentFile = configStore.get("currentFile")
136:         const wasCurrentInGroup = g.files.some(f => f.url === currentFile)
137:         if (g.type === 'assets') {
138:             const dirs = [...configStore.get("assetDirs")]
139:             const idx = dirs.indexOf(g.configKey)
140:             if (idx >= 0) {
141:                 dirs.splice(idx, 1)
142:                 configStore.set("assetDirs", dirs)
143:                 configStore.save()
144:             }
145:         } else if (g.type === 'local') {
146:             const dirs = [...configStore.get("localFolders")]
147:             const idx = dirs.indexOf(g.configKey)
148:             if (idx >= 0) {
149:                 dirs.splice(idx, 1)
150:                 configStore.set("localFolders", dirs)
151:                 configStore.save()
152:             }
153:         }
154:         clearPreview()

156:             reselectBackground()
157:         }
158:         refreshAll()
159:     }
160: 
161:     function setAsBackground(item: ImageItem) {
162:         devLog("[bgCover] setAsBackground:", item.name)
163:         configStore.set("currentFile", item.url)
164:         configStore.save()
165:         if (item.type === 'image') {
166:             renderImage(item.url)
167:         } else {
168:             renderVideo(item.url)
169:         }
170:     }
171: 
172:     function selectPreview(item: ImageItem) {
173:         if (item.type !== 'image') return
174:         if (selectedItem?.url === item.url) {
175:             clearPreview()
176:             return
177:         }
178:         selectedItem = item
179:         loadPreview(item.url)
180:     }
181: 
182:     function clearPreview() {
183:         if (previewObjectUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(previewObjectUrl)
184:         selectedItem = null
185:         previewSrc = null
186:         previewObjectUrl = null
187:     }
188: 
189:     function loadPreview(url: string) {
190:         if (previewObjectUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(previewObjectUrl)
191:         previewObjectUrl = null
192:         previewSrc = null
193:         fetch(url)
194:             .then(r => r.blob())
195:             .then(b => {
196:                 if (selectedItem?.url === url) {
197:                     previewObjectUrl = URL.createObjectURL(b)
198:                     previewSrc = previewObjectUrl
199:                 }
200:             })
201:             .catch(() => {})
202:     }
203: 
204:     async function clearCache() {
205:         const group = groups.find(g => g.type === 'upload')
206:         if (!group || group.files.length === 0) return
207:         const imgCount = group.files.filter(f => f.type === 'image').length
208:         const vidCount = group.files.filter(f => f.type === 'video').length
209:         const parts: string[] = []
210:         if (imgCount > 0) parts.push(`${imgCount} ${i18n.imageCount}`)
211:         if (vidCount > 0) parts.push(`${vidCount} ${i18n.videoCount}`)
212:         const confirmed = await new Promise<boolean>(resolve => {
213:             confirmDialog({
214:                 title: i18n.clearCacheTitle,
215:                 content: `${i18n.clearCacheConfirm} ${parts.join('、')}`,                confirm: () => resolve(true),
216:                 cancel: () => resolve(false),
217:                 width: "360px",
218:             })
219:         })
220:         if (!confirmed) return
221:         devLog("[bgCover] clearCache:", group.files.length, "files")
222:         const wasCurrentDeleted = group.files.some(f => f.url === configStore.get("currentFile"))
223:         for (const file of group.files) {
224:             await removeFile(file.apiPath)
225:         }
226:         if (wasCurrentDeleted) await reselectBackground()
227:         refreshAll()
228:     }
229: 
230:     function openInFileManager(group: SourceGroup) {
231:         const wsDir = (window as any).siyuan?.config?.system?.workspaceDir ?? ''
232:         let absPath = group.path
233:         if (group.type === 'upload' || group.type === 'assets') {
234:             absPath = wsDir + absPath
235:         }
236:         try {
237:             const shell = (window as any).require?.('electron')?.shell
238:             if (shell) {
239:                 shell.openPath(absPath)
240:             } else {
241:                 const { exec } = (window as any).require?.('child_process') ?? {}
242:                 if (exec) {
243:                     const cmd = process.platform === 'darwin' ? 'open' : process.platform === 'win32' ? 'explorer' : 'xdg-open'
244:                     exec(`${cmd} "${absPath}"`)
245:                 }
246:             }
247:         } catch { /* ignore */ }
248:     }
249: 
250:     async function reselectBackground() {
251:         configStore.set("currentFile", null)
252:         await configStore.save()
253:         await (window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.plugin?.randomSelect?.()
254:         if (!configStore.get("currentFile")) {
255:             configStore.set("currentFile", pickDefaultBackground())
256:             await configStore.save()
257:             ;(window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.plugin?.applyBackground?.()
258:         }
259:     }
260: 
261:     async function deleteFile(file: ImageItem) {
262:         devLog("[bgCover] deleteFile:", file.name)
263:         const wasCurrent = file.url === configStore.get("currentFile")
264:         await removeFile(file.apiPath)
265:         if (wasCurrent) await reselectBackground()
266:         refreshAll()
267:     }
268: 
269:     function pickMultipleFiles() {
270:         setupMultipleFilePicker(() => { refreshAll() })

272: 
273:     function pickFolderFiles() {

275:     }

11:     assetDirs: string[] = [],
12:     localFolders: string[] = [],
13: ): Promise<ImageItem[]> {
14:     const tasks: Promise<ImageItem[]>[] = [

16:     ]

18:     const validAssetDirs = assetDirs.filter(d => d.length > 0)

40:     const results = batch.flat()
41:     devDebug(`${ENGINE} scanAll total: ${results.length} 个文件`)

45: export async function scanSource(
46:     type: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets',
47:     path: string,
48: ): Promise<ImageItem[]> {
49:     const filenames = type === 'local'
50:         ? await readLocalDir(path)
51:         : await readSiyuanDir(path)
52: 
53:     const items: ImageItem[] = []
54:     const skipped: string[] = []
55: 
56:     for (const name of filenames) {
57:         const fileType = classifyFileType(name)
58: 
59:         if (fileType === null) {
60:             skipped.push(name)
61:             continue
62:         }
63: 
64:         const cleanPath = path.endsWith('/') ? path : path + '/'
65:         const apiPath = `${cleanPath}${name}`
66:         const url = getFileUrl(apiPath, type)
67: 
68:         items.push({
69:             name,
70:             url,
71:             apiPath,
72:             type: fileType,
73:             sourceType: type,
74:             sourceLabel: getSourceLabel(type, path),
75:         })
76:     }
77: 
78:     if (skipped.length > 0) {
79:         devDebug(`${ENGINE} scanSource[${type}] 跳过不可识别的文件: [${skipped.join(', ')}]`)
80:     }
81: 
82:     return items
83: }
84: 
85: export function pickRandom(items: ImageItem[], excludeUrl?: string | null): ImageItem | null {
86:     if (items.length === 0) return null
87: 
88:     if (excludeUrl) {
89:         const filtered = items.filter(item => item.url !== excludeUrl)
90:         if (filtered.length === 0) return null
91:         const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * filtered.length)
92:         return filtered[idx]
93:     }
94: 
95:     const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * items.length)
96:     return items[idx]
97: }
98: 
99: export async function validatePath(path: string): Promise<boolean> {
100:     if (path.length === 0) return false
101: 
102:     if (isDesktop()) {
103:         return fileExistsLocal(path)
104:     }
105: 
106:     try {
107:         await readSiyuanDir(path)
108:         return true
109:     } catch {
110:         return false
111:     }
112: }
113: 
114: function getSourceLabel(type: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets', path: string): string {
115:     switch (type) {
116:         case 'upload':
117:             return 'upload'
118:         case 'assets':
119:             return toAssetRelPath(path)
120:         case 'local':
121:             return path
122:     }

Wait, let me also think about the fallback image approach more carefully.

For the fallback, the user suggested a "404 background image" - a default image that shows when dynamic URL fails.

The best approach:
1. Include a small built-in fallback image as a base64 data URI in constants (or reuse one of the existing default backgrounds)
2. In `bgRender.ts`, add a `renderDynamic(url: string, fallbackUrl?: string)` function
3. Use a hidden `<img>` element to test-load the dynamic URL:
   - If `onload` fires: set canvas background to dynamic URL
   - If `onerror` fires: set canvas background to fallback URL

Actually, for CSS background-image, we can use two layers:
```css
background-image: url(fallback), url(dynamic_with_cache_bust);
```
The browser will try to load both. If dynamic fails, fallback remains visible. But the issue is: if dynamic loads, BOTH are visible (fallback behind dynamic, which is fine since dynamic covers it).

Wait, actually this is exactly what we want! The CSS would be:
```css
background-image: url('dynamic?t=123'), url('fallback');
background-size: cover, cover;
```

But there's a subtle issue: CSS loads all background layers regardless. If the dynamic URL returns a 404, the browser just doesn't render that layer, and the fallback shows through. If the dynamic URL loads, it renders on top of the fallback.

This is simpler than the hidden `<img>` approach! No extra DOM manipulation needed.

BUT - there's a potential flicker. When switching backgrounds:
1. Set fallback first → fallback visible
2. Immediately set dynamic → browser starts loading dynamic
3. If dynamic loads → dynamic covers fallback
4. If dynamic fails → fallback remains

The flicker would happen between step 1 and 3, but since it's all in one CSS update, it should be atomic.

Actually no, CSS background-image layers are applied top to bottom (first listed is topmost). So:
```css
background-image: url('dynamic?t=123'), url('fallback');
```
- dynamic is top layer
- If dynamic loads: dynamic is shown (covers fallback)
- If dynamic fails: fallback shows through

This is actually perfect and elegant. Only concern: if the dynamic URL takes a long time to load, the user sees the fallback first, then the dynamic. But this is acceptable UX.

Let me use this approach. The fallback image can be one of the `DEFAULT_BACKGROUNDS` entries, or a specific built-in fallback.

```typescript
export const DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK = DEFAULT_BACKGROUNDS[0]  // or a specific default image

```

The first one is a video! Better to use the second (the JPG image) or create a specific fallback path.

Let me use the JPG default background as fallback. Or better yet, define an explicit constant.

Actually, I'll just use `DEFAULT_BACKGROUNDS.find(bg => bg.endsWith('.jpg'))` or hardcode the JPG one.

Let me now think about the ConfigTab display for dynamic URLs.

Currently:
```svelte
<code class="fn__code">{currentFile ?? i18n.none}</code>
```

For a dynamic URL, `currentFile` would be like `https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images?_t=1234567890` which is very long. We should display a friendly name.

Option 1: Store just the URL (without cache-busting) in `currentFile`, and add cache-busting only at render time.
Option 2: Store a display name alongside.

I think the cleanest approach:
- `currentFile` stores the canonical URL WITHOUT cache-busting
- `randomSelect()` adds cache-busting when calling `renderDynamic`
- ConfigTab checks if `currentFile` matches a dynamic URL and displays preset name, or truncates

Actually, better: we can look up the preset name from the URL. If the URL matches a preset, show the name; otherwise show shortened URL.

Or even simpler: `currentFile` stores the dynamic URL (no cache-busting). ConfigTab just shows it truncated.

```typescript
function displayCurrentFile(currentFile: string): string {
    // Check if it's a known preset
    const preset = DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS.find(p => p.url === currentFile)
    if (preset) return `🌐 ${preset.name}`
    // If it looks like a URL (not a file path)
    if (currentFile.startsWith('http')) {
        const url = new URL(currentFile)
        return `🌐 ${url.hostname}${url.pathname.substring(0, 30)}...`
    }
    return currentFile
}
```

This keeps the config simple (just stores URL strings) while providing a friendly display.

Wait, one more thing: for `applyBackground()` in index.ts, it uses extension detection:
```typescript
const ext = '.' + (currentFile.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) renderVideo(currentFile)
else if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext)) renderImage(currentFile)
else console.warn(`unknown extension "${ext}"`)
```

For a dynamic URL like `https://imgapi.cn/api.php?...`, the extension would be `.php?...` after splitting. This won't match and will log a warning and skip rendering.

I need to fix this in `applyBackground()`:
```typescript
if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) {
    renderVideo(currentFile)
} else if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext)) {
    renderImage(currentFile)
} else if (isDynamicUrl(currentFile)) {
    // Dynamic URLs don't have recognizable extensions
    renderDynamic(currentFile, DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL)
} else {
    console.warn(`unknown extension "${ext}"`)
    return
}
```

And in `randomSelect()`:
```typescript
if (item.sourceType === 'dynamic') {
    const cacheBustUrl = item.url + (item.url.includes('?') ? '&' : '?') + '_t=' + Date.now()
    renderDynamic(cacheBustUrl, DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL)
} else if (item.type === 'image') {
    renderImage(item.url)
} else {
    renderVideo(item.url)
}
```

OK, now I need to also think about how `renderDynamic` works with the fallback approach.

```typescript
export function renderDynamic(url: string, fallbackUrl: string): void {
    if (!canvasEl) return
    currentMode = 'image'
    
    if (videoEl) {
        videoEl.style.display = 'none'
        try { videoEl.pause() } catch { /* ignored */ }
        videoEl.removeAttribute('src')
    }
    canvasEl.style.display = ''
    // Layer 1 (top): dynamic URL with cache-busting
    // Layer 2 (bottom): fallback image that shows if dynamic fails
    canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}'), url('${fallbackUrl}')`
}
```

This is clean and simple. The CSS handles the fallback natively.

For `backgroundSize`, since we're using `cover` for single images, with multiple layers we need `cover, cover`:
```css
background-size: cover, cover;
```

But currently `backgroundSize` is set once in `createBgLayer()`. We'd need to override it:
```typescript
canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover, cover'
```

Actually, we can just do this once in the `renderDynamic` function.

One last consideration: when the user switches from a dynamic background to a regular file, the CSS properties like `backgroundSize` need to be reset. This should be handled by `renderImage()` which already sets the single `cover`.

OK, I'm satisfied with the plan. Let me present it now.

好的，现在我有了完整理解。下面是根据你的三个补充要求调整后的最终计划。

---

## 实施计划：动态订阅源 (Plan A 增强版)

### 你的三个补充要求

| # | 要求 | 解决方案 |
|---|------|---------|
| 1 | 动态URL默认图片类型 | `render()` 接受可选 `forceType`，动态URL传 `'image'`；About页列视频站 |
| 2 | ConfigTab 当前背景更新 | `currentFile` 存原始 URL，ConfigTab 按预设名/域名截断显示 |
| 3 | 404 fallback 底图 | CSS `background-image` 双层：`url(dynamic), url(fallback)` |

### 新增关键设计

#### 1. Fallback 机制：CSS 双层 background-image

```
background-image: url('https://imgapi.cn/...?_t=12345'), url('plugins/.../default.jpg');
                     ─────────── Layer 1 (top) ──────────   ── Layer 2 (bottom) ──
```

- 动态 URL 加载成功 → Layer 1 覆盖 Layer 2，用户看到动态图
- 动态 URL 404/超时 → Layer 1 渲染失败，Layer 2 自动暴露
- **零 JS 开销**，完全由浏览器引擎处理，无需 `<img onerror>` hack

#### 2. `randomSelect()` 和 `applyBackground()` 两个入口都要处理动态URL

当前这两个函数都靠文件后缀决定 image/video。动态URL 无有效后缀，需要特殊分支。

### 文件改动清单（11 个文件）

```
修改:
  src/types.ts              sourceType 联合添加 'dynamic'
  src/constants.ts          预设列表 + fallback 常量 + isDynamicUrl()
  src/stores/config.ts      AppConfig 新增 dynamicBgUrls

export const DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS = [
    { id: 'bing_1920',     name: '必应每日壁纸',          url: 'https://api.dujin.org/bing/1920.php' },
    { id: 'imgapi_scenic', name: '随机风景 (imgapi.cn)',  url: 'https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images' },
    { id: 'unsplash_rand', name: 'Unsplash 随机',         url: 'https://source.unsplash.com/random/1920x1080' },
]
export const DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL = DEFAULT_BACKGROUNDS[1]  // 内置 JPG
export function isDynamicUrl(url: string, dynamicUrls: string[]): boolean { ... }
```

**`bgRender.ts`** — 核心渲染改动
```typescript
export function render(url: string, forceType?: 'image' | 'video'): void {
    const type = forceType ?? detectType(url)
    ...
}

export function renderDynamic(url: string, fallbackUrl: string): void {
    // double-layer CSS background for auto-fallback
    canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}'), url('${fallbackUrl}')`
    canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover, cover'
    currentMode = 'image'
}
```

**`sourceManager.ts`** — 动态源纳入扫描池
```typescript
export function scanDynamicUrls(urls: string[]): ImageItem[] {
    return urls.map(url => ({
        name: getDynamicPresetName(url) ?? new URL(url).hostname,
        url,
        apiPath: url,    // 无本地路径，用 URL 本身
        type: 'image',   // 默认 image
        sourceType: 'dynamic',
        sourceLabel: 'dynamic',
    }))
}
```

**`index.ts`** — 两个入口适配
```typescript
async randomSelect() {
    const dynamicUrls = configStore.get("dynamicBgUrls")
    const pool = await scanAll(assetDirs, localFolders, dynamicUrls)
    // ...
    if (item.sourceType === 'dynamic') {
        const cb = item.url + (item.url.includes('?') ? '&' : '?') + '_t=' + Date.now()
        renderDynamic(cb, DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL)
    } else if (item.type === 'image') {
        renderImage(item.url)
    } else {
        renderVideo(item.url)
    }
}

private applyBackground() {
    const currentFile = configStore.get("currentFile")
    // ...
    if (isDynamicUrl(currentFile)) {
        const cb = currentFile + (currentFile.includes('?') ? '&' : '?') + '_t=' + Date.now()
        renderDynamic(cb, DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL)
    } else if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) { ... }
    else if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext)) { ... }
}
```

**`ConfigTab.svelte`** — 当前背景显示

    {#if isDynamicUrl(currentFile)}
        🌐 {presetName ?? currentFile}   <!-- 查找预设名，兜底显示截断URL -->
    {:else}
        {currentFile ?? i18n.none}
