### 各文件改动详情

#### 1. `types.ts`

```typescript
export interface ImageItem {
    // ... existing fields ...
    sourceType: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets' | 'dynamic'  // 新增
}
```

#### 2. `constants.ts`

```typescript
export const DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS = [
    { id: 'bing_1920',     name: '必应每日壁纸',          url: 'https://api.dujin.org/bing/1920.php' },
    { id: 'imgapi_scenic', name: '随机风景 (imgapi.cn)',  url: 'https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images' },
    { id: 'unsplash_rand', name: 'Unsplash 随机',         url: 'https://source.unsplash.com/random/1920x1080' },
]

export const DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL = DEFAULT_BACKGROUNDS[1]
  // plugins/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/default/FyBE0bUakAELfeF.jpg

export function isDynamicUrl(url: string): boolean {
    const clean = url.split('?')[0]
    const ext = '.' + (clean.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
    return !IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext) && !VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext) && url.startsWith('http')
}
```

#### 3. `bgRender.ts` — 两个关键改动

```typescript
// ① 接受可选类型强制
export function render(url: string, forceType?: 'image' | 'video'): void {
    const type = forceType ?? detectType(url)
    if (type === 'image') renderImage(url)
    else if (type === 'video') renderVideo(url)
}

// ② CSS 双层 background 自动 fallback
export function renderDynamic(url: string, fallbackUrl: string): void {
    if (!canvasEl) return
    if (videoEl) {
        videoEl.style.display = 'none'
        try { videoEl.pause() } catch { /* ignored */ }
        videoEl.removeAttribute('src')
    }
    currentMode = 'image'
    canvasEl.style.display = ''
    canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}'), url('${fallbackUrl}')`
    canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover, cover'
}
```

#### 4. `sourceManager.ts`

```typescript
export async function scanAll(
    assetDirs: string[] = [],
    localFolders: string[] = [],
    dynamicBgUrls: string[] = [],      // 新增参数
): Promise<ImageItem[]> {
    const tasks: Promise<ImageItem[]>[] = [
        scanSource('upload', pluginAssetsDir),
        scanDynamicUrls(dynamicBgUrls),  // 新增
    ]
    // ...
}

export function scanDynamicUrls(urls: string[]): ImageItem[] {
    return urls.map(url => {
        const preset = DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS.find(p => p.url === url)
        return {
            name: preset?.name ?? new URL(url).hostname,
            url,
            apiPath: url,
            type: 'image' as const,
            sourceType: 'dynamic' as const,
            sourceLabel: 'dynamic',
        }
    })
}
```

#### 5. `index.ts` — 两个入口适配

```typescript
// randomSelect: 加入 dynamicBgUrls 到扫描池
async randomSelect() {
    const dynamicUrls = configStore.get("dynamicBgUrls")
    const pool = await scanAll(assetDirs, localFolders, dynamicUrls)
    // ...
    if (item.sourceType === 'dynamic') {
        const cb = item.url + (item.url.includes('?') ? '&' : '?') + '_t=' + Date.now()
        renderDynamic(cb, DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL)
    } else if (item.type === 'image') {
        renderImage(item.url)
    } else {
        renderVideo(item.url)
    }
}

// applyBackground: 处理无后缀的 dynamic URL
private applyBackground() {
    const currentFile = configStore.get("currentFile")
    if (!currentFile) return

    if (isDynamicUrl(currentFile)) {
        const cb = currentFile + (currentFile.includes('?') ? '&' : '?') + '_t=' + Date.now()
        renderDynamic(cb, DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL)
    } else if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) {
        renderVideo(currentFile)
    } else if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext)) {
        renderImage(currentFile)
    } else {
        console.warn(...)
        return
    }
    // ... opacity, blur, position ...
}
```

#### 6. `SourcesTab.svelte` — 顶部新增动态 URL group

```
▼ ☁️ 动态网络壁纸                                          [+添加]
   ├─ [✓] 必应每日壁纸 (https://api.dujin.org/bing/1920.php)         ← 预设, 无删除
   ├─ [ ] 随机风景 (imgapi.cn)                                        ← 预设
   ├─ [ ] Unsplash 随机                                             ← 预设
   ├─ [✓] https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images    [🗑]    ← 自定义, 可删
   └─ [✓] https://example.com/myapi.php                     [🗑]    ← 自定义, 可删
```

**预设勾选逻辑**：勾选 → 将 URL 加入 `config.dynamicBgUrls`；取消 → 移除。立即 `configStore.save()`。

**自定义 URL 删除**：从 `config.dynamicBgUrls` splice，`configStore.save()`。如果该 URL 是当前背景，触发 `reselectBackground()`。

**`[+添加]` 按钮**：调用新增的 `showAddDynamicUrlDialog(onSuccess(url, isDynamic))`。

#### 7. UrlDialog 扩展（或新 Dialog）— 双模式 URL 输入

```
┌─ 添加网络背景资源 ────────────────────────────┐
│                                                │
│  输入图片 API 或文件 URL                        │
│  [https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing...   ] │
│                                                │
│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
│  │           🔄 检测中…                      │  │
│  │     或    [预览图]                        │  │
│  │     或    ⚠ URL 后缀不在支持的格式列表中   │  │
│  │     或    ⚠ 网络请求失败                  │  │
│  └──────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
│                                                │
│  检测结果: 🌐 动态图像源 (每次返回不同图片)     │
│                              [添加到订阅源]     │
└────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**自动类型判断逻辑**（`checkExt()` 扩展）：

| URL 后缀 | 判定 | 按钮文案 |
|----------|------|---------|
| `.jpg`, `.png`, `.webp` ... | 普通图片 | `上传到缓存` |
| `.mp4`, `.webm` ... | 普通视频 | `上传到缓存` |
| `.php`, 无后缀 ... | **动态源** | `添加到订阅源` |

#### 8. `ConfigTab.svelte` — 当前背景显示

```typescript
function formatCurrentFile(url: string | null): string {
    if (!url) return i18n.none
    if (!isDynamicUrl(url)) return url
    const preset = DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS.find(p => p.url === url)
    if (preset) return `🌐 ${preset.name}`
    const u = new URL(url)
    return `🌐 ${u.hostname}...`
}
```

```svelte
<code class="fn__code">{formatCurrentFile(currentFile)}</code>
```

#### 10. i18n 新增键（12个）

| 键 | 中文 | 用途 |
|----|------|------|
| `dynamicBgGroup` | 动态网络壁纸 | 新 group 标题 |
| `addDynamicUrl` | 添加订阅源 | [+添加] 按钮 |
| `addDynamicUrlTitle` | 添加动态背景源 | Dialog 标题 |
| `detectedDynamic` | 🌐 动态图像源（每次返回不同图片） | 检测结果 |
| `detectedUpload` | 📁 文件资源（下载并缓存到本地） | 检测结果 |
| `addToDynamic` | 添加到订阅源 | 按钮 (dynamic 模式) |
| `uploadToCache` | 上传到缓存 | 按钮 (upload 模式) |
| `dynamicUrlHint` | 输入图片 API 地址（每次返回不同图片） | 输入框 placeholder |
| `videoBgRecommend` | 视频背景素材推荐 | About 标题 |
| `videoBgRecommendDesc` | 动态订阅源仅支持图片… | About 说明 |
| `presetPrefix` | [预设] | 预设项前缀 |
| `refreshDynamicList` | 刷新订阅源列表 | tooltip |

```json
{
  "filePath": "/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/.agents/plans/20260519_dynamic-bg-url.md",
  "content": "# 动态订阅源功能实施计划\n\n> 创建于 2026-05-19 | 方案 A：直接 canvas URL + CSS 双层 fallback\n\n## 背景\n\n支持类似 `https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images` 的随机图片 API，每次返回不同背景图。\n\n## 设计决策\n\n| 决策 | 理由 |\n|------|------|\n| **跳过可达性检测** | 失败时 CSS fallback 自动兜底，无需预检+缓存基础设施 |\n| **直接插入 canvas CSS** | `canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url(...)` 而非下载到本地 |\n| **CSS 双层 background-image 做 fallback** | `url(dynamic), url(fallback)` — dynamic 失败自动暴露 fallback |\n| **缓存破坏** | 渲染时追加 `?_t=timestamp` |\n| **动态 URL 默认 image 类型** | 不存在返回视频的动态 API |\n| **混合预设+自定义** | 插件内置维护低频失效的预设，用户可添加自己的 URL |\n\n## UI 布局\n\n动态 URL group 放在 SourcesTab **最顶部**：\n\n```\n┌─ 数据源管理 ────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│                                                              │\n│  [+ 链接本地目录]  [+ 链接资源目录]                            │\n│                                                              │\n│  ▼ ☁️ 动态网络壁纸                                    [+添加]  │\n│     ├─ [✓] 必应每日壁纸 (https://api.dujin.org/bing/1920.php) │ ← 预设，无删除\n│     ├─ [ ] 随机风景 (imgapi.cn)                                │ ← 预设\n│     ├─ [ ] Unsplash 随机                                     │ ← 预设\n│     ├─ [✓] https://imgapi.cn/api.php?...            [🗑]      │ ← 自定义，可删\n│     └─ [✓] https://example.com/myapi.php           [🗑]      │ ← 自定义，可删\n│                                                              │\n│  ▼ 📦 Plugin Cache（云同步）              (Images:2 Videos:1) │\n│     ...                                                      │\n│  ▼ 📁 assets/...                                             │\n│     ...                                                      │\n```\n\n\n## 文件改动清单\n\n| # | 文件 | 操作 | 说明 |\n|---|------|------|------|\n| 1 | `src/types.ts` | 修改 | `sourceType` 联合添加 `'dynamic'` |\n| 2 | `src/constants.ts` | 修改 | `DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS` + `DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL` + `isDynamicUrl()` |\n| 3 | `src/stores/config.ts` | 修改 | `AppConfig` 新增 `dynamicBgUrls: string[]` |\n| 4 | `src/services/bgRender.ts` | 修改 | `render(forceType?)` + `renderDynamic(url, fallback)` |\n| 5 | `src/services/sourceManager.ts` | 修改 | `scanDynamicUrls()` + `scanAll` 含 dynamic + `getSourceLabel` |\n| 6 | `src/index.ts` | 修改 | `randomSelect` / `applyBackground` 处理 dynamic 分支 |\n| 7 | `src/ui/settings/SourcesTab.svelte` | 修改 | 顶部新增动态 URL group（预设 checkbox + [+添加] + 自定义删除） |\n| 8 | `src/ui/settings/ConfigTab.svelte` | 修改 | `currentFile` 对 dynamic URL 格式化显示（预设名/域名截断） |\n| 9 | `src/ui/settings/AboutTab.svelte` | 修改 | 视频背景素材站推荐 |\n| 10 | `src/ui/dialogs/index.ts` | 修改 | 新增 `showAddDynamicUrlDialog()` |\n| 11 | `public/i18n/zh_CN.json` | 修改 | ~12 新键 |\n| 12 | `public/i18n/en_US.json` | 修改 | ~12 新键 |\n\n\n## 详细设计\n\n### 1. `src/types.ts`\n\n```typescript\nexport interface ImageItem {\n    name: string\n    url: string\n    apiPath: string\n    type: 'image' | 'video'\n    sourceType: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets' | 'dynamic'  // 新增 'dynamic'\n    sourceLabel: string\n}\n```\n\n### 2. `src/constants.ts`\n\n```typescript\nexport const DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS: { id: string; name: string; url: string }[] = [\n    { id: 'bing_1920',     name: '必应每日壁纸',          url: 'https://api.dujin.org/bing/1920.php' },\n    { id: 'imgapi_scenic', name: '随机风景 (imgapi.cn)',  url: 'https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images' },\n    { id: 'unsplash_rand', name: 'Unsplash 随机',         url: 'https://source.unsplash.com/random/1920x1080' },\n]\n\nexport const DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL = DEFAULT_BACKGROUNDS[1]\n// plugins/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/default/FyBE0bUakAELfeF.jpg\n\n/**\n * 判断 URL 是否为动态源（无已知图片/视频后缀且是 http 开头）\n */\nexport function isDynamicUrl(url: string): boolean {\n    const clean = url.split('?')[0]\n    const ext = '.' + (clean.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')\n    return !IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext) && !VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext) && url.startsWith('http')\n}\n```\n\n### 3. `src/stores/config.ts`\n\n```typescript\nconst APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS: AppConfig = {\n    // ...existing...\n    dynamicBgUrls: [],\n}\n```\n\n### 4. `src/services/bgRender.ts`\n\n```typescript\n// ① render() 接受可选类型强制\nexport function render(url: string, forceType?: 'image' | 'video'): void {\n    const type = forceType ?? detectType(url)\n    if (type === 'image') renderImage(url)\n    else if (type === 'video') renderVideo(url)\n}\n\n// ② CSS 双层 background-image 实现自动 fallback\nexport function renderDynamic(url: string, fallbackUrl: string): void {\n    if (!canvasEl) return\n    if (videoEl) {\n        videoEl.style.display = 'none'\n        try { videoEl.pause() } catch { /* ignored */ }\n        videoEl.removeAttribute('src')\n    }\n    currentMode = 'image'\n    canvasEl.style.display = ''\n    canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}'), url('${fallbackUrl}')`\n    canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover, cover'\n}\n```\n\n### 5. `src/services/sourceManager.ts`\n\n```typescript\nexport async function scanAll(\n    assetDirs: string[] = [],\n    localFolders: string[] = [],\n    dynamicBgUrls: string[] = [],   // 新增参数\n): Promise<ImageItem[]> {\n    const tasks: Promise<ImageItem[]>[] = [\n        scanSource('upload', pluginAssetsDir),\n        scanDynamicUrls(dynamicBgUrls),   // 新增\n    ]\n    const validAssetDirs = assetDirs.filter(d => d.length > 0)\n        .map(dir => {\n            const normalized = toAssetRelPath(dir)\n            return `/data/${normalized}`\n        })\n    tasks.push(...validAssetDirs.map(path => scanSource('assets', path + '/')))\n    // ...local folder logic...\n    const batch = await Promise.all(tasks)\n    return batch.flat()\n}\n\nexport function scanDynamicUrls(urls: string[]): ImageItem[] {\n    return urls.map(url => {\n        const preset = DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS.find(p => p.url === url)\n        return {\n            name: preset?.name ?? new URL(url).hostname,\n            url,\n            apiPath: url,            // 无本地路径，用 URL 本身\n            type: 'image' as const,\n            sourceType: 'dynamic' as const,\n            sourceLabel: 'dynamic',\n        }\n    })\n}\n\n// getSourceLabel 新增 case\nfunction getSourceLabel(type: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets' | 'dynamic', path: string): string {\n    switch (type) {\n        case 'dynamic':\n            return 'dynamic'\n        // ...existing cases...\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 6. `src/index.ts`\n\n**randomSelect** — 纳入 dynamic URLs 到随机池：\n\n```typescript\nasync randomSelect() {\n    const assetDirs = configStore.get(\"assetDirs\")\n    const localFolders = configStore.get(\"localFolders\")\n    const dynamicBgUrls = configStore.get(\"dynamicBgUrls\")  // 新增\n    const pool = await scanAll(assetDirs, localFolders, dynamicBgUrls)\n    if (pool.length === 0) return\n    const exclude = pool.length > 1 ? configStore.get(\"currentFile\") : null\n    const item = pickRandom(pool, exclude)\n    if (!item) return\n\n    configStore.set(\"currentFile\", item.url)\n    configStore.save()\n\n    if (item.sourceType === 'dynamic') {\n        const cb = item.url + (item.url.includes('?') ? '&' : '?') + '_t=' + Date.now()\n        renderDynamic(cb, DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL)\n    } else if (item.type === 'image') {\n        renderImage(item.url)\n    } else {\n        renderVideo(item.url)\n    }\n    changeOpacity(configStore.get(\"opacity\"))\n    changeBlur(configStore.get(\"blur\"))\n    changePosition(configStore.get(\"positionX\"), configStore.get(\"positionY\"))\n}\n```\n\n**applyBackground** — 处理无后缀的 dynamic URL：\n\n```typescript\nprivate applyBackground() {\n    try {\n        const currentFile = configStore.get(\"currentFile\")\n        if (!currentFile) return\n\n        // 优先判断动态 URL\n        if (isDynamicUrl(currentFile)) {\n            const cb = currentFile + (currentFile.includes('?') ? '&' : '?') + '_t=' + Date.now()\n            renderDynamic(cb, DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL)\n        } else {\n            const ext = '.' + (currentFile.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')\n            if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) {\n                renderVideo(currentFile)\n            } else if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext)) {\n                renderImage(currentFile)\n            } else {\n                console.warn(`[bgCover] applyBackground: unknown extension \"${ext}\" for ${currentFile}`)\n                return\n            }\n        }\n    } finally {\n        // opacity, blur, position...\n    }\n    // autoRefresh timer...\n}\n```\n\n**onload** — 初始化扫描包含 dynamic：\n\n```typescript\n// onload 中 scanAll 调用\nconst dynamicBgUrls = configStore.get(\"dynamicBgUrls\")\nconst pool `UrlDialog.svelte` 或新建 `DynamicUrlDialog.svelte`。扩展现有 `showUrlDialog` 为双模式：\n\n```typescript\nimport DynamicUrlDialog from './DynamicUrlDialog.svelte'\n\nexport function |\n|-------------|------|---------|\n| `.jpg`, `.png`, `.webp` ... | 普通图片 → upload | `📁 文件资源（下载并缓存到本地）` |\n| `.mp4`, `.webm` ... | 普通视频 → upload | `📁 文件资源（下载并缓存到本地）` |\n| `.php`, 无后缀 ... | **动态源** → dynamic | `🌐 动态图像源（每次返回不同图片）` |\n\n```typescript\nfunction classifyUrlType(ext: string): 'upload' | 'dynamic' {\n    if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext) || VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) return 'upload'\n    return 'dynamic'\n}\n```\n\n### 11. i18n 新增键\n\n| 键 | 中文 | 英文 | 用途 |\n|----|------|------|------|\n| `dynamicBgGroup` | 动态网络壁纸 | Dynamic Web Wallpaper | group 标题 |\n| `addDynamicUrl` | 添加订阅源 | Add Feed | `videoBgRecommendDesc` | 动态订阅源仅支持图片背景。如需视频背景，请从以下网站下载后通过本地上传添加。 | Dynamic feeds support images only. For video backgrounds, download from these sites and add via local upload. | About 说明 |\n| `presetPrefix` | [预设] | [Preset] | 预设项名称前缀 |\n| `removeDynamic` | 移除订阅源 | Remove Feed | 删除 tooltip |\n\n\n## 验证清单\n\n- [ ] 勾选预设 → `dynamicBgUrls` 写入 config，`save()`\n- [ ] 取消勾选预设 → 从 `dynamicBgUrls` 移除\n- [ ] 点击 [+添加] → Dialog 弹出，输入 URL → fetch 检测 → 后缀自动分类\n- [ ] 无后缀 URL → 判定为 dynamic，按钮为「添加到订阅源」\n- [ ] 有图片后缀 URL → 判定为 upload，按钮为「上传到缓存」\n- [ ] 有视频后缀 URL → 判定为 upload，按钮为「上传到缓存」\n- [ ] URL 不可达 → 添加按钮禁用，显示错误信息\n- [ ] 自定义 URL 添加成功 → 出现在 dynamic group 列表中\n- [ ] 自定义 URL 删除 → 从 `dynamicBgUrls` 移除，若为当前背景则触发 reselect\n- [ ] `随机抽一张` → dynamic URL 入选随机池，选中后 cache-bust 渲染\n- [ ] 动态 URL 加载成功 → canvas 显示图片\n- [ ] 动态 URL 加载失败 → CSS fallback 自动显示默认背景图\n- [ ] 关闭再打开背景 → `applyBackground()` 正确识别 dynamic URL 并渲染\n- [ ] 启动时 `changeBgOnStart` → dynamic URL 参与随机，正确渲染\n- [ ] ConfigTab 当前背景 → dynamic URL 显示为预设名或截断域名\n- [ ] AboutTab → 显示视频素材站推荐列表\n- [ ] i18n 中英文切换正常\n- [ ] 预设项无删除按钮（仅 checkbox），自定义 URL 有删除按钮\n- [ ] 删除预设的最后一个\"自定义URL\"后，group 仍可见（预设列表存在）\n\n\n## 禁止事项\n\n- ❌ 不做批量可达性检测和本地缓存\n- ❌ 不支持视频动态 URL\n- ❌ 预设 URL 不提供删除按钮\n- ❌ 不硬编码中文文本（全部走 i18n 键）\n- ❌ 不使用 `createObjectURL` 做缩略图预览\n- ❌ 不在 `for...of` 中串行 `await` 扫描\n"

https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images 这种地址，输入会自动跳转  https://i.33xp.cn/__imgapi.cn__/__imgapi.cn__5cc80efda17d7.jpg， 这种情况是否可以正确处理？

### 🤖 Assistant
*2026-05-19 14:16:11*

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

The user is pointing out that some dynamic image APIs don't return the image directly at the given URL, but instead redirect (HTTP 302) to the actual image URL. For example:

- Input: `https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images`
- Redirects to: `https://i.33xp.cn/__imgapi.cn__/__imgapi.cn__5cc80efda17d7.jpg`

This raises several questions about how our Plan A (direct canvas URL) would handle this:

1. **CSS `background-image: url(...)`**: When the browser loads a CSS `url()`, it follows redirects automatically. So if we set `canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url('https://imgapi.cn/api.php?...?_t=12345')`, the browser will follow the 302 redirect and load the redirected image. This should work fine for CSS.

2. **Cache-busting**: The `?_t=timestamp` parameter is appended to the original URL. The redirect target might have its own query parameters or different behavior. But since the browser follows redirects transparently, the cache-busting should still work - the browser treats the original URL (with `_t`) as a new request each time.

3. **detectType / isDynamicUrl**: The original URL `https://imgapi.cn/api.php?...` has `.php` extension, which is correctly classified as dynamic. This works fine.

4. **The issue in UrlDialog**: Looking at the current `UrlDialog.svelte`, it does `fetch(trimmed)` which by default follows redirects (`redirect: 'follow'`). So the content-type check would work - it would get the redirected response with `content-type: image/jpeg`.

5. **However**: After `fetch()` follows the redirect, `response.url` changes to the final URL. But we're storing the original URL in config, not the redirected one. This is correct behavior - we want to re-fetch from the original URL each time so we get different images.

So the redirect case should work fine with Plan A. The browser handles redirects transparently for both CSS `url()` and `fetch()`.

But wait, let me think about potential issues:

1. **Mixed content**: If the original URL is HTTPS but redirects to HTTP, the browser might block it. Similarly, if the original is HTTP and the page is HTTPS. This depends on the specific APIs and the user's environment.

2. **Cross-origin redirects**: CSS `background-image` doesn't have CORS restrictions, so this should be fine.

3. **Redirect loops**: Theoretically possible but unlikely with these APIs.

4. **Performance**: Each redirect adds latency. Not a significant issue for background images.

5. **The UrlDialog detection**: When the user enters `https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images` in the dialog:
   - `checkExt()` strips `?` → gets `.php` → not in IMAGE_EXTS/VIDEO_EXTS
   - In our new dual-mode logic, this would be classified as `dynamic`
   - Then we do `fetch()` to check reachability → follows redirect → gets image response → confirms it's reachable
   - This should work correctly

So the answer is: **yes, redirects are handled correctly by both CSS rendering and the dialog's reachability check, without any special code**.

The only edge case to consider: if the redirect chain is very long or involves authentication, it might fail. But this is rare for public image APIs.

Let me also think about whether there's any issue with the canvas background-image approach specifically for redirect URLs:

- CSS `url()` in `background-image`: Browser follows redirects natively. ✅
- Cache-busting with `?_t=timestamp`: Works because it changes the original request URL. ✅
- Fallback with double-layer: If redirect fails, fallback shows. ✅

I should also consider: what if the redirect goes to a URL that has a known image extension? For example, redirect from `api.php` to `image.jpg`. The browser and CSS handle this fine - the extension of the redirect source doesn't matter, only the final content.

So my answer is: redirects are handled correctly, no code changes needed. The only thing to verify is that the `UrlDialog`'s `doCheck()` function properly follows redirects (it does, by default fetch follows redirects).

Let me present this analysis clearly.

</details>

重定向情况完全可以正确处理，不需要额外代码。

## 分析

### CSS `background-image` 层

```
canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url('https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images?_t=12345')
                                    │
                                    ▼ 浏览器原生 302 跟随
                  https://i.33xp.cn/__imgapi.cn__/__imgapi.cn__5cc80efda17d7.jpg
                                    │
                                    ▼ 加载成功 → 渲染
                                    ▼ 加载失败 → fallback Layer 2 自动暴露
```

CSS `url()` 由浏览器引擎处理，**302 重定向透明跟随**，不需要任何 JS 介入。

### Dialog 检测层

当前 `UrlDialog.svelte:44` 的 `fetch(trimmed)` 默认 `redirect: 'follow'`：

```typescript
const resp = await fetch(trimmed)     // 自动跟随 302
const contentType = resp.headers.get('content-type')  // → 'image/jpeg'
```

实际拿到的是重定向后的图片响应，`content-type` 检查正常通过。

### 后缀判定

```
checkExt('https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images')
  → 去 ? 后 → 'https://imgapi.cn/api.php'
  → 后缀 → '.php'
  → 不在 IMAGE_EXTS/VIDEO_EXTS → 判定为 dynamic ✅
```

### cache-busting 仍然有效

`?_t=1234567890` 加在原始 URL 上，浏览器对不同的 `_t` 值发起新请求，每次都会走一遍 302 重定向链到不同图片。

---

**结论：重定向是浏览器的内置能力，CSS `url()` 和 `fetch()` 都原生处理，不需要额外代码。**

5: ## 背景
6: 
7: 支持类似 `https://imgapi.cn/api.php?fl=fengjing&gs=images` 的随机图片 API，每次返回不同背景图。

9: ## 设计决策
10: 
11: | 决策 | 理由 |
12: |------|------|
13: | **跳过可达性检测** | 失败时 CSS fallback 自动兜底，无需预检+缓存基础设施 |
14: | **直接插入 canvas CSS** | `canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url(...)` 而非下载到本地 |
15: | **CSS 双层 background-image 做 fallback** | `url(dynamic), url(fallback)` — dynamic 失败自动暴露 fallback |
16: | **缓存破坏** | 渲染时追加 `?_t=timestamp` |
17: | **动态 URL 默认 image 类型** | 不存在返回视频的动态 API |
18: | **混合预设+自定义** | 插件内置维护低频失效的预设，用户可添加自己的 URL |

89: export const DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL = "plugins/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/default/404.jpg"
90: 
91: /**
92:  * 判断 URL 是否为动态源（无已知图片/视频后缀且是 http 开头）
93:  */
94: export function isDynamicUrl(url: string): boolean {
95:     const clean = url.split('?')[0]
96:     const ext = '.' + (clean.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
97:     return !IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext) && !VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext) && url.startsWith('http')
98: }
99: ```

110: ### 4. `src/services/bgRender.ts`
111: 
112: ```typescript
113: // ① render() 接受可选类型强制
114: export function render(url: string, forceType?: 'image' | 'video'): void {
115:     const type = forceType ?? detectType(url)
116:     if (type === 'image') renderImage(url)
117:     else if (type === 'video') renderVideo(url)
118: }
119: 
120: // ② CSS 双层 background-image 实现自动 fallback
121: export function renderDynamic(url: string, fallbackUrl: string): void {
122:     if (!canvasEl) return
123:     if (videoEl) {
124:         videoEl.style.display = 'none'
125:         try { videoEl.pause() } catch { /* ignored */ }
126:         videoEl.removeAttribute('src')
127:     }
128:     currentMode = 'image'
129:     canvasEl.style.display = ''
130:     canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}'), url('${fallbackUrl}')`
131:     canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover, cover'
132: }
133: ```
134: 
135: ### 5. `src/services/sourceManager.ts`
136: 
137: ```typescript
138: export async function scanAll(
139:     assetDirs: string[] = [],
140:     localFolders: string[] = [],
141:     dynamicBgUrls: string[] = [],   // 新增参数
142: ): Promise<ImageItem[]> {
143:     const tasks: Promise<ImageItem[]>[] = [
144:         scanSource('upload', pluginAssetsDir),
145:         scanDynamicUrls(dynamicBgUrls),   // 新增
146:     ]
147:     const validAssetDirs = assetDirs.filter(d => d.length > 0)
148:         .map(dir => {
149:             const normalized = toAssetRelPath(dir)
150:             return `/data/${normalized}`
151:         })
152:     tasks.push(...validAssetDirs.map(path => scanSource('assets', path + '/')))
153:     // ...local folder logic...
154:     const batch = await Promise.all(tasks)
155:     return batch.flat()
156: }
157: 
158: export function scanDynamicUrls(urls: string[]): ImageItem[] {
159:     return urls.map(url => {
160:         const preset = DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS.find(p => p.url === url)
161:         return {
162:             name: preset?.name ?? new URL(url).hostname,
163:             url,
164:             apiPath: url,            // 无本地路径，用 URL 本身
165:             type: 'image' as const,
166:             sourceType: 'dynamic' as const,
167:             sourceLabel: 'dynamic',
168:         }
169:     })
170: }
171: 
172: // getSourceLabel 新增 case
173: function getSourceLabel(type: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets' | 'dynamic', path: string): string {
174:     switch (type) {
175:         case 'dynamic':
176:             return 'dynamic'
177:         // ...existing cases...
178:     }
179: }
180: ```
181: 
182: ### 6. `src/index.ts`
183: 
184: **randomSelect** — 纳入 dynamic URLs 到随机池：
185: 
186: ```typescript
187: async randomSelect() {
188:     const assetDirs = configStore.get("assetDirs")
189:     const localFolders = configStore.get("localFolders")
190:     const dynamicBgUrls = configStore.get("dynamicBgUrls")  // 新增
191:     const pool = await scanAll(assetDirs, localFolders, dynamicBgUrls)
192:     if (pool.length === 0) return
193:     const exclude = pool.length > 1 ? configStore.get("currentFile") : null
194:     const item = pickRandom(pool, exclude)
195:     if (!item) return
196: 
197:     configStore.set("currentFile", item.url)
198:     configStore.save()
199: 
200:     if (item.sourceType === 'dynamic') {
201:         const cb = item.url + (item.url.includes('?') ? '&' : '?') + '_t=' + Date.now()
202:         renderDynamic(cb, DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL)
203:     } else if (item.type === 'image') {
204:         renderImage(item.url)
205:     } else {
206:         renderVideo(item.url)
207:     }
208:     changeOpacity(configStore.get("opacity"))
209:     changeBlur(configStore.get("blur"))
210:     changePosition(configStore.get("positionX"), configStore.get("positionY"))
211: }
212: ```
213: 
214: **applyBackground** — 处理无后缀的 dynamic URL：
215: 
216: ```typescript
217: private applyBackground() {
218:     try {
219:         const currentFile = configStore.get("currentFile")
220:         if (!currentFile) return
221: 
222:         // 优先判断动态 URL
223:         if (isDynamicUrl(currentFile)) {
224:             const cb = currentFile + (currentFile.includes('?') ? '&' : '?') + '_t=' + Date.now()
225:             renderDynamic(cb, DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL)
226:         } else {
227:             const ext = '.' + (currentFile.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
228:             if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) {
229:                 renderVideo(currentFile)
230:             } else if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext)) {
231:                 renderImage(currentFile)
232:             } else {
233:                 console.warn(`[bgCover] applyBackground: unknown extension "${ext}" for ${currentFile}`)
234:                 return
235:             }
236:         }
237:     } finally {
238:         // opacity, blur, position...
239:     }
240:     // autoRefresh timer...
241: }
242: ```
243: 
244: **onload** — 初始化扫描包含 dynamic：
245: 
246: ```typescript
247: // onload 中 scanAll 调用
248: const dynamicBgUrls = configStore.get("dynamicBgUrls")
249: const pool = await scanAll(assetDirs, localFolders, dynamicBgUrls)
250: ```

256: ```svelte

259:     import { renderDynamic } from "../../services/bgRender"
260: 
261:     // 动态订阅源相关状态

263:

265:         if (dynamicUrls.includes(url)) {
266:             dynamicUrls = dynamicUrls.filter(u => u !== url)
267:         } else {
268:             dynamicUrls = [...dynamicUrls, url]
269:         }

273:         refreshAll()

277:         return DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS.some(p => p.url === url)
278:     }
279:

281:         dynamicUrls = dynamicUrls.filter(u => u !== url)

294:                 refreshAll()

440: 
441: **自动类型判断**（`UrlDialog.svelte` 中 `checkExt` 扩展）：
442: 
443: | URL 后缀模式 | 判定 | 结果标签 |
444: |-------------|------|---------|
445: | `.jpg`, `.png`, `.webp` ... | 普通图片 → upload | `📁 文件资源（下载并缓存到本地）` |
446: | `.mp4`, `.webm` ... | 普通视频 → upload | `📁 文件资源（下载并缓存到本地）` |
447: | `.php`, 无后缀 ... | **动态源** → dynamic | `🌐 动态图像源（每次返回不同图片）` |
448: 
449: ```typescript
450: function classifyUrlType(ext: string): 'upload' | 'dynamic' {
451:     if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext) || VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) return 'upload'
452:     return 'dynamic'
453: }
454: ```

```typescript

    `plugins/${packageName}/default/av71658201.mp4`,
    `plugins/${packageName}/default/FyBE0bUakAELfeF.jpg`,
]
```

These paths are served by SiYuan at `plugins/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/default/FyBE0bUakAELfeF.jpg`. The 404.jpg is in the same directory, so the path `plugins/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/default/404.jpg` will work.

24: function siyuanApiPost<T = any>(url: string, data?: any): Promise<T> {
25:     return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
26:         fetchPost(url, data ?? {}, (response: any) => {
27:             if (response.code === 0) {
28:                 resolve(response.data)
29:             } else {
30:                 reject(new Error(response.msg ?? "fetchPost failed"))
31:             }
32:         })
33:     })
34: }

36: class ConfigStore {
37:     private cfg: AppConfig = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS }
38:     private dirty = false
39:     private ready = false
40: 
41:     async load(): Promise<void> {
42:         if (this.ready) return
43: 
44:         let stored: any = (window as any).siyuan?.storage?.[STORAGE_KEY]
45: 
46:         if (stored === undefined || stored === null) {
47:             try {
48:                 const all = await siyuanApiPost<Record<string, any>>("/api/storage/getLocalStorage")
49:                 stored = all?.[STORAGE_KEY] ?? {}
50:             } catch {
51:                 stored = {}
52:             }
53:         }
54: 
55:         this.cfg = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS, ...stored }
56:         devLog("[bgCover] config loaded, keys:", Object.keys(this.cfg))
57:         this.ready = true
58:     }
59: 
60:     async save(): Promise<void> {
61:         if (!this.dirty || !this.ready) return
62:         devLog("[bgCover] config save")
63:         await siyuanApiPost("/api/storage/setLocalStorageVal", {
64:             key: STORAGE_KEY,
65:             val: this.cfg,
66:         })
67:         this.dirty = false
68:     }

76:         this.dirty = true
77:     }
78: 
79:     async setAndSave<K extends keyof AppConfig>(key: K, value: AppConfig[K]): Promise<void> {
80:         this.set(key, value)
81:         await this.save()
82:     }
83:

85:         return { ...this.cfg }

117:             await siyuanApiPost("/api/storage/removeLocalStorageVals", { keys: [STORAGE_KEY] })
118:             this.cfg = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS }
119:             return

128:                 await siyuanApiPost("/api/file/removeFile", { path: `/data/storage/petal/${STORAGE_KEY}/` })

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

Now I need to make sure renderImage also resets backgroundSize when switching from dynamic back to regular image. The current renderImage sets `canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url('${url}')` but doesn't set backgroundSize. However, renderDynamic sets `backgroundSize = 'cover, cover'`. When switching from dynamic to regular, we need to reset backgroundSize to 'cover'.

Let me check the current renderImage code... It sets backgroundImage but doesn't touch backgroundSize. The initial `createBgLayer()` sets `backgroundSize = 'cover'` once. So when switching:
1. Start → renderImage(path/to/file.jpg) → backgroundImage updated, backgroundSize stays 'cover' (from createBgLayer) ✅
2. renderDynamic(url, fallback) → sets backgroundSize to 'cover, cover' 
3. Switch back to renderImage → backgroundImage updated to single url, but backgroundSize stays 'cover, cover' ❌

I need to fix renderImage to also reset backgroundSize.

</details>

`renderImage()` 需要恢复 `backgroundSize` 为单层 `cover`，否则从 dynamic 切换回来时会有残余的 `cover, cover`。

'')\n        return IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext) || VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext) ? ''\n            if (contentType.startsWith('image/')) {\n                if (urlType === 'upload') {\n                    const blob = await resp.blob()\n                    if (blobUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(blobUrl)\n                    blobUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob)\n                    previewSrc = blobUrl\n                    validExt = true\n                } else {\n                    isDynamic = true\n                    const blob = await resp.blob()\n                    if (blobUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(blobUrl)\n                    blobUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob)\n                    previewSrc = blobUrl\n                }\n            } else if (contentType.startsWith('video/')) {\n                if (urlType === 'upload') {\n                    validExt = true\n                } else {\n                    errorMsg = i18n.notImageOrVideo\n                }\n            } else {\n                errorMsg = i18n.notImageOrVideo\n            }\n        } catch {\n            errorMsg = i18n.networkFailed\n        }\n        checking = false\n    }\n\n    function handleInput() {\n        const trimmed = url.trim()\n        if (!trimmed) {\n            validExt = false\n            isDynamic = false\n            errorMsg = \"\"\n            previewSrc = null\n            return\n        }\n        if (debounceTimer) clearTimeout(debounceTimer)\n        debounceTimer = setTimeout(() => doCheck(trimmed), 500)\n    }\n\n    async function handleUpload() {\n        const trimmed = url.trim()\n        if (!trimmed || !validExt) return\n\n        const fileName = trimmed.split('/').pop()?.split('?')[0] ?? 'download'\n        const destPath = `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${fileName}`\n\n        const ok = await downloadUrl(trimmed, destPath)\n        if (ok) {\n            const renderingUrl = getFileUrl(`/data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${fileName}`, 'upload')\n            onSuccess?.(renderingUrl)\n        }\n    }\n\n    function handleDynamicAdd() {\n        const trimmed = url.trim()\n        if (!trimmed || !isDynamic) return\n        onDynamicAdd?.(trimmed)\n    }\n\n    function getFileName(): string {\n        return url.trim().split('/').pop()?.split('?')[0] ?? ''\n    }\n\n    function canConfirm(): boolean {\n        return validExt || isDynamic\n    }\n\n    onDestroy(() => {\n        if (blobUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(blobUrl)\n    })\n</script>"

4. Another possibility: the site might have HTTP redirects or require specific headers. CSS `background-image` doesn't handle redirects the same way as browser navigation.

5. Or it could be that the response is something like a redirect that doesn't work well in CSS background-image context (e.g., the server returns a non-image content-type, or something else).

6. Wait - another possibility: the response might be JSON or HTML that redirects to an image URL, which CSS url() can't follow. Some random image APIs return a redirect or an HTML page that loads the image.

1. CORS/CSP blocking in the Electron webview
2. The server returns a redirect that CSS can't follow
3. Mixed content (HTTP vs HTTPS)
4. The server blocks referrer-based loading
5. The response is not actually a direct image

```html
<canvas id="bglayer" style="background-image: url("https://img.xjh.me/random_img.php?_t=1779157053361"), url("plugins/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/default/404.jpg"); background-size: cover, cover; ...">
```

Wait - there's a potential issue with the quotes! The style attribute uses `"` for the attribute value, and inside `url()`, the URL is also quoted with `"`. This creates a parsing issue:

```
style="background-image: url("https://..."), url("plugins/..."); ..."
                              ^            ^
```

The browser parser sees: style attribute starts with `"`, then `url(` then `"` which closes the style attribute. The rest is garbage.

But actually, the user's output shows `&quot;` which is the HTML-encoded form. So the DOM inspector shows `url(&quot;...&quot;)`. This is likely just the inspector display format. The actual DOM style property set by JavaScript doesn't have this issue since `canvasEl.style.backgroundImage` is set directly (not via HTML attribute).

### 🤖 Assistant
*2026-05-19 14:16:11*

*[step-start part]*

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

The user is asking if it's possible to parse HTML pages returned by some of these URLs and extract the `<img>` tag's `src` attribute to use as the actual background image.

Let me think about this:

1. `img.xjh.me/random_img.php` returns HTML with `<img alt="..." src="//img.xjh.me/img/63190664_p0.jpg">`
2. `acg.sx/images` returns an HTML gallery page

Could we fetch the HTML, parse it, extract the `<img>` src, and then use THAT URL as the background?

Technically, yes:
1. `fetch(url)` → get HTML
2. Parse with DOMParser → extract `img[src]`
3. Use the extracted src URL as the dynamic background URL

But there are complications:

1. **Different HTML structures**: Each site has different HTML. `img.xjh.me` has a bare `<img>` tag. `acg.sx` has a complex gallery page with multiple images. We'd need site-specific parsers.

2. **Relative URLs**: The `src` might be `//img.xjh.me/img/63190664_p0.jpg` (protocol-relative), `/img/foo.jpg` (root-relative), or `../img/foo.jpg` (relative). We'd need to resolve them against the base URL.

3. **Fragility**: If the site changes its HTML structure, the parser breaks silently.

4. **Performance**: Extra fetch + parse step per background change.

5. **CORS**: The fetch for the HTML page should work (since these are open APIs), but then we'd use a different URL for the actual image in CSS background-image.

The approach would be:
1. For presets that are known to return HTML, add a `parser: 'html-img'` or similar config
2. `fetch()` the URL
3. `new DOMParser().parseFromString(html, 'text/html')`
4. Query `document.querySelector('img')` or a site-specific selector
5. Extract `src`, resolve it to absolute URL
6. Use that URL (with cache-busting) as the CSS background-image

This is getting complex. A simpler approach might be:
- Just remove HTML-returning URLs from presets (which we already did)
- If the user really wants img.xjh.me, they can find the actual image URL pattern directly

But the user is asking about a more general solution. Let me think about this...

Actually, for these specific sites:
- `img.xjh.me/random_img.php` → returns a single `<img>` tag pointing to a random image
- The actual image pattern seems to be `//img.xjh.me/img/{random_id}.jpg`

For `acg.sx` - this is a full website, not just a random image API. This shouldn't be supported.

For the general case, we could add a `urlType` field to presets:
```typescript
{ id: '...', name: '...', url: '...', type: 'direct' | 'html-img' }
```

But this adds complexity. Let me think about whether it's worth it.

Actually, a simpler approach: we could try to fetch the URL and detect if it returns HTML. If so, try to extract an `<img>` tag and use its `src`. This would work generically without site-specific config.

```typescript
async function resolveImageUrl(url: string): Promise<string | null> {
    const resp = await fetch(url)
    const ct = resp.headers.get('content-type') ?? ''
    if (ct.startsWith('image/')) return url // already an image
    
    if (ct.includes('html')) {
        const html = await resp.text()
        const doc = new DOMParser().parseFromString(html, 'text/html')
        const img = doc.querySelector('img')
        if (img) {
            const src = img.getAttribute('src')
            if (src) return new URL(src, url).href
        }
    }
    return null
}
```

But wait - this changes the architecture. Currently, for dynamic URLs, we set the CSS background-image directly. If we need to fetch + parse HTML first, this becomes async and can't be done in the CSS setter.

We'd need to change the flow for these types of URLs:
1. In `randomSelect()`, when picking a dynamic URL
2. Fetch the URL first
3. If it returns image → use directly
4. If it returns HTML → parse, extract img src, use that
5. Then render with the resolved URL

This would work but adds latency to the background change (a network round-trip before rendering).

Also, we'd need to distinguish between direct-image URLs and HTML-returning URLs in the preset config, or do auto-detection.

**My recommendation:**

For presets, just use URLs that return actual images. Sites that return HTML wrappers aren't suitable for CSS background-image. We already removed the broken ones.

If the user specifically wants `img.xjh.me`, we could:
1. Add it back with a `resolveHtml` flag
2. In the render flow, fetch the HTML, extract the img src, use the resolved URL

But this adds significant complexity for one site that's already somewhat unreliable. The 4 remaining presets all work directly.

Actually, let me think about an even simpler approach: just use a `<img>` element for dynamic URLs instead of CSS background-image. An `<img>` element has `onerror` and we could handle HTML parsing in a pre-fetch step.

Wait no, the whole point of the canvas approach is for CSS styling (cover, position, blur, etc.). Using an `<img>` element would need different styling.

Let me just present the analysis to the user:
- Technically possible but adds complexity
- Each site has different HTML structure (fragile)
- Adds latency (extra network round-trip)
- Better to just use URLs that return direct images
- If a specific HTML-wrapper site is important, we could add site-specific resolvers as a separate feature

I should present this concisely.

</details>

技术上可行，但不推荐。

## 可行性分析

```typescript
// 通用方案：fetch → DOMParser → 提取 img src → 用提取的 URL 渲染
async function resolveImgFromHtml(pageUrl: string): Promise<string | null> {
    const resp = await fetch(pageUrl)
    const ct = resp.headers.get('content-type') ?? ''
    if (ct.startsWith('image/')) return pageUrl            // 直接是图
    if (!ct.includes('html')) return null
    const doc = new DOMParser().parseFromString(await resp.text(), 'text/html')
    const img = doc.querySelector('img')
    const src = img?.getAttribute('src')
    return src ? new URL(src, pageUrl).href : null         // 解析相对路径
}
```

## 不推荐的原因

| 问题 | 说明 |
|------|------|
| **HTML 结构各异** | `img.xjh.me` 是裸 `<img>`，`acg.sx` 是复杂画廊页，每个站解析规则不同 |
| **脆弱** | 站点改 HTML 结构 → 静默失效，用户不知道原因 |
| **延迟** | 每次切换背景多一次网络往返（fetch HTML → 解析 → 再 fetch 图片） |
| **复杂度** | 需要在 preset 上加 `type: 'html'` 标记，渲染流程分支增加 |
| **收益低** | `img.xjh.me` 等效于 `//img.xjh.me/img/{id}.jpg` 的 wrapper，本质也是静态图 |

## 结论

保留现有策略——预设只收录返回裸图片的 API。HTML wrapper 类型的站点应该找到其底层图片链接模式直接使用，或由用户下载到本地添加。

当前的 4 个预设（必应×2、Unsplash、imgapi）全部返回 `image/jpeg`，无需解析。

```

The `name` field is used in:
1. `SourceTab.svelte` - displayed in the preset list
2. `ConfigTab.svelte` - `formatCurrentFile()` shows preset name
3. `sourceManager.ts` - `scanDynamicUrls()` uses preset name for `ImageItem.name`

Since `constants.ts` is imported at module level and i18n comes from `window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n` which is set at runtime, we can't access i18n at module level.

Solutions:
A. Store i18n keys instead of display names, resolve at usage point
B. Use `id` as the i18n key, lookup in components
C. Add a lookup function that takes i18n object

Best approach: Store i18n keys in presets, and create a `getPresetDisplayName(preset, i18n)` helper.

```typescript
// constants.ts
export const DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS = [
    { id: 'bing_1920', nameKey: 'presetBing1920', url: '...' },
    ...
]
```

Then in each usage point, resolve the display name via i18n.

Wait, but `sourceManager.ts` also uses the name for `ImageItem.name`. sourceManager doesn't have access to i18n either. 

Alternative: Keep the `name` field as a fallback in constants, but if i18n is available, use that. Or better: in sourceManager, just use the URL as name (like for custom URLs), and in UI components, resolve the display name using i18n.

Actually, looking at how it works:
- `scanDynamicUrls()` creates `ImageItem` with `name` from preset
- `ImageItem.name` is displayed in the random select log: `devLog("[bgCover] randomSelect: picked", item.name, ...)`
- In `SourcesTab.svelte`, preset names are displayed directly from `preset.name` (from constants), not from ImageItem

So the name in ImageItem is used for logging and potentially for display in the current file. The main display is in SourcesTab where it reads from preset.name directly.

Best approach:
1. In `constants.ts`: add `nameKey` field (i18n key), keep `name` as fallback
2. In `SourcesTab.svelte`: when displaying preset name, resolve via `i18n[preset.nameKey] ?? preset.name`
3. In `ConfigTab.svelte`: same resolution
4. In `sourceManager.ts`: use `name` (fallback) for ImageItem.name (logging)

最新的constants代码已经是这个版本了，请重新读取一下

另外，由于用了404 fallback而图片加载还有时间，每次都会先看到404的那张图, 然后随着图片的加载，在看到图片渐渐从上到下刷新出来，这一点是否可以改进体验？

### 🤖 Assistant
*2026-05-19 14:16:11*

*[step-start part]*

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

The user has made changes to the constants.ts file and wants me to re-read it. They also mention two things:

1. The constants.ts is now different from what I last read - they added `img_xjh` back with `?return=302&type=bg` params
2. There's a UX issue with the CSS double-layer fallback: the 404.jpg shows briefly before the dynamic image loads (because the fallback loads faster being a local file, and the dynamic image takes time to download)

Let me think about the second issue.

**Problem**: With CSS double-layer background-image:
```css
background-image: url("dynamic_url"), url("404.jpg");
background-size: cover, cover;
```

The browser loads both layers simultaneously. Since `404.jpg` is a local file, it loads instantly. The dynamic URL takes time to download. So the user sees `404.jpg` for a moment until the dynamic image loads on top.

**Solutions**:

A. **Remove the CSS fallback, use JS-based fallback instead**:
   - Set only the dynamic URL as background
   - Use a hidden `<img>` element to detect load success/failure
   - On error, switch to fallback
   - This way, 404.jpg never shows unless the dynamic URL fails

B. **Preload the dynamic image before setting it**:
   - First, keep showing the current background (don't clear it)
   - Use `fetch()` or `new Image()` to preload the dynamic image
   - Only switch the background after the dynamic image is fully loaded
   - If fetch fails, switch to fallback

C. **Don't show fallback until error is confirmed**:
   - Set only the dynamic URL as background first
   - The canvas shows nothing (or previous background) while loading
   - Use `onerror` detection via hidden `<img>`
   - Only add fallback if the hidden `<img>` fails

Option B seems best - it's the smoothest UX:
1. Current background stays visible (no flash)
2. Dynamic image loads in background via `new Image()`
3. On load success: smooth transition to new background
4. On load error: transition to fallback

For option B, the implementation would be:

```typescript
export function renderDynamic(url: string, fallbackUrl: string): void {
    if (!canvasEl) return
    
    const img = new Image()
    img.onload = () => {
        // Dynamic image loaded successfully
        canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}')`
        canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover'
    }
    img.onerror = () => {
        // Dynamic image failed, use fallback
        canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${fallbackUrl}')`
        canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover'
    }
    img.src = url
    
    // Keep current background visible while loading
    // (don't clear canvasEl.style.backgroundImage)
}
```

This approach:
- Keeps the current background (previous image or nothing) visible while loading
- Only updates when the new image is ready
- No flash of 404.jpg
- Clean fallback on error

But there's a caveat: `new Image()` creates an `<img>` element, not a CSS background. Some browsers might handle this differently from CSS `url()`. Also, browser caching: if the image URL has `?_t=timestamp`, the browser should download it fresh. But `new Image()` respects cache headers.

Wait, actually there's a subtlety. With `new Image()`:
- `img.src = url` triggers a download
- The browser might serve from cache if the URL was previously cached
- But with `?_t=timestamp`, the URL is unique each time

Also, `new Image()` triggers an immediate GET request. For redirect URLs (like bing wallpaper), it follows redirects correctly.

One more consideration: if the user switches backgrounds rapidly (auto-refresh), multiple `Image` objects might be in flight. We should handle that by canceling previous loads. But this is an edge case.

Let me think about option A (remove CSS fallback, use hidden img):

```typescript
export function renderDynamic(url: string, fallbackUrl: string): void {
    if (!canvasEl) return
    if (videoEl) { ... }
    currentMode = 'image'
    canvasEl.style.display = ''
    
    // Set dynamic URL first, fallback not yet
    canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}')`
    canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover'
    
    // Use hidden img to detect failure
    const img = new Image()
    img.onerror = () => {
        // Dynamic image failed — switch to fallback
        canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${fallbackUrl}')`
    }
    img.src = url
}
```

This is simpler but has the issue that the user sees a blank background while the dynamic image is loading (unless the previous CSS background-image is still set).

Actually, the issue is: when `renderDynamic` is called, what's currently on the canvas? If the previous background is still there, we shouldn't clear it. Let me check...

In `renderImage()`:
```typescript
canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}')`
```

In `renderDynamic()`:
```typescript
canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}'), url('${fallbackUrl}')`
```

Both overwrite `backgroundImage`. So when switching from image A to dynamic URL B, the image A is immediately replaced. With the CSS double-layer approach, the fallback shows while the dynamic loads. The fix is: don't overwrite backgroundImage until the new image is loaded.

Best approach: Option B - preload with `new Image()`.

```typescript
export function renderDynamic(url: string, fallbackUrl: string): void {
    if (!canvasEl) return
    if (videoEl) {
        videoEl.style.display = 'none'
        try { videoEl.pause() } catch { /* ignored */ }
        videoEl.removeAttribute('src')
    }
    
    const img = new Image()
    img.onload = () => {
        canvasEl.style.display = ''
        canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}')`
        canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover'
        currentMode = 'image'
    }
    img.onerror = () => {
        canvasEl.style.display = ''
        canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${fallbackUrl}')`
        canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover'
        currentMode = 'image'
    }
    img.src = url
}
```

Wait, but `img.src = url` uses browser image loading which might have different caching behavior than CSS `url()`. Let me think...

Actually, `new Image().src = url` uses the same HTTP cache as CSS `url()`. The cache-busting `?_t=timestamp` works the same way. So this should be fine.

But there's a caveat: `new Image()` downloads the image into memory as an `<img>` element, then we set it as CSS `backgroundImage` which causes a SECOND download. However, since the browser has already cached the image (it was just loaded by `new Image()`), the second download comes from cache and is instant.

Actually, this is the standard technique for preloading images. The first `img.src = url` populates the browser cache. Then `canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url(...)` reads from cache.

Let me also think about `Image.decode()` - a modern API that ensures the image is fully decoded before use:

```typescript
const img = new Image()
img.src = url
img.decode().then(() => {
    canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}')`
}).catch(() => {
    canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${fallbackUrl}')`
})
```

`img.decode()` returns a promise that resolves when the image is fully decoded and ready to render. This is better than `onload` because it ensures no partial rendering.

But `img.decode()` is not supported in all older Electron versions. Let me check... It's supported since Chrome 64 (2018). SiYuan uses a modern Electron so it should work.

Actually, `img.decode()` is cleaner but `onload`/`onerror` is more widely supported and more explicit about error handling. Let me use `onload`/`onerror` for clarity.

OK, let me put together the plan:

### Fix: Eliminate 404.jpg flash during loading

Replace the CSS double-layer approach with JS-based preloading:

```typescript
// Before (current):
canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}'), url('${fallbackUrl}')`
canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover, cover'

// After (improved):
const preload = new Image()
preload.onload = () => {
    canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}')`
    canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover'
}
preload.onerror = () => {
    canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${fallbackUrl}')`
    canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover'
}
preload.src = url
// Don't clear existing background during preload
```

Benefits:
- Existing background stays visible while new image loads
- No flash of 404.jpg
- 404.jpg only appears if the dynamic URL actually fails
- `new Image()` caching means CSS `url()` reads from cache (no double download)

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

Good, confirmed. The user has:
- `img_xjh` with `?return=302&type=bg` which is the working version (302 redirect to image)
- 4 presets total (no bing_1366 now)

Now let me address the 404.jpg flash issue.

The problem: with CSS double-layer `background-image: url(dynamic), url(fallback)`, the fallback (local 404.jpg) loads instantly while the dynamic URL takes time. User sees a flash of 404.jpg before the dynamic image loads.

Solution: Replace CSS double-layer with JS `new Image()` preloading.

```typescript
export function renderDynamic(url: string, fallbackUrl: string): void {
    if (!canvasEl) return
    if (videoEl) {
        videoEl.style.display = 'none'
        try { videoEl.pause() } catch { /* ignored */ }
        videoEl.removeAttribute('src')
    }
    
    const preload = new Image()
    preload.onload = () => {
        if (currentMode !== 'image') return  // guards against rapid switching
        canvasEl.style.display = ''
        canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}')`
        canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover'
    }
    preload.onerror = () => {
        canvasEl.style.display = ''
        canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${fallbackUrl}')`
        canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover'
    }
    currentMode = 'image'
    preload.src = url
}
```

Note: `currentMode` is set to 'image' before preloading so the guard in `onload` works.

But wait - there's a subtlety. If the user rapidly switches backgrounds (e.g., auto-refresh), multiple `new Image()` instances could be in flight. The `onload` of an old instance could overwrite a newer background. We need a way to cancel stale preloads.

Solution: Use a module-level counter or AbortController.

```typescript
let preloadId = 0

export function renderDynamic(url: string, fallbackUrl: string): void {
    if (!canvasEl) return
    if (videoEl) {
        videoEl.style.display = 'none'
        try { videoEl.pause() } catch { /* ignored */ }
        videoEl.removeAttribute('src')
    }
    
    currentMode = 'image'
    const id = ++preloadId
    const preload = new Image()
    
    preload.onload = () => {
        if (id !== preloadId || currentMode !== 'image') return
        canvasEl.style.display = ''
        canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}')`
        canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover'
    }
    preload.onerror = () => {
        if (id !== preloadId) return
        canvasEl.style.display = ''
        canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${fallbackUrl}')`
        canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover'
    }
    preload.src = url
}
```

This way, if a new `renderDynamic` call happens before the previous preload completes, the old callbacks are invalidated by the counter check.

Now let me think about whether `new Image()` has the same HTTP behavior as CSS `url()`. Key differences:

1. **Caching**: Both use the browser HTTP cache. `?_t=timestamp` ensures unique URLs.
2. **Redirects**: Both follow 302 redirects. `img.xjh.me?return=302` will redirect correctly.
3. **Headers**: `new Image()` sends standard image request headers. CSS `url()` does the same.
4. **Content-Type**: `new Image()` only accepts image content-types. If a server returns HTML, `onerror` fires. This is actually better than CSS which might try to render non-image data.

So `new Image()` should work correctly for all our presets.

Now, one more thing: after `onload` fires, we set `backgroundImage = url(...)`. This triggers the browser to fetch the URL AGAIN for CSS background. But since the URL was just loaded by `new Image()`, it should be in the browser cache and load instantly.

Actually, there's a potential issue: the `onload` event fires when the image is fully downloaded and decoded. Setting `backgroundImage` might trigger another cache hit which is instant. But some browsers might not cache the `new Image()` result for CSS `url()` usage.

To be safe, we could use the same approach as the original URL but without the fallback layer:

Actually wait, `new Image()` populates the browser's image cache. CSS `background-image: url()` uses the same cache. So the second fetch is from cache (instant). This is standard web development practice for image preloading.

Let me now present the plan for the 404 flash fix + the other issues.

Actually, the user asked me to present plans only (plan mode). I should present the combined plan for all issues and wait for confirmation.

</details>

确认了当前代码。现在来说 404.jpg 闪现问题。

---

## 问题分析

CSS 双层 `background-image` 的问题：

```
background-image: url(dynamic), url(404.jpg)
                    ── 慢 ──    ── 快(本地) ──
```

浏览器并行加载两层。404.jpg 是本地文件，瞬间显示；动态 URL 需要网络，加载完才覆盖 404.jpg。用户看到：**404 闪现 → 图片从上到下刷出**。

---

## 解决方案：JS `Image` 预加载替代 CSS 双层

```typescript
// 之前（CSS 双层，有闪现）：
canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}'), url('${fallbackUrl}')`

// 之后（JS 预加载，无闪现）：
const preload = new Image()
preload.onload = () => {
    canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}')`      // 后台就绪后才设置
}
preload.onerror = () => {
    canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${fallbackUrl}')` // 真的失败了才兜底
}
preload.src = url
// 期间不修改 canvas，保持当前背景不变
```

| 对比 | CSS 双层 | JS 预加载 |
|------|---------|----------|
| 加载中显示 | 404.jpg 闪现 | 保持上一张背景 |
| 加载成功 | 动态图覆盖 404 | 直接切到动态图 |
| 加载失败 | 404.jpg 保留 | 切到 404.jpg |
| 额外下载 | 无 | `new Image()` 填充缓存，CSS `url()` 读缓存（0 开销） |
| 缓存破坏 | `?_t=timestamp`（同） | `?_t=timestamp`（同） |

**防竞态**：加计数器防止快速切换时旧回调覆盖新结果：

```typescript
let preloadSeq = 0

export function renderDynamic(url: string, fallbackUrl: string): void {
    // ...
    const seq = ++preloadSeq
    const preload = new Image()
    preload.onload = () => {
        if (seq !== preloadSeq) return   // 被新调用废弃
        canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}')`
    }
    preload.onerror = () => {
        if (seq !== preloadSeq) return
        canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${fallbackUrl}')`
    }
    preload.src = url
}
```

**`new Image()` vs CSS `url()` 行为一致性**：
- 缓存：共用浏览器 HTTP 缓存，`?_t=timestamp` 破坏缓存一致
- 重定向：都跟随 302（`img.xjh.me?return=302` 正确跟随）
- Content-Type：`new Image()` 只接受 image，HTML 等 → `onerror`（比 CSS 更严格，更安全）

<content>
1: <script lang="ts">
2:     import { onMount } from "svelte"
3:     import { configStore } from "../../stores/config"
4:     import { isDesktop } from "../../utils/fs"
5:     import { scanSource } from "../../services/sourceManager"
6:     import { renderImage, renderVideo, renderDynamic, changeOpacity, changeBlur } from "../../services/bgRender"
7:     import { confirmDialog } from "../../libs/dialog"
8:     import { pluginAssetsDir, pickDefaultBackground, DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS, DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL, isDynamicUrl } from "../../constants"
9:     import { removeFile } from "../../utils/api"
10:     import { toAssetRelPath } from "../../utils/path"
11:     import { devLog } from "../../utils/logger"
12:     import {
13:         showLocalDirDialog,
14:         showAssetsDirDialog,
15:         showUrlDialog,
16:         showAddDynamicUrlDialog,
17:         setupMultipleFilePicker,
18:         setupFolderFilePicker,
19:     } from "../dialogs"
20:     import type { ImageItem } from "../../types"
21: 
22:     const i18n = (window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.i18n ?? {}
23: 
24:     interface SourceGroup {
25:         type: 'upload' | 'assets' | 'local'
26:         label: string
27:         path: string
28:         removable: boolean
29:         files: ImageItem[]
30:         inaccessible: boolean
31:         collapsed: boolean
32:         configKey: string
33:     }
34: 
35:     let groups = $state<SourceGroup[]>([])
36:     let selectedItem = $state<ImageItem | null>(null)
37:     let previewSrc = $state<string | null>(null)
38:     let previewObjectUrl = $state<string | null>(null)
39:     let dynamicCollapsed = $state(false)
40:     let dynamicUrls = $state<string[]>([])
41: 
42:     onMount(() => {
43:         dynamicUrls = [...configStore.get("dynamicBgUrls")]
44:         refreshAll()
45:     })
46: 
47:     async function refreshAll() {
48:         const newGroups: SourceGroup[] = []
49: 
50:         const uploadFiles = await scanSource('upload', pluginAssetsDir)
51:         newGroups.push({
52:             type: 'upload',
53:             label: i18n.pluginCache,
54:             path: pluginAssetsDir,
55:             removable: false,
56:             files: uploadFiles,
57:             inaccessible: false,
58:             collapsed: false,
59:             configKey: '',
60:         })
61: 
62:         const assetDirs = configStore.get("assetDirs").filter(Boolean)
63:         const localFolders = isDesktop() ? configStore.get("localFolders").filter(Boolean) : []
64: 
65:         const assetTasks = assetDirs.map(async (dir) => {
66:             const normalized = toAssetRelPath(dir)
67:             const path = `/data/${normalized}`
68:             const label = normalized.startsWith('assets/') ? normalized.slice('assets/'.length) : normalized
69:             const files = await scanSource('assets', path + '/')
70:             return { type: 'assets' as const, label, path, files, normalized }
71:         })
72: 
73:         const localTasks = localFolders.map(async (dir) => {
74:             const files = await scanSource('local', dir + (dir.endsWith('/') ? '' : '/'))
75:             return { type: 'local' as const, label: dir, path: dir, files }
76:         })
77: 
78:         const allScanResults = await Promise.all([...assetTasks, ...localTasks])
79: 
80:         for (const r of allScanResults) {
81:             if (r.type === 'assets') {
82:                 newGroups.push({
83:                     type: 'assets', label: r.label, path: r.path,
84:                     removable: true, files: r.files,
85:                     inaccessible: r.files.length === 0 && r.path.length > 0,
86:                     collapsed: false, configKey: r.normalized,
87:                 })
88:             } else {
89:                 newGroups.push({
90:                     type: 'local', label: r.label, path: r.path,
91:                     removable: true, files: r.files,
92:                     inaccessible: r.files.length === 0,
93:                     collapsed: false, configKey: r.label,
94:                 })
95:             }
96:         }
97: 
98:         groups = newGroups
99:     }
100: 
101:     function togglePreset(url: string) {
102:         if (dynamicUrls.includes(url)) {
103:             dynamicUrls = dynamicUrls.filter(u => u !== url)
104:         } else {
105:             dynamicUrls = [...dynamicUrls, url]
106:         }
107:         configStore.set("dynamicBgUrls", dynamicUrls)
108:         configStore.save()
109:         if (url === configStore.get("currentFile")) reselectBackground()
110:         refreshAll()
111:     }
112: 
113:     function isPreset(url: string): boolean {
114:         return DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS.some(p => p.url === url)
115:     }
116: 
117:     function removeDynamicUrl(url: string) {
118:         dynamicUrls = dynamicUrls.filter(u => u !== url)
119:         configStore.set("dynamicBgUrls", dynamicUrls)
120:         configStore.save()
121:         if (url === configStore.get("currentFile")) reselectBackground()
122:         refreshAll()
123:     }
124: 
125:     function addDynamicUrl() {
126:         showAddDynamicUrlDialog((url: string) => {
127:             if (!dynamicUrls.includes(url)) {
128:                 dynamicUrls = [...dynamicUrls, url]
129:                 configStore.set("dynamicBgUrls", dynamicUrls)
130:                 configStore.save()
131:                 refreshAll()
132:             }
133:         })
134:     }
135: 
136:     function setDynamicAsBackground(url: string) {
137:         const cb = url + (url.includes('?') ? '&' : '?') + '_t=' + Date.now()
138:         configStore.set("currentFile", url)
139:         configStore.save()
140:         renderDynamic(cb, DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL)
141:         changeOpacity(configStore.get("opacity"))
142:         changeBlur(configStore.get("blur"))
143:     }
144: 
145:     function toggleGroup(i: number) {
146:         groups[i].collapsed = !groups[i].collapsed
147:         groups = groups
148:     }
149: 
150:     function openAssetDirDialog() {
151:         showAssetsDirDialog((paths: string[]) => {
152:             for (const dir of paths) addAssetFolder(dir)
153:         })
154:     }
155: 
156:     function openLocalDirDialog() {
157:         showLocalDirDialog((path: string) => {
158:             addLocalFolder(path)
159:         })
160:     }
161: 
162:     function addAssetFolder(dir: string) {
163:         if (!dir) return
164:         devLog("[bgCover] addAssetFolder:", dir)
165:         const dirs = [...configStore.get("assetDirs"), dir]
166:         configStore.set("assetDirs", dirs)
167:         configStore.save()
168:         refreshAll()
169:     }
170: 
171:     function addLocalFolder(path: string) {
172:         if (!path) return
173:         devLog("[bgCover] addLocalFolder:", path)
174:         const folders = [...configStore.get("localFolders"), path]
175:         configStore.set("localFolders", folders)
176:         configStore.save()
177:         refreshAll()
178:     }
179: 
180:     function removeGroup(i: number) {
181:         const g = groups[i]
182:         devLog("[bgCover] removeGroup:", g.type, g.configKey)
183:         const currentFile = configStore.get("currentFile")
184:         const wasCurrentInGroup = g.files.some(f => f.url === currentFile)
185:         if (g.type === 'assets') {
186:             const dirs = [...configStore.get("assetDirs")]
187:             const idx = dirs.indexOf(g.configKey)
188:             if (idx >= 0) {
189:                 dirs.splice(idx, 1)
190:                 configStore.set("assetDirs", dirs)
191:                 configStore.save()
192:             }
193:         } else if (g.type === 'local') {
194:             const dirs = [...configStore.get("localFolders")]
195:             const idx = dirs.indexOf(g.configKey)
196:             if (idx >= 0) {
197:                 dirs.splice(idx, 1)
198:                 configStore.set("localFolders", dirs)
199:                 configStore.save()
200:             }
201:         }
202:         clearPreview()
203:         if (wasCurrentInGroup) {
204:             reselectBackground()
205:         }
206:         refreshAll()
207:     }
208: 
209:     function setAsBackground(item: ImageItem) {
210:         devLog("[bgCover] setAsBackground:", item.name)
211:         configStore.set("currentFile", item.url)
212:         configStore.save()
213:         if (item.type === 'image') {
214:             renderImage(item.url)
215:         } else {
216:             renderVideo(item.url)
217:         }
218:     }
219: 
220:     function selectPreview(item: ImageItem) {
221:         if (item.type !== 'image') return
222:         if (selectedItem?.url === item.url) {
223:             clearPreview()
224:             return
225:         }
226:         selectedItem = item
227:         loadPreview(item.url)
228:     }
229: 
230:     function clearPreview() {
231:         if (previewObjectUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(previewObjectUrl)
232:         selectedItem = null
233:         previewSrc = null
234:         previewObjectUrl = null
235:     }
236: 
237:     function loadPreview(url: string) {
238:         if (previewObjectUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(previewObjectUrl)
239:         previewObjectUrl = null
240:         previewSrc = null
241:         fetch(url)
242:             .then(r => r.blob())
243:             .then(b => {
244:                 if (selectedItem?.url === url) {
245:                     previewObjectUrl = URL.createObjectURL(b)
246:                     previewSrc = previewObjectUrl
247:                 }
248:             })
249:             .catch(() => {})
250:     }
251: 
252:     async function clearCache() {
253:         const group = groups.find(g => g.type === 'upload')
254:         if (!group || group.files.length === 0) return
255:         const imgCount = group.files.filter(f => f.type === 'image').length
256:         const vidCount = group.files.filter(f => f.type === 'video').length
257:         const parts: string[] = []
258:         if (imgCount > 0) parts.push(`${imgCount} ${i18n.imageCount}`)
259:         if (vidCount > 0) parts.push(`${vidCount} ${i18n.videoCount}`)
260:         const confirmed = await new Promise<boolean>(resolve => {
261:             confirmDialog({
262:                 title: i18n.clearCacheTitle,
263:                 content: `${i18n.clearCacheConfirm} ${parts.join('、')}`,                confirm: () => resolve(true),
264:                 cancel: () => resolve(false),
265:                 width: "360px",
266:             })
267:         })
268:         if (!confirmed) return
269:         devLog("[bgCover] clearCache:", group.files.length, "files")
270:         const wasCurrentDeleted = group.files.some(f => f.url === configStore.get("currentFile"))
271:         for (const file of group.files) {
272:             await removeFile(file.apiPath)
273:         }
274:         if (wasCurrentDeleted) await reselectBackground()
275:         refreshAll()
276:     }
277: 
278:     function openInFileManager(group: SourceGroup) {
279:         const wsDir = (window as any).siyuan?.config?.system?.workspaceDir ?? ''
280:         let absPath = group.path
281:         if (group.type === 'upload' || group.type === 'assets') {
282:             absPath = wsDir + absPath
283:         }
284:         try {
285:             const shell = (window as any).require?.('electron')?.shell
286:             if (shell) {
287:                 shell.openPath(absPath)
288:             } else {
289:                 const { exec } = (window as any).require?.('child_process') ?? {}
290:                 if (exec) {
291:                     const cmd = process.platform === 'darwin' ? 'open' : process.platform === 'win32' ? 'explorer' : 'xdg-open'
292:                     exec(`${cmd} "${absPath}"`)
293:                 }
294:             }
295:         } catch { /* ignore */ }
296:     }
297: 
298:     async function reselectBackground() {
299:         configStore.set("currentFile", null)
300:         await configStore.save()
301:         await (window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.plugin?.randomSelect?.()
302:         if (!configStore.get("currentFile")) {
303:             configStore.set("currentFile", pickDefaultBackground())
304:             await configStore.save()
305:             ;(window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.plugin?.applyBackground?.()
306:         }
307:     }
308: 
309:     async function deleteFile(file: ImageItem) {
310:         devLog("[bgCover] deleteFile:", file.name)
311:         const wasCurrent = file.url === configStore.get("currentFile")
312:         await removeFile(file.apiPath)
313:         if (wasCurrent) await reselectBackground()
314:         refreshAll()
315:     }
316: 
317:     function pickMultipleFiles() {
318:         setupMultipleFilePicker(() => { refreshAll() })
319:     }
320: 
321:     function pickFolderFiles() {
322:         setupFolderFilePicker(() => { refreshAll() })
323:     }
324: 
325:     function showAddUrlDialog() {
326:         showUrlDialog((uploadUrl?: string) => {
327:             if (uploadUrl) {
328:                 configStore.set("currentFile", uploadUrl)
329:                 configStore.save()
330:                 if (uploadUrl.match(/\.(mp4|webm|ogg|mov|avi|mkv)$/i)) {
331:                     renderVideo(uploadUrl)
332:                 } else {
333:                     renderImage(uploadUrl)
334:                 }
335:                 changeOpacity(configStore.get("opacity"))
336:                 changeBlur(configStore.get("blur"))
337:             }
338:             refreshAll()
339:         })
340:     }

### 1. bgRender.ts - Replace renderDynamic

```typescript
let preloadSeq = 0

export function renderDynamic(url: string, fallbackUrl: string): void {
    if (!canvasEl) return
    if (videoEl) {
        videoEl.style.display = 'none'
        try { videoEl.pause() } catch { /* ignored */ }
        videoEl.removeAttribute('src')
    }
    currentMode = 'image'
    canvasEl.style.display = ''
    
    const seq = ++preloadSeq
    const preload = new Image()
    preload.onload = () => {
        if (seq !== preloadSeq || currentMode !== 'image') return
        canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}')`
        canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover'
    }
    preload.onerror = () => {
        if (seq !== preloadSeq) return
        canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${fallbackUrl}')`
        canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover'
    }
    preload.src = url
}
```

### 3. types.ts - Add customDynamicUrls, config.ts - Add default

### 🤖 Assistant
*2026-05-19 14:16:11*

*[step-start part]*

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

I need to restructure the AboutTab layout:

Top (vertically centered): version + description
Bottom (aligned to bottom): GitHub link + author
Middle: empty space (auto-flex)

The approach:
1. Set the container to `height: 100%` and `justify-content: space-between`
2. Group top content (version + description) in one div
3. Group bottom content (GitHub + author) in another div
4. Both groups will be pushed to opposite ends

Or better: use `flex: 1` on a middle spacer, or use `margin-top: auto` on the bottom group.

Option 1: Two group approach with `justify-content: space-between` + `height: 100%`:
```html
<div style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; height: 100%; justify-content: space-between;">
    <div>       <!-- top group: vertically centered in upper half -->
        <div>version</div>
        <div>description</div>
    </div>
    <div>       <!-- bottom group: at the bottom -->
        <div>GitHub</div>
        <div>author</div>
    </div>
</div>
```

Wait, `justify-content: space-between` with two items pushes them to top and bottom. But the top group should be vertically CENTERED, not at the very top.

So I'd need a three-section layout:
```html
<div style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; height: 100%;">
    <div style="flex: 1; display: flex; flex-direction: column; justify-content: center; align-items: center;">
        <!-- top group: centered -->
        <div>version</div>
        <div>description</div>
    </div>
    <div>
        <!-- bottom group -->
        <div>GitHub</div>
        <div>author</div>
    </div>
</div>
```

This way:
- Top `flex: 1` takes remaining space and centers its content
- Bottom group sits at the bottom

That's the cleanest approach. Let me implement it.

</details>

27: ## 特性
28: 
29: - [X] 插件全平台支持（桌面端 / 移动端 / 浏览器）
30: - [X] 图片和视频作为思源笔记背景（自动识别扩展名，canvas / video 双模式渲染）
31: - [X] 三种背景源类型统一管理
32:   - [X] 本地文件夹直读（桌面端，零上传）
33:   - [X] 思源 assets 子文件夹引用（全平台）
34:   - [X] 上传文件到插件缓存（全平台，支持网络 URL 下载）
35: - [X] 背景资源管理
36:   - [X] 多文件/整个目录上传
37:   - [X] 文件删除、目录定位、缓存清空
38:   - [X] 鼠标悬浮文件缩略图预览
39: - [X] 选择与切换背景
40:   - [X] 手动选择
41:   - [X] 手动触发随机选择
42:   - [X] 定时自动随机切换
43:   - [X] 启动时随机选择
44: - [X] 手动调整透明度（加权算法保证可读性）
45: - [X] 手动调整背景虚化程度
46: - [X] 背景图片 X/Y 偏移控制
47: - [X] 按主题屏蔽（指定主题上不启用插件）
48: - [X] 快捷键支持
49: 
50: ## 实现思路
51: 
52: 在 `<HTML>` 元素中添加和 `<head>` 与 `<body>` 平级的 `<canvas>` 和 `<video>` 元素，平铺居中且处于笔记最底层，用来存放背景。根据文件扩展名自动选择 canvas（图片）或 video（视频）元素渲染。通过给 `<body>` 整体添加 `style='opacity: xxx'` 属性来实现笔记面板的透明。
53: 
54: 背景资源通过三种源类型管理：`local`（桌面端本地文件夹，使用 `window.require('fs/promises')` 直读，`file:///` 渲染，零上传）、`upload`（插件缓存目录，支持文件上传和 URL 下载）、`assets`（思源笔记资源子文件夹引用，零额外存储开销）。
55: 
56: 用户可设置的透明度定义域为 `[0.1, 1]`。但为了笔记内容的可读性，使用加权逻辑 `f(x) = 0.99 - 0.25x`，加权后透明度值域为 `[0.74, 0.99]`。由于不同主题本身就有完全不同的颜色设定，所以同样的透明度设置在不同的主题上表现不完全一致。
57:

59:

67: * <b>背景源重构</b>：新增本地文件夹直读（桌面端）、assets 子文件夹引用、网络 URL 下载，三种源类型统一随机池管理
68: * <b>视频背景</b>：支持 .mp4、.webm、.ogg、.mov 视频作为背景，自动切换渲染模式
69: * <b>UI 重写</b>：全新的 5 标签设置面板、顶栏下拉菜单、文件树预览、缩略图悬浮预览
