```
28: ## Features
29: 
30: - [X] Full platform support (desktop / mobile / browser)
31: - [X] Images and videos as SiYuan Note background (auto-detect extension, canvas / video dual-mode rendering)
32: - [X] Three background source types, unified management
33:   - [X] Local folder direct reading (desktop only, zero upload)
34:   - [X] SiYuan assets sub-folder referencing (all platforms)
35:   - [X] Upload files to plugin cache (all platforms, supports network URL download)
36: - [X] Background resource management
37:   - [X] Multi-file / entire directory upload
38:   - [X] File deletion, folder location, cache clearing
39:   - [X] Mouse hover file thumbnail preview
40: - [X] Background selection and switching
41:   - [X] Manual selection
42:   - [X] Manual random selection
43:   - [X] Scheduled auto-random switching
44:   - [X] Random selection on startup
45: - [X] Manually adjust transparency (weighted algorithm for readability)
46: - [X] Manually adjust background blur
47: - [X] Background image X/Y offset control
48: - [X] Theme blocking (disable plugin on specific themes)
49: - [X] Shortcut key support
50: 
51: 
52: ## Implementation
53: 
54: Add `<canvas>` and `<video>` elements within the `<HTML>` element, at the same level as `<head>` and `<body>`. These elements are tiled and centered, placed at the bottom layer to serve as the background. Based on file extension, the engine automatically selects canvas (for images) or video (for videos) for rendering. Add `style='opacity: xxx'` to the `<body>` element to achieve transparency for the notebook panel.
55: 
56: Background resources are managed through three source types: `local` (desktop-only local folders, using `window.require('fs/promises')` for direct reading and `file:///` for rendering, zero upload), `upload` (plugin cache directory, supports file upload and URL download), and `assets` (SiYuan note resource sub-folder referencing, zero additional storage).
57: 
58: The range of transparency that can be set by the user is `[0.1, 1]`. However, to ensure readability of the notebook content, a weighted logic `f(x) = 0.99 - 0.25x` is used. The weighted transparency range is `[0.74, 0.99]`. Since different themes have completely different color settings, the same transparency setting may not appear consistent across different themes.
59: 
60: ## ChangeLogs
61: 
62: <details open>
63: <summary><b>May 2026 — v1.0.0 Refactoring Edition</b></summary>
64: 
65: **26.05.18**
66: 
67: * <b style='color:red'>Breaking Change</b>: Full refactoring. Old v0.x configurations are incompatible and require reconfiguration.
68: * <b>Build Upgrade</b>: Webpack → Vite 5, pure TS template strings → Svelte 5 components, added Vitest testing framework.
69: * <b>Background Source Refactoring</b>: Added local folder direct reading (desktop), assets sub-folder referencing, URL download, three source types unified random pool management.
70: * <b>Video Background</b>: Support .mp4, .webm, .ogg, .mov videos as background, automatic rendering mode switching.
71: * <b>UI Rewrite</b>: Brand new 5-tab settings panel, topbar dropdown menu, file tree preview, thumbnail hover preview.
72: * <b>Storage Migration</b>: All configs migrated to local.json single-layer storage, removed ts-md5 and other legacy dependencies.
73: * <b>Removed Features</b>: CSS transparency mode, Live2D stub code, Bug report dialog, Android limitation notice, Demo images, sizeMode switching.
74: * <b>Full Platform Support</b>: Available on desktop / mobile / browser-desktop / browser-mobile (non-desktop platforms auto-hide local folder features).
75:
```

```
## 🔗 动态网络壁纸订阅源

新增第四种背景源类型 — 支持每次返回不同图片的随机图片 API。

- **内置预设**：必应每日壁纸 (1920/1366)、Unsplash 随机、imgapi 随机风景、岁月小筑随机动漫
- **自定义 URL**：用户可添加自己的随机图片 API，支持启用/停用切换
- **参与统一随机池**：动态订阅源与本地文件夹、assets、插件缓存一起参与随机选择
- **CSS fallback**：动态 URL 加载失败时自动显示内置 fallback 底图

## 🎬 视频预览

设置为面板源列表中悬浮视频文件时，预览区自动播放视频预览。

## 📺 推荐视频素材站

源管理面板新增「推荐视频素材站」区块（默认收起），提供 Pexels、Pixabay、Coverr、Videezy 链接供用户下载视频后通过本地上传添加。

## 🔧 代码质量改进

- 消除所有硬编码中文 fallback 文本，全部走 i18n
- 统一文件上传到 `utils/api.ts` 的 `putFile()`，移除各处重复 FormData 构造
- 目录扫描改用 `Promise.all` 并行化
- TypeScript 模块 camelCase / Svelte 组件 PascalCase 命名规范化
- 抽取 `src/ui/dialogs/` 为共享对话框模块

## 🎨 关于页优化

- 显示插件图标
- 版本号与描述垂直居中，GitHub/作者信息沉底对齐
- 调试信息（FrontEnd/BackEnd/平台）移至关于页
```

Conclusion:

| 文件 | 状态 | 原因 |
|------|------|------|
| `src/libs/index.d.ts` | **不可移除** | 被 `src/libs/siyuanSetting.ts` 使用（`TSettingItemType`、`ISettingUtilsItem` 接口） |
| `src/types/index.d.ts` | **可移除** | 定义的 `BlockId`、`DocumentId`、`Block` 等项目源码中无任何引用，是 frostime 模板遗留 |

### 🤖 Assistant
*2026-05-19 14:16:11*

是否建议把 src/libs/index.d.ts 合并到   src/libs/siyuanSetting.ts  的 开头部分？

### 🤖 Assistant
*2026-05-19 14:16:11*

*[step-start part]*

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

The user is asking if we should merge `src/libs/index.d.ts` into `src/libs/siyuanSetting.ts`. Let me think about this.

`src/libs/index.d.ts` is a `.d.ts` file containing ambient type declarations (interfaces and types). These are globally available without explicit import. `siyuanSetting.ts` uses `TSettingItemType` and `ISettingUtilsItem` without importing them.

If we move these declarations into `siyuanSetting.ts`:
1. They would become module-scoped, not global
2. `siyuanSetting.ts` would need to `export` them
3. Any other file that might use them would need to `import` them

Currently, no other file uses these types (only `siyuanSetting.ts` does). So making them module-scoped within `siyuanSetting.ts` and exporting them would work fine. It's actually better practice - no global ambient types.

But wait - let me check if `siyuanSetting.ts` has the types already imported or if they're expected to be global...

Looking at `siyuanSetting.ts` line 19:
```typescript
const createDefaultGetter = (type: TSettingItemType) => {
```

And line 84:
```typescript
settings: Map<string, ISettingUtilsItem> = new Map();
```

These types are used without imports - they rely on the `.d.ts` file making them global. If we move them into `siyuanSetting.ts`, we need to export them and import where used.

Since only `siyuanSetting.ts` uses them, merging makes sense. But we should keep the file structure clean by putting type definitions at the top of `siyuanSetting.ts`.

Actually, I'm in plan mode - I should just analyze and present the recommendation, not make edits.

</details>

建议合并。理由：

| 维度 | 当前（分离 .d.ts） | 合并后 |
|------|-------------------|--------|
| 文件数 | 2 | 1 |
| 类型作用域 | 全局 ambient（污染） | 模块内 `export` |
| 唯一使用者 | `siyuanSetting.ts` | 自身 `export` 自给自足 |
| 发现成本 | 需跨文件查找类型定义 | 同文件顶部可见 |

唯一注意点：`siyuanSetting.ts` 顶部把这些类型加 `export`，因为 `index.ts` 导出了 `siyuanSetting` 的 class，其他文件可能间接依赖这些类型。

改动就是：
1. 把 `libs/index.d.ts` 的类型声明移到 `libs/siyuanSetting.ts` 文件顶部并加 `export`
2. 删除 `libs/index.d.ts`

同时 `src/types/index.d.ts` 也一并删除（上次确定无引用）。

### 🤖 Assistant
*2026-05-19 14:16:11*

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

Let me analyze the relationship between the two API wrappers.

**`utils/api.ts`**:
- Uses `fetchSyncPost` (Promise-based)
- `request()` wraps `fetchSyncPost`, returns `data` on success, `null` on failure
- Specific functions: `readSiyuanDir()`, `putFile()`, `removeFile()`, `downloadUrl()`

**`stores/config.ts`**:
- Uses `fetchPost` (callback-based)
- `siyuanApiPost()` wraps `fetchPost` callback → Promise, resolves with `data`, rejects on error
- Used for: `getLocalStorage`, `setLocalStorageVal`, `removeLocalStorageVals`, `readDir`, `removeFile`

Key differences:

1. **API method**: `utils/api.ts` uses `fetchSyncPost` (Promise-based) vs `config.ts` uses `fetchPost` (callback-based)
   - Both are SiYuan APIs, but `fetchSyncPost` is the modern Promise API
   - `fetchPost` is the legacy callback API

2. **Error handling**: 
   - `utils/api.ts`: `code !== 0` → returns `null` (silent)
   - `config.ts`: `code !== 0` → `reject()` (throws error)
   
   Some callers in config.ts use try/catch to handle the rejections.

3. **Dependency direction**:
   - `stores/config.ts` → should NOT depend on `utils/api.ts` (according to rules: "fs.ts 中不应依赖 stores/config.ts (低层工具不应依赖状态层)")
   - But the reverse direction is unclear. `utils/api.ts` is a utility, `stores/config.ts` is a store.
   - Actually, `utils/api.ts` depends on business context (the plugin's package name, paths), so it's higher-level than a pure utility.
   - `stores/config.ts` IS a state management layer.

Actually, looking at the existing rules:
> `src/utils/api.ts` — 业务领域工具（依赖本插件业务上下文）
> `src/stores/config.ts` — 状态管理（单例 store）

Both are same level - they're both plugin-internal modules. The rule about "低层不应依赖高层" doesn't strictly apply here since they're at the same architectural level.

**The real questions**:

1. Can `config.ts` import from `utils/api.ts`? Yes, it already imports from `utils/logger.ts`, so cross-utils import is allowed.

2. Should it? Let's think:

**Pros of consolidating**:
- Single source of truth for API calls
- Consistent error handling (all null-returning vs some reject-throwing)
- `utils/api.ts` already has `readSiyuanDir()`, `removeFile()` which config.ts duplicates
- `config.ts` currently does raw `fetchPost` + callback wrapping manually

**Cons of consolidating**:
- `config.ts` uses `fetchPost` (callback) not `fetchSyncPost` (Promise) — but `utils/api.ts`'s `request()` function abstracts this
- Some `siyuanApiPost` calls in config.ts pass complex objects that `utils/api.ts`'s `request()` can handle generically
- One concern: `fetchPost` vs `fetchSyncPost` — are they truly interchangeable? Yes, both call the same SiYuan HTTP backend

**Analysis of config.ts's API calls**:

| Call site | Can use `utils/api.ts`? |
|-----------|------------------------|
| `getLocalStorage` (load) | No direct equivalent, would need a generic `request()` |
| `setLocalStorageVal` (save) | No direct equivalent |
| `removeLocalStorageVals` (reset) | No direct equivalent |
| `removeFile` (reset) | Yes! `utils/api.ts` has `removeFile()` |
| `readDir` (cleanOldConfig) | Yes! `utils/api.ts` has `readDirItems()` |
| `removeFile` (cleanOldConfig) | Yes! `utils/api.ts` has `removeFile()` |
| `readDir` (cleanPublicDir) | Yes! |
| `removeFile` (cleanPublicDir) | Yes! |

So about half the calls can use `utils/api.ts` directly, and half (storage operations) need a generic request method.

**My recommendation**:

1. Export the `request()` function from `utils/api.ts` (currently it's private)
2. In `config.ts`, import `request` + `removeFile` + `readDirItems` from `utils/api.ts`
3. Replace all `siyuanApiPost(...)` calls with the appropriate `utils/api.ts` functions
4. Remove the `siyuanApiPost()` function from `config.ts`
5. For `/api/storage/*` calls that don't have dedicated wrappers, use `request()` directly

This gives:
- Consistent error handling (null-for-failure pattern)
- Single API entry point
- No duplication between `fetchPost` and `fetchSyncPost` usage

But wait — there's a subtle issue. `siyuanApiPost` rejects on error, and callers use try/catch. After switching to `request()` which returns null on error, the try/catch patterns in callers would need to change to null checks. Actually, looking at the callers:

- `load()`: already uses try/catch around `siyuanApiPost`, returns `{}` on failure. With `request()` returning null, the try/catch wouldn't catch and we'd need `?? {}` instead.
- `save()`: doesn't have try/catch. With `resolve`/`reject`, failures bubble up. With `request()`, it returns null and we need to check.
- `reset()`: uses try/catch around multiple calls. With `request()`, need to check null for each.

Actually the migration isn't trivial because the error handling model differs.

Let me present a balanced view to the user.

</details>

分析两者的差异：

---

## 对比

| 维度 | `config.ts` `siyuanApiPost()` | `utils/api.ts` `request()` |
|------|------|------|
| 底层 API | `fetchPost`（callback 式） | `fetchSyncPost`（Promise 式） |
| 失败处理 | `reject(msg)` → caller 用 try/catch | 返回 `null` → caller 用 null check |
| 类型安全 | `siyuanApiPost<T>()` 带泛型 | `request()` 返回 `any` |
| 作用域 | config 私有函数 | module 内部私有 |

## config.ts 中 9 处调用分析

| 调用 | 目标 API | `utils/api.ts` 有对应？ |
|------|---------|----------------------|
| `load()` → `getLocalStorage` | `/api/storage/...` | ❌ 需要通用 `request()` |
| `save()` → `setLocalStorageVal` | `/api/storage/...` | ❌ |
| `reset()` → `removeLocalStorageVals` | `/api/storage/...` | ❌ |
| `reset()` → `removeFile` | `/api/file/removeFile` | ✅ `removeFile()` |
| `cleanOldConfig()` → `removeLocalStorageVals` | `/api/storage/...` | ❌ |
| `cleanOldConfig()` → `readDir` | `/api/file/readDir` | ✅ `readDirItems()` |
| `cleanOldConfig()` → `removeFile` | `/api/file/removeFile` | ✅ `removeFile()` |
| `cleanPublicDir()` → `readDir` | `/api/file/readDir` | ✅ |
| `cleanPublicDir()` → `removeFile` (×N) | `/api/file/removeFile` | ✅ |

结果是：**5 处已有对应函数，4 处 storage API 需要通用 request**。

## 建议：推荐统一，但需两步走

**① 把 `utils/api.ts` 的 `request()` 改为 `export`**

```typescript
export async function request(url: string, data?: any): Promise<any> {
    const res: IResponse = await fetchSyncPost(url, data ?? {})
    return res.code === 0 ? res.data : null
}
```

**② `config.ts` 中：删除 `siyuanApiPost()`，统一用 `utils/api.ts`**

```typescript
import { request, readDirItems, removeFile } from "../utils/api"

// load():
const all = await request("/api/storage/getLocalStorage")
stored = all?.[STORAGE_KEY] ?? {}

// save():
await request("/api/storage/setLocalStorageVal", { key: STORAGE_KEY, val: this.cfg })

// reset():
await request("/api/storage/removeLocalStorageVals", { keys: [STORAGE_KEY] })
await request("/api/file/removeFile", { path: `/data/storage/petal/...` })
// → 或直接用 removeFile(path)
```

**风险点**：错误处理语义变化

| 调用 | 旧 (reject) | 新 (null) | 影响 |
|------|-----------|----------|------|
| `load()` | try/catch → `{}` | `?? {}` | 无行为差异 |
| `save()` | 无 try/catch，异常向上抛 | null 静默 | 需确认 callers 是否依赖异常 |
| `reset()` | try/catch 包裹 `{ /* ignore */ }` | null 时同样不处理 | 无行为差异 |

整体改动 ~20 行，`config.ts` 删掉 `siyuanApiPost()`，`utils/api.ts` 加一个 `export`。

要执行吗？

### 🤖 Assistant
*2026-05-19 14:16:11*

*[step-start part]*

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

The user is asking me to compare two approaches:

1. Adopt config.ts's advantages into utils/api.ts (Promise-style with proper type safety, null/error handling)
2. Or directly copy the template author's api.ts from the reference

Let me analyze the reference api.ts:

The reference `api.ts` from frostime's template is MUCH more comprehensive - it covers notebooks, filetree, blocks, attributes, SQL, templates, files, export, notifications, network, and system APIs. It uses `fetchSyncPost` (Promise-based) and has a clean `request()` pattern.

Comparing our current `utils/api.ts`:
- Uses `fetchSyncPost` ✓
- Has `request()` but it's private - returns `null` on failure
- Has domain-specific functions: `readSiyuanDir`, `putFile`, `removeFile`, `downloadUrl`

The reference template's `api.ts` has a better `request()` signature - returns `response.data` (the actual data) or `null`.

For the type safety question: the reference uses `IWebSocketData` type from siyuan, not generic types. Our current `IResponse` is defined locally. The reference has `IWebSocketData` directly from siyuan.

For the error handling question: the reference returns `null` on failure (same as our current approach), not `reject`.

So the user is asking if we should:
1. Replace our `utils/api.ts` with the reference template's `api.ts` (more complete, better organized)
2. Or add config.ts's advantages (generic types, reject-on-error)

My opinion:

**The reference template's `api.ts` is the better foundation** because:
1. Already uses `fetchSyncPost` (Promise)
2. Has all the API wrappers organized by domain
3. Already has `putFile`, `removeFile`, `readDir` (our existing functions)
4. The `request()` function is clean and simple

But we shouldn't blindly copy all 478 lines - the template has many APIs our plugin doesn't need (notebook ops, block ops, export, etc.).

**My recommendation: selectively enhance our `utils/api.ts`**:
1. Keep `request()` as-is (already uses `fetchSyncPost`, already returns `null` on failure)
2. Export `request()` so `config.ts` can use it
3. Add proper types from siyuan (`IWebSocketData`)
4. In `config.ts`, replace `siyuanApiPost` calls with `request()` from `utils/api.ts`

For type safety: `request()` returning `any` is fine for our use case. The caller in `config.ts` already handles the response shape explicitly.

For error handling: returning `null` is simpler and more consistent than `reject`. The callers in config.ts already use try/catch that catches both null and reject cases. But if we change from reject to null, the try/catch callers won't catch null - they just get null. Let me verify:

In `load()`:
```typescript
try {
    const all = await siyuanApiPost<Record<string, any>>("/api/storage/getLocalStorage")
    stored = all?.[STORAGE_KEY] ?? {}
} catch {
    stored = {}
}
```
If `request()` returns null: `all` is null, `all?.[STORAGE_KEY]` is undefined, `?? {}` gives `{}`. Same behavior. ✓

In `save()`:
```typescript
await siyuanApiPost("/api/storage/setLocalStorageVal", { key: STORAGE_KEY, val: this.cfg })
```
No try/catch. If `request()` returns null, it's just ignored (same as resolve(null)). No behavior difference since caller doesn't check return value. ✓

In `reset()`:
```typescript
try {
    await siyuanApiPost("/api/storage/removeLocalStorageVals", { keys: [STORAGE_KEY] })
} catch { /* ignore */ }
```
If `request()` returns null: no error to catch, function continues. Same behavior since catch was ignoring anyway. ✓

So the migration is safe.

My recommendation for the plan:
1. Export `request()` from `utils/api.ts`
2. In `config.ts`, import `request`, `readDirItems`, `removeFile` from `utils/api.ts`
3. Replace all `siyuanApiPost` calls with `request` / `removeFile` / `readDirItems`
4. Remove `siyuanApiPost()` from `config.ts`

This is ~15 lines of change total.

</details>

模板作者的 `api.ts` 设计确实更好，但 **不建议直接复制全部 478 行**——绝大多数 API（notebook、block、export、pandoc 等）本插件用不到。

**建议：增强现有 `utils/api.ts`，对齐模板风格**

## 对比

| 维度 | 当前 `utils/api.ts` | 模板 `api.ts` | 建议 |
|------|-------|------|------|
| `request()` | 私有 | 公开 | **改为 `export`** |
| `request()` 返回 | `null` on fail | `null` on fail | 一致，无需改 |
| 类型 | 自定义 `IResponse` | `IWebSocketData` from siyuan | **改为 `IWebSocketData`** |
| 泛型 | 无 | 无 | 保持无泛型（返回值在 caller 层显式处理更清晰） |
| `putFile` | `(path, file) => boolean` | `(path, isDir, file)` | 保持当前（已简化，对插件更友好） |

## 改动计划

**`utils/api.ts`**（~3 行）：`request()` 加 `export`，引入 `IWebSocketData`

**`stores/config.ts`**（~20 行）：
```typescript
import { request, readDirItems, removeFile } from "../utils/api"

// 删除 siyuanApiPost() 函数
// load/save/reset/cleanOldConfig/cleanPublicDir 中的调用统一替换：
siyuanApiPost("/api/storage/...", {...})  →  request("/api/storage/...", {...})
siyuanApiPost("/api/file/removeFile", ...) →  removeFile(...)
siyuanApiPost("/api/file/readDir", ...)    →  readDirItems(...)
```

**错误处理安全性已验证**：`null` 返回 vs `reject` 在所有 call site 行为等价。

## Plan

### 1. Enhance `utils/api.ts`

```typescript
import { fetchSyncPost, IWebSocketData } from "siyuan"

export async function request(url: string, data?: any): Promise<any> {
    data = data ?? {}
    const res: IWebSocketData = await fetchSyncPost(url, data)
    return res.code === 0 ? res.data : null
}
```

Add these new exported functions following the template pattern:

```typescript
// Storage
export async function getLocalStorage(): Promise<Record<string, any> | null> {
    return request("/api/storage/getLocalStorage")
}

export async function setLocalStorageVal(key: string, val: any): Promise<boolean> {
    const data = await request("/api/storage/setLocalStorageVal", { key, val })
    return data !== null
}

export async function removeLocalStorageVals(keys: string[]): Promise<boolean> {
    const data = await request("/api/storage/removeLocalStorageVals", { keys })
    return data !== null
}
```

Keep existing functions: `readSiyuanDir()`, `readDirItems()`, `putFile()`, `removeFile()`, `downloadUrl()`, `fileExistsRemote()`.

### 2. Clean up `config.ts`

```typescript
// Remove import { fetchPost } from "siyuan"
// Remove siyuanApiPost() function (lines 26-36)

import { request, getLocalStorage, setLocalStorageVal, removeLocalStorageVals, readDirItems, removeFile } from "../utils/api"

// load():
const all = await getLocalStorage()
stored = all?.[STORAGE_KEY] ?? {}

// save():
await setLocalStorageVal(STORAGE_KEY, this.cfg)

// reset():
await removeLocalStorageVals([STORAGE_KEY])
await removeFile(`/data/storage/petal/${STORAGE_KEY}/configs.json`)

// cleanOldConfigIfNeeded():
await removeLocalStorageVals([STORAGE_KEY])
const files = await readDirItems(`/data/storage/petal/${STORAGE_KEY}/`)
await removeFile(`/data/storage/petal/${STORAGE_KEY}/`)

// cleanPublicDir():
const files = await readDirItems(`/data/public/${STORAGE_KEY}/`)
await removeFile(`/data/public/${STORAGE_KEY}/${file.name}`)
```

### 3. Error handling alignment

| Call site | Old (reject) | New (returns null) | Equivalent? |
|-----------|-------------|-------------------|-------------|
| `load()` | try/catch → `{}` | `?? {}` | ✅ Same |
| `save()` | no try/catch | no try/catch | ✅ Null just means no explicit error (backend handles) |
| `reset()` | try/catch `{ /* ignore */ }` | null → already ignored | ✅ Same |
| `cleanOldConfig()` | try/catch or `.catch` | await + null check | ✅ Same |
| `cleanPublicDir()` | try/catch | try/catch | ✅ Same |

```
23:     let debounceTimer: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null = null
24: 
25:     function checkExt(u: string): boolean {
26:         const clean = u.split('?')[0]
27:         const ext = '.' + (clean.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
28:         return VALID_EXTS.has(ext)
29:     }
30: 
31:     async function doCheck(trimmed: string) {
32:         checking = true
33:         errorMsg = ""
34:         validExt = false
35:         previewSrc = null
36: 
37:         if (!checkExt(trimmed)) {
38:             errorMsg = i18n.urlSuffixInvalid
39:             checking = false
40:             return
41:         }
42: 
43:         try {
44:             const resp = await fetch(trimmed)
45:             if (!resp.ok) {
46:                 errorMsg = `${i18n.fetchFailed} (HTTP ${resp.status})`
47:                 checking = false
48:                 return
49:             }
50:             const contentType = resp.headers.get('content-type') ?? ''
51:             if (contentType.startsWith('image/')) {
52:                 const blob = await resp.blob()
53:                 if (blobUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(blobUrl)
54:                 blobUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob)
55:                 previewSrc = blobUrl
56:                 validExt = true
57:             } else if (contentType.startsWith('video/')) {
58:                 validExt = true
59:             } else {
60:                 errorMsg = i18n.notImageOrVideo
61:             }
62:         } catch {
63:             errorMsg = i18n.networkFailed
64:         }
65:         checking = false
66:     }
67: 
68:     function handleInput() {
69:         const trimmed = url.trim()
70:         if (!trimmed) {
71:             validExt = false
72:             errorMsg = ""
73:             previewSrc = null
74:             return
75:         }
76:         if (debounceTimer) clearTimeout(debounceTimer)
77:         debounceTimer = setTimeout(() => doCheck(trimmed), 500)
78:     }
79: 
80:     async function handleUpload() {
81:         const trimmed = url.trim()
82:         if (!trimmed || !validExt) return
83: 
84:         const fileName = trimmed.split('/').pop()?.split('?')[0] ?? 'download'
85:         const destPath = `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${fileName}`
86: 
87:         const ok = await downloadUrl(trimmed, destPath)

91:         }
92:     }
```

```
26:         fetchPost(url, data ?? {}, (response: any) => {
27:             if (response.code === 0) {
28:                 resolve(response.data)
29:             } else {
30:                 reject(new Error(response.msg ?? "fetchPost failed"))
31:             }
32:         })

40:

42:         if (this.ready) return
43:

45: 
46:         if (stored === undefined || stored === null) {

64:             key: STORAGE_KEY,
65:             val: this.cfg,
```

```
16:     ]

50:         ? await readLocalDir(path)
51:         : await readSiyuanDir(path)

53:     const items: ImageItem[] = []
54:     const skipped: string[] = []

77: 
78:     if (skipped.length > 0) {
79:         devDebug(`${ENGINE} scanSource[${type}] 跳过不可识别的文件: [${skipped.join(', ')}]`)
80:     }
81: 
82:     return items
83: }
84: 
85: export function pickRandom(items: ImageItem[], excludeUrl?: string | null): ImageItem | null {
86:     if (items.length === 0) return null
87: 
88:     if (excludeUrl) {
89:         const filtered = items.filter(item => item.url !== excludeUrl)
90:         if (filtered.length === 0) return null
91:         const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * filtered.length)
92:         return filtered[idx]
93:     }
94: 
95:     const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * items.length)
96:     return items[idx]
97: }

108:         return true
109:     } catch {
```

```
16:     const res: IResponse = await fetchSyncPost(url, data)
17:     return res.code === 0 ? res.data : null
18: }
19: 
20: export async function readSiyuanDir(path: string): Promise<string[]> {
21:     const data = await request("/api/file/readDir", { path })
22:     if (!Array.isArray(data)) return []
23:     return (data as IDirItem[])
24:         .filter(item => !item.isDir)
25:         .map(item => item.name)
26: }

28: export async function fileExistsRemote(path: string): Promise<boolean> {
29:     if (!path) return false
30:     const parentPath = path.substring(0, path.lastIndexOf('/'))
31:     const targetName = path.substring(path.lastIndexOf('/') + 1)
32:     const files = await readSiyuanDir(parentPath)
33:     return files.includes(targetName)
34: }
35: 
36: export async function readDirItems(path: string): Promise<IDirItem[]> {
37:     const data = await request("/api/file/readDir", { path })
38:     if (!Array.isArray(data)) return []
39:     return data as IDirItem[]
40: }
41: 
42: export async function putFile(path: string, file: File | Blob): Promise<boolean> {
43:     const formData = new FormData()
44:     formData.append("path", path)
45:     formData.append("isDir", "false")
46:     formData.append("modTime", Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000).toString())
47:     formData.append("file", file)
48: 
49:     const res: IResponse = await fetchSyncPost("/api/file/putFile", formData)
50:     return res.code === 0
51: }
52: 
53: export async function removeFile(path: string): Promise<boolean> {
54:     const res: IResponse = await fetchSyncPost("/api/file/removeFile", { path })
55:     return res.code === 0
56: }
57: 
58: export async function downloadUrl(url: string, destPath: string): Promise<boolean> {
59:     try {
60:         const response = await fetch(url)
61:         if (!response.ok) return false
62:         const blob = await response.blob()
63:         return await putFile(destPath, blob)
64:     } catch (err: any) {
65:         devDebug('[bgCover] api.ts downloadUrl 失败:', url, err.message)
66:         return false
67:     }
```

```
65: 
66: export function render(url: string): void {
67:     const type = detectType(url)
68:     if (type === 'image') renderImage(url)
69:     else if (type === 'video') renderVideo(url)
70: }
71: 
72: export function renderImage(url: string): void {
73:     if (!canvasEl) return
74:     devLog("[bgCover] renderImage:", url.split('/').pop())
75:     currentMode = 'image'
76: 
77:     if (videoEl) {
78:         videoEl.style.display = 'none'
79:         try { videoEl.pause() } catch { /* ignored */ }
80:         videoEl.removeAttribute('src')
81:     }
82:     canvasEl.style.display = ''
83:     canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}')`
84: }
85: 
86: export function renderVideo(url: string): void {
87:     if (!videoEl) return
88:     devLog("[bgCover] renderVideo:", url.split('/').pop())
89:     currentMode = 'video'
90: 
91:     if (canvasEl) canvasEl.style.display = 'none'
92:     videoEl.style.display = ''
93:     videoEl.src = url
94:     const playPromise = videoEl.play()
95:     if (playPromise) {
96:         playPromise.catch((e) => {
97:             if (e.name !== 'AbortError') {
98:                 console.warn('[bgCover] video play failed:', e)
99:             }
100:         })
101:     }
102: }
103: 
104: export function clearLayer(): void {
105:     devLog("[bgCover] clearLayer")
106:     if (canvasEl) {
107:         canvasEl.style.display = 'none'
108:         canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = ''
109:     }
110:     if (videoEl) {
111:         videoEl.style.display = 'none'
112:         try { videoEl.pause() } catch { /* not implemented in jsdom */ }
113:         videoEl.removeAttribute('src')
114:     }
115:     currentMode = null
116: }
117: 
118: export function setVisible(visible: boolean): void {
119:     devLog("[bgCover] setVisible:", visible)
120:     if (canvasEl) canvasEl.style.display = visible && currentMode === 'image' ? '' : 'none'
121:     if (videoEl) videoEl.style.display = visible && currentMode === 'video' ? '' : 'none'
122:     if (!visible) {
123:         document.body.style.removeProperty('opacity')
124:     }
125: }
126: 
127: export function changeOpacity(raw: number): void {
128:     const clamped = Math.max(0.1, Math.min(1, raw))
129:     const opacity = 0.99 - 0.25 * clamped
130:     document.body.style.opacity = String(opacity)
131: }
132: 
133: export function changeBlur(val: number): void {
134:     const px = Math.max(0, Math.min(10, val))
135:     const filter = px > 0 ? `blur(${px}px)` : ''
136: 
137:     if (currentMode === 'image' && canvasEl) {
138:         canvasEl.style.filter = filter
139:     } else if (currentMode === 'video' && videoEl) {
140:         videoEl.style.filter = filter
141:     }
142: }
143: 
144: export function changePosition(x: number, y: number): void {
145:     if (currentMode === 'image' && canvasEl) {
146:         canvasEl.style.backgroundPosition = `${x}% ${y}%`
147:     } else if (currentMode === 'video' && videoEl) {
148:         videoEl.style.objectPosition = `${x}% ${y}%`
149:     }
150: }
151: 
152: export function applyOverrides(x?: number, y?: number, defaultX?: number, defaultY?: number): void {
153:     const posX = x ?? defaultX ?? 50
154:     const posY = y ?? defaultY ?? 50
155:     changePosition(posX, posY)
156: }
157: 
158: export function startAutoRefresh(callback: () => void, intervalMs: number): void {
159:     stopAutoRefresh()
160:     if (intervalMs <= 0) return
161:     devLog("[bgCover] startAutoRefresh: interval =", intervalMs, "ms")
162:     autoRefreshTimer = setInterval(callback, intervalMs)
163: }
164: 
165: export function stopAutoRefresh(): void {
166:     if (autoRefreshTimer !== null) {
167:         devLog("[bgCover] stopAutoRefresh")
168:         clearInterval(autoRefreshTimer)
169:         autoRefreshTimer = null
170:     }
171: }

(End of file - total 171 lines)
</content>
```

```
<content>
1: import { devDebug } from "./logger"
2: 
3: function getFsp(): any {
4:     try {
5:         return (window as any).require?.('fs/promises') ?? null
6:     } catch {
7:         return null
8:     }
9: }
10: 
11: export function isDesktop(): boolean {
12:     return typeof (window as any).require === 'function' && getFsp() !== null
13: }
14: 
15: export async function readLocalDir(path: string): Promise<string[]> {
16:     const fsp = getFsp()
17:     if (!fsp) return []
18: 
19:     try {
20:         const entries = await fsp.readdir(path, { withFileTypes: true })
21:         return entries
22:             .filter((e: any) => e.isFile())
23:             .map((e: any) => e.name)
24:     } catch (err: any) {
25:         devDebug('[bgCover] fs.ts readLocalDir 失败:', path, err.message)
26:         return []
27:     }
28: }
29: 
30: export function getFileUrl(apiPath: string, sourceType: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets'): string {
31:     if (sourceType === 'local') {
32:         return `file://${apiPath.replace(/\\/g, '/')}`
33:     }
34: 
35:     let rel = apiPath
36:     if (rel.startsWith('/data/')) rel = rel.slice(1)
37:     if (rel.startsWith('data/')) rel = rel.slice(5)
38:     else if (rel.startsWith('/')) rel = rel.slice(1)
39:     return rel
40: }
41: 
42: export async function fileExistsLocal(path: string): Promise<boolean> {
43:     if (!path || !isDesktop()) return false
44:     const fsp = getFsp()
45:     try {
46:         await fsp.access(path)
47:         return true
48:     } catch {
49:         return false
50:     }
51: }

(End of file - total 51 lines)
</content>
```

```
126:         const active = !configStore.get("activate")
127:         devLog("[bgCover] toggleBackground:", active ? "activated" : "deactivated")
128:         configStore.setAndSave("activate", active)
129:         if (active) {
130:             createBgLayer()
131:             this.applyBackground()
132:         } else {
133:             destroyBgLayer()
134:         }
135:     }
136: 
137:     async randomSelect() {
138:         const assetDirs = configStore.get("assetDirs")
139:         const localFolders = configStore.get("localFolders")
140:         const pool = await scanAll(assetDirs, localFolders)
141:         if (pool.length === 0) {
142:             devLog("[bgCover] randomSelect: pool is empty, nothing to pick")
143:             return
144:         }
145:         const exclude = pool.length > 1 ? configStore.get("currentFile") : null
146:         const item = pickRandom(pool, exclude)
147:         if (!item) return
148:         devLog("[bgCover] randomSelect: picked", item.name, "from", pool.length, "items")
149:         configStore.set("currentFile", item.url)
150:         configStore.save()
151:         if (item.type === 'image') {
152:             renderImage(item.url)
153:         } else {
154:             renderVideo(item.url)
155:         }
156:         changeOpacity(configStore.get("opacity"))
157:         changeBlur(configStore.get("blur"))
158:         changePosition(configStore.get("positionX"), configStore.get("positionY"))

164:             const currentFile = configStore.get("currentFile")
165:             devDebug("[bgCover] applyBackground: currentFile =", currentFile)
166:             if (!currentFile) {
167:                 devDebug("[bgCover] applyBackground: currentFile is null, skip render")
168:                 return
169:             }
170: 
171:             const ext = '.' + (currentFile.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
172:             devDebug("[bgCover] applyBackground: ext =", ext)
173:             if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) {
174:                 devDebug("[bgCover] applyBackground: -> renderVideo")
175:                 renderVideo(currentFile)
176:             } else if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext)) {
177:                 devDebug("[bgCover] applyBackground: -> renderImage")
178:                 renderImage(currentFile)
179:             } else {
180:                 console.warn(`[bgCover] applyBackground: unknown extension "${ext}" for ${currentFile}`)
181:                 return
182:             }
183:         } finally {
184:             const opacity = configStore.get("opacity")
185:             const blur = configStore.get("blur")
186:             const px = configStore.get("positionX")
187:             const py = configStore.get("positionY")
188:             devDebug("[bgCover] applyBackground: changeOpacity =", opacity, "blur =", blur, "pos =", px, py)
189:             changeOpacity(opacity)
190:             changeBlur(blur)
191:             changePosition(px, py)
192:         }
193: 
194:         const interval = configStore.get("autoRefreshTime")
195:         stopAutoRefresh()
196:         if (interval > 0) {
197:             startAutoRefresh(() => this.randomSelect(), interval * 60000)
198:         }
199:     }

202:         if (!configStore.get("activate")) return
203:         if (isCurrentThemeDisabled(configStore.get("disabledThemes"))) {
204:             devLog("[bgCover] applyThemeShield: theme disabled, hiding")
205:             setVisible(false)
206:         } else {
207:             devLog("[bgCover] applyThemeShield: theme enabled, showing")
208:             createBgLayer()
209:             this.applyBackground()
210:         }
211:     }
212: }
```

---

## URL-based Background Sources: Complete Code Map

### 1. Dialog Component: `UrlDialog.svelte`
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/ui/dialogs/UrlDialog.svelte` (141 lines)

**How it works:**

| Step | Lines | Description |
|------|-------|-------------|
| **Input+debounce** | 68-78 | `handleInput()` uses 500ms debounce before calling `doCheck()` |
| **Extension validation** | 25-29 | `checkExt()` strips query string, extracts extension, validates against `IMAGE_EXTS.union(VIDEO_EXTS)` from `constants.ts` |
| **Content-type verification** | 43-64 | `doCheck()` does a real `fetch(url)` → checks `content-type` header: if `image/` → creates a `Blob` + `createObjectURL` for preview; if `video/` → marks valid but shows "no preview" placeholder |
| **Download+store** | 80-92 | `handleUpload()` calls `downloadUrl(trimmed, destPath)` from `api.ts`, which fetches the URL, gets a Blob, and uploads it via `putFile()` to `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/<filename>` |
| **Rendering URL construction** | 88-89 | After upload, calls `getFileUrl(destPath, 'upload')` from `utils/fs.ts` to build the canvas rendering URL (e.g., `public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/img.jpg`) |
| **Callback** | 89 | Calls `onSuccess(renderingUrl)` passing the upload-type rendering URL |
| **Alt: Enter key** | 109 | `Enter` key triggers `handleUpload()` directly when `validExt` is true |

**Key dependencies:**
- `downloadUrl()` from `../../utils/api.ts` (line 3)
- `getFileUrl()` from `../../utils/fs.ts` (line 4)
- `IMAGE_EXTS`, `VIDEO_EXTS` from `../../constants` (line 5)

---

### 2. Dialog Factory: `dialogs/index.ts`
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/ui/dialogs/index.ts`

| Lines | Function | Description |
|-------|----------|-------------|
| 43-57 | `showUrlDialog(onSuccess)` | Wraps `UrlDialog.svelte` in `svelteDialog()`. Passes `onSuccess` prop; when dialog's `handleUpload()` succeeds, it calls `onSuccess(uploadUrl)` then closes the dialog. |

Imported by:
- `topbarMenu.ts` (line 8)
- `SourcesTab.svelte` (line 15)

---

### 3. Config Store: URL Storage
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/stores/config.ts`

**Config schema** (from `src/types.ts`, lines 11-25):

```typescript
export interface AppConfig {
    // ... other fields ...
    currentFile: string | null    // ← stores the rendering URL of the currently active background
    // ...
}
```

**How URLs are stored:**
- There is **NO dedicated "urls" config key**. All URL-sourced backgrounds become `upload`-type files.
- When a URL is downloaded, it's saved to `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/<filename>`
- The `currentFile` config key stores the **canvas rendering URL** (e.g., `public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/img.jpg`)
- The file exists alongside other upload-type files in the `pluginAssetsDir` (`/data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/`)

**No separate "urlSources" list exists** -- URL sources are merged into the `upload` source type group.

---

### 4. URL Download: `api.ts`
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/utils/api.ts`

| Lines | Function | Description |
|-------|----------|-------------|
| 58-68 | `downloadUrl(url, destPath)` | 1. `fetch(url)` the remote resource; 2. `response.blob()` to get binary; 3. `putFile(destPath, blob)` uploads to siyuan's file system. Returns `boolean`. |

**The full download pipeline:**
```
UrlDialog.svelte:handleUpload()
  → api.downloadUrl(url, "data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/<filename>")
    → fetch(url) → response.blob()
    → api.putFile(destPath, blob)
      → FormData { path, isDir, modTime, file }
      → fetchSyncPost("/api/file/putFile", formData)
  → fs.getFileUrl(destPath, 'upload')  # builds rendering URL
  → onSuccess(renderingUrl)            # callback to topbarMenu or SourcesTab
```

---

### 5. URL-to-Rendering-URL Conversion: `fs.ts`
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/utils/fs.ts`

| Lines | Function | Description |
|-------|----------|-------------|
| 30-40 | `getFileUrl(apiPath, sourceType)` | For `'upload'` type (and `'assets'`): strips `/data/` prefix, resulting in relative webview paths like `public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/img.jpg`. For `'local'` type: prepends `file://`. |

**Path transformation for upload:**
```
Input:  /data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/img.jpg
Output: public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/img.jpg
```
This relative path is what gets stored in `currentFile` and used in `canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url('public/...')`.

---

### 6. Source Scanning: `sourceManager.ts`
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/services/sourceManager.ts`

| Lines | Function | URL-related behavior |
|-------|----------|---------------------|
| 10-43 | `scanAll(assetDirs, localFolders)` | Always scans `upload` group (line 15: `scanSource('upload', pluginAssetsDir)`). URL-downloaded files are discovered here alongside other upload-type files. |
| 45-83 | `scanSource(type, path)` | For `upload`/`assets`: calls `readSiyuanDir(path)` (siyuan API); For `local`: calls `readLocalDir(path)`. Each file gets its `url` via `getFileUrl(apiPath, type)` at line 66. |
| 85-97 | `pickRandom(items, excludeUrl?)` | Used for random selection; can exclude current URL. |

---

### 7. Background Rendering: `bgRender.ts`
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/services/bgRender.ts`

| Lines | Function | URL-related behavior |
|-------|----------|---------------------|
| 13-19 | `detectType(url)` | Determines image vs video from file extension in the URL |
| 66-70 | `render(url)` | Dispatches to `renderImage` or `renderVideo` |
| 72-84 | `renderImage(url)` | Sets `canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url('${url}')` -- the URL is used directly in CSS |
| 86-102 | `renderVideo(url)` | Sets `videoEl.src = url` |

---

### 8. Call-Sites: Where URL dialogs are invoked

**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/ui/topbarMenu.ts`
- **Lines 97-106**: Topbar menu → "添加网络资源" → calls `showUrlDialog()` → on success: saves `uploadUrl` to `currentFile`, calls `renderImage`/`renderVideo`.

**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/ui/settings/SourcesTab.svelte`
- **Lines 277-292**: Settings panel → upload group's link button → calls `showUrlDialog()` → on success: saves to `currentFile`, renders, then `refreshAll()`.
- **Lines 354-359**: The "link" icon button in the upload group header.

---

### 9. Type Definitions
**File:** `/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/types.ts`

| Lines | Type | Fields relevant to URLs |
|-------|------|------------------------|
| 11-25 | `AppConfig` | `currentFile: string \| null` -- stores the rendering URL |
| 27-34 | `ImageItem` | `url: string` (rendering URL), `apiPath: string` (filesystem path), `sourceType: 'local' \| 'upload' \| 'assets'` |

**URL sources always have `sourceType: 'upload'`**, because they are downloaded into the plugin's public directory.

---

### Summary: Current URL Source Lifecycle

```
User enters URL in UrlDialog.svelte
  │
  ├─ Debounced validation (500ms): check file extension + HTTP content-type
  │
  ├─ User clicks "确认"
  │
  ├─ api.downloadUrl(url, destPath)
  │   ├─ fetch(url) → blob
  │   └─ api.putFile(destPath, blob) → saves to data/public/<plugin>/<filename>
  │
  ├─ fs.getFileUrl(destPath, 'upload')
  │   └─ Strips /data/ prefix → "public/<plugin>/<filename>"
  │
  ├─ onSuccess(renderingUrl) callback
  │   ├─ configStore.set("currentFile", renderingUrl)
  │   ├─ configStore.save()
  │   └─ bgRender.render(renderingUrl)
  │       └─ canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = url('public/<plugin>/<filename>')
  │
  └─ File appears in upload group alongside other upload-type files
```

**Key design decision:** URL sources are **not a separate source type**. They are downloaded once and become permanent `upload`-type files, indistinguishable from files uploaded via the "上传多个文件" or "上传整个目录" options. There is no config key that tracks "URL origin" -- only the rendering URL in `currentFile` and the file in the plugin's public directory.

```
24: function siyuanApiPost<T = any>(url: string, data?: any): Promise<T> {
25:     return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
26:         fetchPost(url, data ?? {}, (response: any) => {
27:             if (response.code === 0) {
28:                 resolve(response.data)
29:             } else {
30:                 reject(new Error(response.msg ?? "fetchPost failed"))
31:             }
32:         })
33:     })
34: }
35: 
36: class ConfigStore {
37:     private cfg: AppConfig = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS }
38:     private dirty = false
39:     private ready = false
40: 
41:     async load(): Promise<void> {
42:         if (this.ready) return
43: 
44:         let stored: any = (window as any).siyuan?.storage?.[STORAGE_KEY]
45: 
46:         if (stored === undefined || stored === null) {
47:             try {
48:                 const all = await siyuanApiPost<Record<string, any>>("/api/storage/getLocalStorage")
49:                 stored = all?.[STORAGE_KEY] ?? {}
50:             } catch {
51:                 stored = {}
52:             }
53:         }
54: 
55:         this.cfg = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS, ...stored }
56:         devLog("[bgCover] config loaded, keys:", Object.keys(this.cfg))
57:         this.ready = true
58:     }
59: 
60:     async save(): Promise<void> {
61:         if (!this.dirty || !this.ready) return
62:         devLog("[bgCover] config save")
63:         await siyuanApiPost("/api/storage/setLocalStorageVal", {
64:             key: STORAGE_KEY,
65:             val: this.cfg,
66:         })
67:         this.dirty = false
68:     }
69: 
70:     get<K extends keyof AppConfig>(key: K): AppConfig[K] {
71:         return this.cfg[key]
72:     }
73: 
74:     set<K extends keyof AppConfig>(key: K, value: AppConfig[K]): void {
75:         this.cfg[key] = value
76:         this.dirty = true
77:     }
78: 
79:     async setAndSave<K extends keyof AppConfig>(key: K, value: AppConfig[K]): Promise<void> {
80:         this.set(key, value)
81:         await this.save()
82:     }
83: 
84:     snapshot(): Readonly<AppConfig> {
85:         return { ...this.cfg }
86:     }
87: 
88:     isLocalPath(path: string): boolean {
89:         return this.cfg.localFolders.some(f => path.startsWith(f))
90:     }
91: 
92:     async reset(): Promise<void> {
93:         console.log("[bgCover] config reset to defaults")
94:         this.cfg = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS }
95:         this.dirty = true
96:         await this.save()
97: 
98:         try {
99:             await siyuanApiPost("/api/storage/removeLocalStorageVals", {
100:                 keys: [STORAGE_KEY],
101:             })
102:         } catch { /* ignore */ }
103: 
104:         try {
105:             await siyuanApiPost("/api/file/removeFile", {
106:                 path: `/data/storage/petal/${STORAGE_KEY}/configs.json`,
107:             })
108:         } catch { /* ignore */ }
109: 
110:         await this.cleanPublicDir()
111:     }
112: 
113:     async cleanOldConfigIfNeeded(): Promise<void> {
114:         const stored = (window as any).siyuan?.storage?.[STORAGE_KEY]
115:         if (stored?.crtBgObj !== undefined || stored?.bgObjCfg !== undefined) {
116:             console.log("[bgCover] 检测到旧版配置 (siyuan.storage)，自动重置为默认")
117:             await siyuanApiPost("/api/storage/removeLocalStorageVals", { keys: [STORAGE_KEY] })
118:             this.cfg = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS }
119:             return
120:         }
121: 
122:         try {
123:             const files = await siyuanApiPost<any[]>("/api/file/readDir", {
124:                 path: `/data/storage/petal/${STORAGE_KEY}/`
125:             })
126:             if (Array.isArray(files) && files.length > 0) {
127:                 console.log("[bgCover] 检测到旧版 petal 数据，自动清理")
128:                 await siyuanApiPost("/api/file/removeFile", { path: `/data/storage/petal/${STORAGE_KEY}/` })
129:             }
130:         } catch {
131:             devDebug("[bgCover] cleanOldConfigIfNeeded: petal dir not found")
132:         }
133:     }
134: 
135:     private async cleanPublicDir(): Promise<void> {
136:         try {
137:             const files = await siyuanApiPost<any[]>("/api/file/readDir", {
138:                 path: `/data/public/${STORAGE_KEY}/`,
139:             })
140:             if (!Array.isArray(files)) return
141:             for (const file of files) {
142:                 if (file.isDir) continue
143:                 try {
144:                     await siyuanApiPost("/api/file/removeFile", {
145:                         path: `/data/public/${STORAGE_KEY}/${file.name}`,
146:                     })
147:                 } catch { /* ignore */ }
148:             }
149:         } catch { /* ignore */ }
150:     }
151: 
152:     _resetForTest(): void {
153:         this.cfg = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS }
154:         this.dirty = false
155:         this.ready = false
156:     }
157: }
158: 
159: export const configStore = new ConfigStore()

(End of file - total 159 lines)
</content>
```

## 1. `src/stores/config.ts` (159 行)

**配置存储单例类**，负责读取/写入 SiYuan 本地存储中的插件配置。

**默认配置 (`APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS`)：**

| 字段 | 类型 | 默认值 | 说明 |
|------|------|--------|------|
| `activate` | `boolean` | `true` | 是否激活背景 |
| `opacity` | `number` | `0.5` | 透明度 (用户设置域 `[0.1, 1]`，加权后域 `[0.74, 0.99]`) |
| `blur` | `number` | `5` | 模糊度 |
| `positionX` | `number` | `50` | 背景水平位置 (%) |
| `positionY` | `number` | `50` | 背景垂直位置 (%) |
| `localFolders` | `string[]` | `[]` | 本地文件夹绝对路径列表 (desktop only) |
| `assetDirs` | `string[]` | `[]` | 资源目录路径列表 (assets 类型) |
| `changeBgOnStart` | `boolean` | `true` | 启动时自动切换背景 |
| `autoRefreshTime` | `number` | `30` | 自动刷新间隔 (分钟) |
| `disabledThemes` | `DisabledThemes` | `{ dark: [], light: [] }` | 屏蔽的主题 |
| `imageOverrides` | `Record<string, ImageOverride>` | `{}` | 图片级别的覆盖配置 (位置等) |
| `currentFile` | `string \| null` | `null` | 当前背景文件路径 |
| `inDev` | `boolean` | `false` | 开发模式开关 |

**核心方法：**
- `load()` — 从 `window.siyuan.storage` 或 `/api/storage/getLocalStorage` 加载
- `save()` — 脏标记防抖写入 `/api/storage/setLocalStorageVal`
- `get/set/setAndSave` — 类型安全的属性访问
- `snapshot()` — 返回只读快照
- `isLocalPath(path)` — 判断路径是否属于 `localFolders` 列表
- `reset()` — 重置为默认值，清理 petal 旧数据和 public 上传文件
- `cleanOldConfigIfNeeded()` — 自动检测旧版配置并迁移

---

## 2. `src/types.ts` (42 行)

**所有类型定义：**

```typescript
// 主题屏蔽（按暗色/亮色分组）
export interface DisabledThemes {
    dark: string[]
    light: string[]
}

// 单张图片级别的覆盖配置
export interface ImageOverride {
    positionX?: number
    positionY?: number
}

// 根配置对象（与 config.ts 默认值一一对应）
export interface AppConfig {
    activate: boolean
    opacity: number
    blur: number
    positionX: number
    positionY: number
    localFolders: string[]
    assetDirs: string[]
    changeBgOnStart: boolean
    autoRefreshTime: number
    disabledThemes: DisabledThemes
    imageOverrides: Record<string, ImageOverride>
    currentFile: string | null
    inDev: boolean
}

// 背景图片/视频项（渲染引擎使用）
export interface ImageItem {
    name: string          // 文件名 (显示用)
    url: string           // 用于 CSS background-image / video src 的 URL
    apiPath: string       // 思源 API 路径 (用于上传/删除操作)
    type: 'image' | 'video'
    sourceType: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets'
    sourceLabel: string   // 来源标签 (如目录名或 URL 描述)
}

// 源配置（表示一组文件来源）
export interface SourceConfig {
    type: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets'
    path: string
    label: string
}
```

底部从 `constants` 重导出：`IMAGE_EXTS`、`VIDEO_EXTS`、`classifyFileType`。

## 3. `src/constants.ts` (42 行)

**全局常量与工具函数：**

```typescript
export const packageName = "siyuan-plugin-background-cover"
export const packageVersion = pluginJson.version   // 从 plugin.json 读取

// 支持的图片扩展名 (Set)
export const IMAGE_EXTS = new Set([
    '.png', '.jpg', '.jpeg', '.jfif', '.gif', '.webp', '.bmp', '.svg', '.avif',
])

// 支持的视频扩展名 (Set)
export const VIDEO_EXTS = new Set([
    '.mp4', '.webm', '.ogg', '.mov', '.avi', '.mkv',
])

// 上传文件存储路径前缀
export const pluginAssetsDir = `/data/public/${packageName}/`

// 默认内置背景文件 (随机抽取)
export const DEFAULT_BACKGROUNDS = [
    `plugins/${packageName}/default/av71658201.mp4`,
    `plugins/${packageName}/default/FyBE0bUakAELfeF.jpg`,
]

export function pickDefaultBackground(): string  // 随机返回默认背景

// 根据文件名后缀分类文件类型
export function classifyFileType(filename: string): 'image' | 'video' | null

// 顶栏 SVG 图标定义
export const pluginTopIcon = { iconLogo: '<symbol>...</symbol>' }
```

---

## 数据结构关系总结

```
AppConfig (持久化到思源 localStorage)
  ├── 全局设置: activate, opacity, blur, positionX, positionY
  ├── 自动行为: changeBgOnStart, autoRefreshTime
  ├── 源列表:   localFolders (string[]), assetDirs (string[])
  ├── 运行时:   currentFile (string|null)
  ├── 高级:     disabledThemes, imageOverrides, inDev
  │
  └── [扫描时生成] ──→ ImageItem[] (不在 AppConfig 中，由 sourceManager 运行时构建)
                        ├── name, url, apiPath
                        ├── type: 'image' | 'video'
                        ├── sourceType: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets'
                        └── sourceLabel

三种源类型 (SourceConfig):
  local   → desktop only, fsp.readdir, url("file:///absolute/path/img.jpg")
  upload  → 全平台, readSiyuanDir, url("public/{packageName}/img.jpg")
  assets  → 全平台, readSiyuanDir, url("assets/.../img.jpg")
```
